Desquelz li une maniere si est que tu faices III cauteres, ou IIII, en lignant selonc la longor de la mice, selonc la figure dou cautere dou foie que nos avons dit devant;	 Of which the one manner is that you make three or four cauteries in a line according to the length of the abscess, according to the shape of the liver cautery that we have said before.
et n’apresser mie ta main a tout le cautere, et soit li malaides sovins sor son dos;	 And do not hurry your hand to all the cautery, let the patient remain conscious on his back.
et une autre maniere de cautere si est que tu eschaufe le cautere qui a II ners, si com nos l’avons mostreit en la dislocation de l’espaule;	 And another way of cauterizing is that you heat the cautery with two nerves, as we have shown in the dislocation of the shoulder.
et lieve le keur qui est endroit la mice, ou li coutes dou malaide vient devers senestre, et soit li elevations dont tu lieves le keur selonc la keur, selonc la longesce dou cors, et li cautere soient selonc la largesce dou cors.	 and lift the incision where the worm is, or the patient's wound comes towards the left side; and you shall raise the edges of the incision according to the incision, according to the length of the body, and the cauterizer should be according to the width of the body.
Aprés i boute les II ners enflamez tant que li keurs soit perciez de l’autre part, et puis trai fuers le cautere, et ensi en i avra IIII.	 Afterward insert the two inflamed nerves until the incision is pierced from the other side, and then pull out the cauterizer, and in this way there will be four.
Et se tu vues, si cauterize a tot le cautere a III ners.	 And if you see, cauterize with all the cautery at three veins.
Aprés le cure quant il a geteit porriture par lonc tens, et ce vaut mues que li autre des cures devant dites.	 After the treatment when pus has come out for a long time, it is necessary to use the other treatments mentioned before.
de ydropisie	And from the dropsy
Cautere ne vaut a ydropique, fors c’a la maniere qui est apelee «asclytes».	 Cautery does not work on dropsy, except in the manner called "asclytes".
Quant tu la cures selonc les manieres que nos avons dit en divisions, et ta cure ne profite mie, adonques covient il que tu li faices IIII cauteres entor la boude, et I sus l’estomac, et un sus le foie, et I sus la mice, et II derrier le dos sus l’espinee, et I endroit le pis;	 When the cure is carried out according to the ways we have said in the sections, and your treatment does not benefit, then it is necessary that you make four cauteries around the abscess, one on the stomach, one on the liver, one on the spleen, two behind the back near the spine, and one at the worst place.
et soit li cauteres bien pres de l’espés dou keur.	 And let the cautery be close to the thick part of the sore.
Aprés laisse le cautere aovert por giter porriture lonc tens, et ne lassier mie la cure dou malaide aprés le cautere;	 After opening the cautery to pour the purgative for a long time, do not leave the care of the patient after the cautery.
et sanation se hasterait, et seront ensamble les II ententions avec l’aide de Deu.	 And healing would hasten, and the two intentions would be united with God's help.
Li forme dou cautere por le ventre soit li clavile que nos avons devant mostreit;	 The shape of the cautery for the belly is the clavel that we have shown before;
et cil por le dos soit olivaire, selonc ceu qu’il est ci devant mis.	 and the one for the back should be olive-shaped, as previously described.
de l’enfleure des piez	the swelling of the feet
Quant li piez sont enflez a celui qui est ydropique, et sont plain d’awe citrine, il covient que tu cauterizes sus le dos dou piet entre l’auriculaire et l’anulaire;	 When the feet are swollen in a person who is dropsical and filled with water, you must cauterize on top of the foot between the auricular and anular bones.
et lieve ta main avec le cautere sens torner.	 hold your hand with the cautery without turning it.
Et n’entrer mie trop em parfont, ensi sarrait fuers li awe citrine, et soit li cauteres selonc cest forme:	 And do not enter too deeply, so as not to burn the yellow fluid excessively; and let the cautery be in this shape:
Aprés fai sus II jambes II cauteres en chescune jambe a la pointe dou cutellaire;	 After making two cauterizations on both legs, one at the tip of each shinbone (cautery instrument).
et soit li cauteres dou lonc, l’un desoz le genoil devant et l’autre defuers, enmi la jambe;	 And let the cauteries be long, one under the thigh and the other outside the leg.
et laisse les cauteres aovers longement sens curer, que li awe en isse;	 Leave the cauteries over a long period of time to heal, that is if it is necessary (to leave them there).
aprés le cure des autres cures que nos avons dit.	 After healing from the other treatments that we have said.
de la menoison	In the treatment of the dislocated shoulder:
Quant solution de ventre vient de froidor et de moistor, tant que li vertus retentive et digestive qui est ou stomac et en l’intestine est afleboie, et ne puet estre curez par manieres de cures;	 When abdominal distention comes from cold and moisture, as long as the restorative and digestive qualities that are in the stomach and intestines are weakened and cannot be cured by means of treatments.
et tu vois le malaide bien soffrant et de fort vertut, si fai I grant cautere sus l’estomac selonc ceu qu’il en a parleit ci devant ou cautere de l’estomac, au cautere circule;	 And if you see the patient suffering greatly and with strong vitality, make a large cauterization on the stomach as mentioned earlier or stomach cautery, around the stomach.
et IIII cauteres entor la boude subtilz a tout I cautere clavile subtil, et II cauteres sus les hainches.	 And three subtle cauteries around the buttock, every subtle cautery for nail, and two cauteries on the thighs.
Et se tu vois les moistors habundans et le malaide soffrant, se li fai cautere sus le poignil, et .i. cautere sus chaicun yle, et .ij. petis cauteres sus l’estomac delez le grant, car li cure est profitans quant il i a bone aide.	And if you see abundant moisture and the patient suffering, make a cautery on the shoulder, and one cautery on each joint, and two small cauterizations on the stomach beneath it, for the cure is beneficial when there is good aid.
de la cure des emorroydes	Of the treatment of hemorrhoids
Quant les emorroydes sont ou fondement, ou une ou plusors, et sont ancienes et sont de grosses humors froides et moistes corrumpues, et sont curees si com nos avons dit en divisions, et il ne profite mie, si fai cauteres:	 When piles are deep-seated, one or more, and are old and have thick cold and moist corrupted humors, and are treated as mentioned in the divisions, it does not help if you perform cauterization.
III sus l’espine dou dos, celi qui est tout defuers desoz almecdate poc et poc en triangulant, et I cautere desoz la boude II dois;	 Three on the spine of the back, which is completely displaced below the coccyx and protruding gradually in a triangle shape, and one cautery under the buttock.
et se tu penses que ses estomac soit refroidiez, et li viande ne cuise, et on voit enfler la faice, adonques li faice on I grant cautere sus le stomac, si com il est devant dit, et I autre sus le foie, et I autre sus la mice a tout le cautere clavile;	 And if you think that his stomach is cold and the meat does not cook, and one sees swelling in the face, then the face should receive a large cautery on the stomach as mentioned before, and another on the liver, and another on the spleen with all the subtle cautery.
et laisse le cautere overt lonc tens.	 Leave the cautery open for a long time.
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	 After healing the shoulder when it is healed.
de la charnositeit qui est nommee «thelul»	of the carnivorous disease called "thelul"
Quant tu copes althelul, si eschaufe le cautere qui semble I raseur, et puis le met tout embraseit sus cel althelul copeit;	 When you cut with a hot iron, if the cautery appears to be shaved, then put it all on fire over the place where you are cutting.
et i laisse tant ta main que li cauteres viegne a la naissance de la voine, de coi li sans cort;	 and keep your hand so that the cautery comes to the opening of the vein, in this way it will not tear.
fai ceu une fois ou II, et s’il i a mout d’althelul, si cauterize chaicun si com nos avons dit;	 Do this once or twice, and if there is much blood, then cauterize each one as we have said.
aprés les cure d’oignemens profitans tant qu’il soient sanez;	 After the cure of ointments is profitable until they are healed.
et se tu cauterizes d’un cautere grant sus alchatim, si avra plus grant aide.	 And if you cauterize with a large cautery over a burn, it will have more help.
de plaie mal curee	From badly healed wound
Quant li malaides ne puet soffrir tailleure ne overture, que nos raconterons en son leu, si vient teil maladie que ne puet estre sanee fuer que par cautere.	When the patient cannot bear incision or opening, we will speak about it in its place; this disease can only be cured by cautery.
Quant a aucun vient fistule, et est enveillie et giete porriture et moistors corrumpues, si la doies prover a tot une tente subtil, et garde que tu saiches a tot la tente combien elle a de parfont.	 If a fistula comes, and it is swollen and filled with pus and decayed matter, you should test the whole tent in every way, and be sure that you know the entire tent how much it heals.
Aprés eschaufe le cautere qui semble I raseur, et le boute en la fistule selonc la quantiteit que li tente i est entrée, et rencomence lou cautere tant que cil cors porris et corrumpus soient ars, une fois, ou II ou III, selonc la quantiteit de som besoing;	 After shaving the cautery that appears to be like a razor, put it in the fistula according to the amount that it entered there, and continue the cauterization until the flesh burns and is burned, once or twice or three times, according to the quantity of skin needed.
et te warde d’ardre lé nerf qui sunt enqui, et des grans voinnes.	 And take care of the nerves which are narrow, and of the great veins.
se li fistule vait au cors de la vesie et a l’intestine, si te warde de ces leus, et ne faire ceu fuers que en leu charnut, et pense qu’ele n’est mie persans;	 If the fistula goes to the body of the bladder or intestines, beware of these places, and do not make incisions except in charnu, and think that it is not permanent.
aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez, et se li leus est saielez, et les matieres sont ostees lonc tens, adonc saiches que li leus est sanez entierement;	 After curing the place until it is healed, if the places are festered and the matter has been removed for a long time, then know that the place is completely healed.
et se les matieres ne sont ostees, saiche que li leus est troez, et corrumpus li os au font;	 And if the matter has not been removed, know that the place is rotten and the bone is corrupted.
et ensi com un de ces que nos dirons en son leu.	 And thus in one of these cases.
de la maladie des reins	Of the disease of the kidneys
Quant dolor de froit vient as rains, et de grosse ventositeit, et ne prent talant de femme, adonc covient il que tu li fais cautere sus les rains d’une part et d’autre au cautere clavile que nos avons devant dit;	 When cold pain comes in the kidneys, and of great windiness, and does not take a woman's form, then you must give it fire cautery on both sides of the kidneys using the cautery iron that we have previously mentioned.
et se nos le cauterizons em mileu, si avra III cauteres en ligne, et se feront plus grant aide.	 And if we cauterize it in milk, there will be three cauteries in a row, and they will make more significant help.
de la vessie	Of the bladder
Quant li vessie est mole et foible de froit et de moistor, si que li malaides retient l’urine, adonc li fai cautere en la partie defuers sus la vessie, la ou encomencent li poil dou poignil, et I a destre et I a senestre, et soit chescuns cauteres si lons com li nous d’un poce;	 When the bladder is weak and cold or moist, so that the patient retains urine, then make a cautery in the area outside the bladder, where the hair of the testicle starts, both on the right and left side, and each cautery should be as long as the thumb.
et li fais I cautere defuers le dos, ou II se tu en as besoing;	 and make the cautery behind the back, where you have need of it;
et soit li cauteres clavile selon la forme devant dite.	 and let the cauteries be like a nail in shape, as was said before.
de la marris	of the marriage
Quant li marrix est froide et moiste, et ne laisse mie por ceu a concevoir, et les flors sont corrumpues et lor termines tarde;	 When the matrix is cold and moist, it does not allow conception, and the flowers are corrupted and their terms are delayed;
et quant elles vienent, si sent grant dolor:	 And when they come, there is great pain:
adonques covient il c’on li faice III cauteres entor la boude, si com nos avons dit ou cautere de la vessie, et II cauteres defuers le dos;	 Then you must apply three fire cauteries around the boil, as we have said the fire cautery of the bladder, and two fire cauteries outside the back.
et soit li cauteres clavile, si com nos avons dit.	 let the cautery be heated like a nail, as we have said.
de la hainche	of the itch
Quant les moistors viscouses dessendent a la boiste de la hainche, et por ceste cause si se muet de son leu, et li signes est que li cuisse est plus longe que li autre quant on le mesure ensamble;	 When the viscous humors descend to the bone of the thigh, and for this reason it moves from its place, the signs are that the thigh is longer than the other when measured together.
et est trovez li leus dou departement vuis, si covient que tu cauterizes le malaide sus la boiste de la hainche a I cautere semblant au cercle, et seigne devant le leu entor la boiste si com elle torne, si que li boiste soit dedens le cercle;	 and the joints are found to depart from their place in the thigh region, then you must cauterize the patient over the bone of the thigh with a cautery similar to a circle, and the sign should be before the joint around the bone as it turns, so that the bone is within the circle;
et si soit li cauteres telz com cil dont on a cauterizeit le stomac.	 And if [the cautery] is similar to those with which one cauterizes the stomach.
Et se cist cauteres ne t’est presens, se li fai III cauteres de l’olivaire grans, et soit li cauteres ausi parfont com tous li keurs;	 And if this cautery is not present, make three large olive-oil cauteries, and make the cautery as deep as all other wounds.
et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	 heal it until it becomes healthy.
de la dolor de la hainche	of the pain from the hernia
Quant dolor vient en la boiste de la hainche, et c’est de froidor et de moistor, et li malaides est curez de ceu que nos avons dit en la division et li cure ne vaut, et li maladie est anciene:	 When pain comes in the box of the back, it is from coldness and moisture, and the patient is treated with what we have said in the division, but the treatment does not help, and the disease is old.
adonc covient il que tu purges le malaide des grosses humors de pilules fetides, ou autres pilules bones semblans.	 Therefore, you must purge the patient of the large humors with foul pills or other good-seeming pills.
Aprés li fai cautere;	 After [doing] that, perform a cautery;
et li maniere dou cautere si est selonc II manieres:	 And the method of the cautery is according to two ways:
c’est a savoir ensamble medicines ardans, et cautere de feu.	 This means "namely, together with burning medicines and fire cauterization.
Cautere de feu si est selonc mout de manieres, desquelz li uns est telz:	 Fire cautery is according to many ways, among which one is as follows:
que tu cauterize sus la boiste de la hainche III cauteres triangulalz selonc ceste forme, et i fai bone profunditeit et grant, et ait entre chaicun cautere d’espaice la groissece d’un doi, et soit li cauteres olivaire;	 you cauterize on the boil of the haunch with three triangular cauteries according to this shape, and make a good depth and width, and have space between each cautery of the size of a thumb, and let the cauteries be olive-shaped.
aucune fois fait on cautere en mileu sus lou chief de la hainche, por coi il en i a IIII selonc ceste forme:	 sometimes it is done with cautionery in the middle on the top of the haunch, for which there are four according to this shape:
Et se tu vues, si le cauterize au cautere dou cercle que nos avons devant dit en la dislocation de la hainche;	 And if you see, if you cauterize at the circular cautery that we have mentioned in the dislocation of the haunch;
mais fai en teil maniere que li cercles conteigne toute la hainche, et tous li espés dou keur soit ars.	 But make it so that the circles contain the entire hunchback, and all the humps should be burned.
Et c’est li maniere c’on fait en sciatique, quant li dolor tient en la hainche, et ne parvient mie jusc’a la cuisse ne jusc’a la jambe.	 And this is the method for treating sciatica when the pain remains in the loin and does not reach as far as the thigh nor the leg.
Et s’ele vient jusc’a la cuisse et la jambe, se li fai II cauteres lai ou li malaides dit que li dolor li tient, et I cautere desus la cheville IIII dois, a la partie senestre un poc;	 And if it comes up to the thigh and leg, make II cauterizations there where the patient says the pain is, and the fourth finger width above the ankle on the left side.
et soit li cauteres cutellaire, et soit arse li espesseté dou keur;	 And let the cautery be a surgical instrument, and let the thickness of the coal be sharp.
et se li malaides sent que li dolor s’estende jusc’a dois dou piet ou pres d’enqui, se le cauterize la ou il sent la dolor III poins ou IIII au cautere qui est apelez «poins».	 If the patient feels that the pain extends to the thigh or near it, cauterize the place where they feel the pain with three or four points of the cautery which is called "points".
Et se mestiers est, se li en fai plus;	 And if necessary, do more.
et se il seit que li dolor soit desoz le genoil vers la cuisse, se li fais cautere au cautere cutellaire ou circulaire, et te done bien garde en tous tes cauteres que tu n’i lassier mie tant le cautere que tu brules les ners et les grans arteres, et que tu ne faices au malaide plus grant nuisance et contraction.	 And if the pain is under the knee towards the thigh, perform a cautery with the surgical instrument or circular cautery, but be careful in all your cauterizations not to allow the cautery to burn nerves and large arteries, nor to do greater harm and constriction to the patient.
Et je meisme ai veus plusors qui ont fait cautere sus la cheville dou piet, et li lasserent tant que li jambe fut toute enflee, et li piez ausi, et fut perciez et corrumpus toz li piez.	 And I myself have seen many who made fire cautery on the heel of the foot, and they let it grow so much that the leg was swollen all over, and the toes as well, and all the toes were pierced and corrupted.
Aprés une solution de ventre dont il ot la mort.	 After a belly solution where he died.
Et se li dolors est en II parties ensamble, fai cautere en l’une et en l’autre, selonc ceste maniere.	 And if the pain is in two places at once, do cautery on one and the other, according to this method.
Et li saige dirent en la cautere de la hainche, de coi ci est li maniere, fai I tel fer et soit au chief ausi gros com uns nauvillon de dacte, ou un poc moins, et soit par entrechetres et soit des l’un entrechetres jusc’a l’autre d’espaice la quantiteit d’un nou de poce;	 The wise men say about the cautery of the inguinal region, as follows: make a nail-like iron and its head should be as big as a thumbnail or slightly smaller, and it should have perforations or be one-perforated with a distance of the size of a nut.
et soient li entrechetres aovers de II pars, et soient aussi comme noez, et i ait I mainche de fer bien fait;	 And let the joints above the two parts be over-sized, and also like nuts, and have a hinge made of iron there.
et c’est li forme:	 and this is its form:
Et soit eschaufez tant qu’il soit toz rouges et giete senteles, et puis le mette on sus la boiste de la hainche malaide, et soit tornez sus lou sain costeit;	 And let it be heated until it becomes all red and emits sparks, then place it on the sick person's chest, turning it to the healthy side.
et lou cauterize une fois I cautere reont et lou laisse III jors;	 And apply the fire cautery once, and leave it for three days.
et puis fai emplaustre de burre, et laisse la plaie aoverte lonc tens;	 Then make a plaster of butter and leave the wound open for a long time;
aprés la cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	 After the healing of the ointment until it is healed.
Albucasim dit que nos usons poc de cest cautere por la paor de son regart, et se voions poc qui en usent;	 Al-Bukassim says that we should use this cautery with caution due to fear of its sight, and it is not widely used.
et toutevoie ceu est des boins cauteres, qui le puet soffrir, et lai ou il s’afiert.	 And this is one of the good cauterizations, which can be endured, and there where it hurts him.
Li cauteres de medicine ardant si est que tu faices I estrument a entrechetres en coi dessende li marge de la porte, et soit d’arain ou de fer a une paroit longe, et en la hautece ait II nous, et ait entre chaicun la quantiteit de la groissece d’un doi;	 The cautery of medicine heat is to make the instrument between the joints in such a way as to cut through the edge of the opening, and it should be of iron or steel with a long shaft, and at each end have two noses, and between each nose the thickness of a thumb.
et soient overt defuer et desus, et se joignent ensamble selonc ceste forme:	 and be opened outward and upward, and join together according to this shape:
Aprés met sus la boiste de la hainche au malaide gisant sor suin costeit sain, et apresse ta main mout sus la boiste de la hainche;	 After place the box of the iron heated in the patient lying on his side, and after put your hand much above the box of the iron.
aprés giete entre les II cercles de l’awe chaude qui soit chaufee au feu I poc, et li laisse une houre dou tens, et soffre li malaides la chalor et l’arsure de li.	 After pour between the two circles of hot iron which is heated in the firepot and leave it for an hour and let the patient endure the heat and the burning from it.
Car il i trueve mordication ausi com de feu;	 It bites like a bite from fire;
et quant li mordications iert passee, se lieve ta main avec l’estrument et leve la hainche d’awe douce, et laisse ensi III jors, et met sus burre tant que ceu qui est noir de l’eschaudure soit osteit;	 And when the bites have passed, lay your hand with the instrument and lift the swelling gently, and leave it for three days, and put butter over it so that the blackness from the burn is removed.
et lou laisse III jors que porriture en istrait;	 and let it remain for three days so that pus drains out.
et ceu serait li derriene aide aprés le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	 And this would be the final aid after treatment with ointments until it is healed.
Et se li dolor s’est estendue jusc’a la cuisse ou jusc’a la jambe, se li fai I estrument que teigne awe selonc ceu que tu as fait en la hainche igaument;	 And if the pain extends to the thigh or leg, make the instrument that burns accordingly, as you have done in the swelling.
et c’est li maniere de l’awe chaude, et je l’ai escripte ou traitier de la rectification de medicine.	 And this is the method of hot burn, and I have written or treated it concerning the correction of medicine.
Pren alcali et chaulz vive, autant de l’une com de l’autre, et les broie ensamble, et les met en I nuef pot.	 Take alkali and hot live coal, equal amounts of each, grind them together, and put them in a new pot.
ou il ait I petit pertuis defuer se que li pointe d’un raisor i puisse entreir;	 If there is a small opening closed, ensure that the tip of a razor can enter it.
et met desor celui pot I autre pot bien plombeit, et met sus alcali et chalz et awe douce sus, tant qu’il en i ait I doi desus les poudres cant tu l’avras bien preingte a ta main;	 Then place one pot upon another well weighed pot, and put on top of it alkali and salt and warm water until there is the right amount of powder above it when you have well pressed it with your hand.
et le laisse ensi tant qu’il en dessende awe ague et chiece ou pot plombeit, puis pren toute cele awe, et la giete sus chalz et sus alcali si com devant.	 And leave it like that until it descends warm and thick or the pot becomes weighed; then take all of that water, and pour it over salt and over alkali as before.
Et lors si sera mout ague et est aministree en mou d’ovraiges de medicine et en cauteres d’autres membres.	 And then it will become very thick and be used for the workings of various medicines and for other cauterizations of members.
Car elle fait auteil oevre com feus, et si a autres medicines dont on cauterize bien la hainche ensi com tesisie et miel anacardi et chalz avec savon, toutes ces choses mellees ensamble.	 For it has the same effect as fire, and if other medicines are cauterized in this way, such as figs and honey, aniseed and salt with soap; all these things mixed together.
Et Galiens nos raconte une cure dont uns hons fut curez de la dolor de la hainche et de la voine sciatique, et lou loe mout, et dit que on n’i fist autre cure, et qu’il en fut sanez a une soule fois quant on ot fait ceste cure, et il se fut baigniez si com il l’enseigne ci aprés.	 And Galen tells us of a cure in which a nobleman was healed from the pain of the hernia and sciatica, and he praised it much, and said that no other treatment was used, and that he became healthy once when this cure was performed, and he bathed himself as he instructs hereafter.
Et dist en teil maniere que tu preignes dou litargire vert fres et sec, et le broie mout avec I poc de graisse, et met sus la hainche et sus la cuisse et sus la jambe ou la dolor tient, et la lie;	 And in this manner, you take the green ground-ivy root, dry and powdered, and grind it with a little fat, then place it on the back, thigh, and leg where there is pain, and hold it.
et li laisse III houres et par la quantiteit que li malaides ne sente plus l’arsure.	 And leave it for three hours until the patient no longer feels the burning sensation.
Et puis le fai entrer ou bain tant que li cors li soit un poc arousez, et lou fai entrer ou lit, et li dolor s’en ira toute et sera sanez.	 And then make him enter the bath until his body is slightly warmed, and make him lie down, and the pain will leave completely and he will be cured.
Et saiches que nuls ne doit user de cautere de telz medicines, se ceu n’est aprés l’evacuation de cors.	 And know that no one should use fire cautery of such medications unless after the evacuation of the body.
Et Dyascorides dist que quant li voine sciatique est cauterizee de fiens de chievre, si i aide mout;	 And Dioscorides says that when the sciatic vein is burned with goat's-beard (greater burnet), it helps very much.
et doit estre fais li cauteres en teil maniere.	 The cautery should be done in this manner.
Prenez lainne et la beurez d’oile vielz, et metez sus la fossete qui est entre le pouce dou piez et l’autre qui est apelez foscile.	 Take linen and beat it with old oil, and place it over the furrow which is between the big toe of the foot and the other one which is called the "fossicle".
Aprés pren fiens de chievre sec, et l’empren a feu tant qu’il soit charbons, et lou met sus la laine, et le laisse tant qu’il soit estains;	 After taking dry goat's-beard and heating it until it is charcoal, place it on wool and leave it until it cools.
et refai encor ensi, et ne cesser de faire ensi tant que tu penses par sens qu’il viegne jusc’a la hainche, et que li dolor soit cessee;	 And set it again thus, and do not stop doing so until you think by reason that it will come to the hinge, and that the pain is ceased.
et cist manieres de cautere est apelez «cautere de chievre».	 And this manner of cautery is called "cautery of goat".
de la dolor dou dos	of the pain in the back
Quant dolor vient au dos, ou par cheoir ou de percussion ou par trop grant evacuation, ou par semblans de matiere espandue froide, a nule de ces semblances ne vaut cauteres, fuer que a celi qui vient de infusion de froide matiere.	When pain comes to the back, either by falling or from impact or excessive evacuation, or from similar causes of cold matter spreading, none of these cases are worth cauterization, unless it is due to the influx of cold matter.
Il covient c’aprés ceu que li malaides est voidiez de pilules fetides ou d’autres semblans, que on li faice sus lou dos, lai ou li dolor tient, trois lignes signies d’enche, et en chescune ligne V cauteres ou plus selonc la vertut et la quantiteit que li malaides puet soffrir;	 Afterwards, the patient must be purged with foul pills or similar things, which are made on the back where the pain is, three lines marked with a cross, and in each line V cauteries or more according to the potency and quantity that the patient can bear.
et soit fait li cauteres selonc le cautere qui est apelez «poins»;	 And the cautery should be made according to the cautery which is called "points".
et se tu vues, fai III cauteres ou IIII au cautere clavile moien selonc ceste forme:	 If you wish, make three or four cauteries or five in the middle cautery according to this form:
Maintes fois vient ceste maladie as petis enfans, et li signes de l’encomencement si est qu’il ont estroite alainne quant il se lievent, et paor;	 This disease often comes to small children, and the signs of its onset are that they have narrow throats when they cry and fear.
et tu trueves en la derriene espinee dou dos et en nous l’apparance qui vient sus les autres espinees.	 and you will find it in the lower spine at the back and in its appearance which comes on other spines.
Quant tu vois ceu et tu le vues curer, si le cauterize au cautere de celcle selonc ceste forme.	When you see this thing and intend to cure it, cauterize it with the fire cautery according to this form.
Si que li cautere porpreigne chescune partie de l’espinee egaument.	 The fire cautery increases every part of the spine.
Et se tu vues, si cauterize entor l’espinee au cautere poignant II lignes ou III, et soient li poins pres l’uns de l’autre.	 And if you see, cauterize around the spine with the cautery pointing to two or three lines, and let the tips be close to each other.
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez selonc ceu que nos avons dit, et warde que tu n’amenistrer cautere en gilbositeit qui soit en spame de nerf.	 After curing the joint until it is healed as we have said, make sure you do not administer the cautery in the hollow of a nerve.
de la dolor des jointes	of the pain of the joints
Quant dolor de jointes sunt de moistors que sont espandues a chaicun membre dou cors, et quant dolor vient em piez, que li mire apelent «podagre» proprement, et quant elle est de froide cause et cures de medicines ne la puent curer, si est curez par cauteres en teil maniere:	 When joint pains are caused by moisture spreading to every member of the body, and when pain comes in the feet, which people call "gout" properly, and when it is due to coldness and medicines cannot heal it, then it is cured with cauteries in this way:
fai li mout de cauteres entor la jointure dou piet, et soit li cauteres olivaire selonc ceste forme:	 make the mortar of cautery around the joint of the foot, and let the cautery be olive oil shaped as follows:
Et s’il i a besoigne que tu poignes sus la faice dou piet, se li fai cautere a tot le cautere c’on claime «point».	 And if it is necessary to prick on the pelvis, make the cauterization with the whole cautery, as they claim "point".
Et se les dolors viegnent jusc’a genous et as autres jointures, et ceu avient maintes fois, se li fai cautere sus chaicun genoil III cauteres ou IIII de chescunne partie, a tout le cautere olivaire;	 And if the pains come up to the knee and other joints, which happens frequently, make fire cautery on each knee 3 or 4 times on each part, with every cautery olive oil.
et se tu as mestier de plus, si en fai plus, mais n’i tenir mie ta main fuers que tant que li espés dou keur soit ars.	 and if you need more, do more, but not too much that the charcoal from the fire is burnt out.
Et se les dolors dessendent jusc’a genoil et au dos, se li aministre le cautere que nos avons dit en son chapistre.	 And if the pains descend to the knees and the back, administer the fire cautery as we have said in its chapter.
Et se les dolors sunt as mains, si fai poins entor le foscile II lignes;	 And if the pains are in the hands, make points around the wrist two fingers' width.
et s’il remaint point de dolor as dois, si fai poins sus chescune jointe et sus lou poil de la main;	 and if there remains a point of pain at the elbow, make points on each joint and on the hair of the arm.
et se les dolors vienent jusc’as coutes ou jusc’as espaules, si cauterize chescune partie, et fai boin governement au malaide et penre medicines.	 And if the pains come up to the hips or shoulders, cauterize each part and take good care of the patient and consider remedies.
Car se tu li fais boin governement et tu purges fleume, si sera saneis a l’aide de Deu.	 For if you take good care of him and cleanse him with purgation, he will be healed with God's help.
de la routure dou syfac	From the cutting of the siphac
Quant routure vient en angres, et li bouelz dessendent as coions et c’est novelement, si covient que quant tu lou vues curer, qu’il ne menjuce mie celui jor;	 When rottenness comes in the throat and the bowels descend into the chest, and this is new, if you wish to cure it, it should not eat anything that day.
et qu’il use choses qui laichent lou ventre, si que li fiens dessende de son ventre;	 and use things that relieve the stomach, so that the phlegm descends from the stomach;
aprés le fai seoir sus son dos entre tes mains, et li comande qu’il teigne son alaine tant que li boueil soient repairiet, et les ramoinne a tes dois, et seigne d’enche desoz la routure sus l’os dou poignil, et a tout un signe que soit semblans a la moitiet d’un cercle a desus dou cors;	 after doing so, make him lie on his back between your hands, and command him to press his lower abdomen until the bowels are repaired, and pull them to your sides, and sign below the rottenness on the bone of the thumb, and at a single sign that is similar to half of a circle above the chest;
puis eschaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	 then heat the fire cautery in the shape as follows:
tant qu’il soit blans et qu’il giete senteles.	 until it becomes white and exudes blood.
Puis ramoine les bouels a lor leu;	 Then reattach the bones to their place.
et li ministres teigne sa main sus qu’il ne retornent arrier;	 and the minister anoints his hand so that they do not return back.
et oevre bien les cuisses au malaide, et met desoz lui I cussin et I serjant sus les cuisses, et I autre sus lou pis qui li teigne les mains;	 and work the thighs on the patient, place the cushion and the servant under his thighs, and another one holding his hands.
puis met le cautere sus lou signe a tout ta main, et lou tien droit et lou tien tant que tu ateignes l’os, et se tu ne l’ateins la premiere fois, si le rencomence encor une autre tant que tu viegnes jusc’a l’os;	 then place the fire cautery on the spot with your whole hand, hold it straight and hold until you reach the bone; if you don't reach it the first time, try again until you reach the bone.
et te warde subtilment que li boueil ne saille quant tu fais lou cautere;	 and be careful that the bone does not split when making the cautery.
que tu ne le brulasses;	 do not burn it.
et que par ceu li malaides ne muere, ou autre malz.	 so that the patient does not die or suffer harm.
Et saiches que quant tu ne viens jusc’a l’os au cautere, tes ovraiges ne vaut rien.	 And know that if you do not reach the bone during the cautery, your efforts are worth nothing.
Et covient que li cauteres des enfans soit subtilz selonc la mesure d’ous, et des grans gens aussi grans selonc lor mesure;	 And the cauteries for children should be subtle according to their measurement, and for grown-ups, they should be as large as theirs.
aprés III jors cure lou leu dou cautere de burre tant que li eschaudure soit ostee;	 After three days of care, treat the shoulder with butter until the burn is healed;
aprés le cure d’autres oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez, et gise li malaides XL jors sus son dos tant que li plaie soit bien soudee;	 After treating with other remedies until it is healthy, let the patient lie down for 40 days on his back so that the wound heals well.
et covient que ses norrissemens soit lassatis longement, si que li boueil ne saillent quant il se preigdra d’aler en chambres.	 And it is necessary to restrict his movements for a long time so that the boils do not emerge when he gets up to go to the chamber.
Et aprés XL jors, quant il se voudra lever, se li amenistre une faixe bien faite, et la porse XL autres jors;	 And after 40 days, when he wants to get up, a bed is prepared for him and he rests for another 40 days.
et ait boin repos, qu’il se travaille poc et se warde de trop grant repletion de boivre et de mengier, et de trop haut braire;	 And let him have good rest, that he should work little and beware of excessive drinking and eating, and of too much laughter.
et quant il fait cest enseignement si est sanez entierement.	 And when he follows this instruction, he will become entirely well.
Et je dirai ci aprés la cure de taillier en son chapistre.	 And I shall say after the treatment of amputation in its chapter.
de la routure dou ventre	of the rupture of the abdomen (lit: of the bursting of the belly)
Quant routures vienent en autres ventres et sont connisans, et tu vues qu’elles ne croissent plus, se li fai I cautere dou cautere reont selonc sa quantiteit, et soit ars li tiers dou keur;	 When roundworms come into other bellies and are known, and you see that they no longer grow, then perform the cautery of the cautery according to its quantity, and let it be burned the third degree.
aprés le cure selonc ceu que nos avons dit;	 After the cure according to what we have said;
et aucun des anciens ont dit c’on le doit cauterizer au cautere a III angles selonc ceste forme:	 and no one of the ancients has said that it should be cauterized at the cautery with three angles in this form:
mais signe premier le leu d’enche et fai une ligne per la largesce desus la routure, et une autre defuers, et main ta main emmi a tout le cautere clavile.	 but first mark the location and make a line above the roundworm, and another below, and then place your hand on the entire sharp-pointed cautery.
Mais li premiers cauteres est plus legiers et muedres.	 But the first cauteries are lighter and more mobile.
de dolor anciene en aucun membre	of old pain in any member
Quant dolor vient en aucun membre, ou de cheoir ou de ferir, et cele dolor tient lonc tens, et li cure de medicine n’i vaut, adonc covient qu’il soit cauterizeis au cautere qui est apelez «poins», et soit li cauteres selonc la longesce dou membre et la petitece et sa foibleteit et sa vertut et sa location de torcions et de sa dolor.	 When pain comes in any member, either from falling or being injured, and that pain lasts a long time, and medicine does not heal it, then you should cauterize with the cautery called "poins," and the cauterizing should be according to the length of the limb, its smallness, weakness, its virtue, its location for twisting, and its pain.
s’il est sanez dou premier cautere, c’est bien;	 if it is healed by the first cautery, that is good.
se ceu nom, recomence I autre cautere sus celui, car teilz costume est qu’il se doit muer au membre que li est prochiens, por coi il covient que tu faices les cauteres tant que li malaides soit saneis.	 If that limb has a recurrence of the disease, then perform another cautery on it, because it is customary that it should be changed to the nearest member; therefore, you must perform the cauteries as long as the patient is not healed.
de meselerie	When the humors are out of balance due to moisture and heat, and one feels pain or discomfort, it must be purged through purgation. This involves taking a mixture of wormwood, myrtle leaves, and bread soaked in vinegar, which will help to cleanse and cool the body. After this, you should drink a cold water concoction made from crushed ivy, plantain seeds, or other suitable herbs, which will further aid in balancing the humors and alleviating the discomfort.
Li meseil sont aidiet aucune fois par cautere par grant aide, et meismement li maladie que vient de la putrefaction de fleume et de melancolie.	 The cautery is sometimes helpful to a great extent, and equally so the patient who comes from the putrefaction of phlegm and melancholy.
Cant tu la vues cauterizer, pren warde se li maladie est au comencement, et s’ele est curee selonc ceu que nos avons dit en la division, et ne dessent ne ne demoure, et tu doutes que li corruption ne porpreigne tout le malaide, adonques li fai V cauteres sus lou chief:	 Can you see the patient to be cauterized, take care if the patient is at the beginning of the disease, and if it has been cured according to what we have said in the division, neither draw nor remain, and if you doubt that corruption will affect the entire patient, then perform V cauteries on the head:
I emmi le chief a nouf, et l’autre vers lou front a la fin des chevous;	 Bring the head to you and the other towards the forehead at the end of the hairline.
et II sus les II cornes, et I derrierre sus le haiterel;	 And place it on top of both horns, and the other behind the occiput (the back of the head).
et i laise tant ta main que li cauteres viegne jusc’a l’os, et tant que les escorces en issent fors si que les vapors des grosses humors s’en puissent issir;	 And leave your hand so that the cautery reaches the bone, and so that the scabs come out through it, allowing the vapors of the large humors to escape.
et le cauterize sus la mice selonc ce qu’il est devant.	 And cauterize on the mouse (a swelling) according to what is before.
Et se li meselerie est partout esparse;	 And if the mixture is scattered everywhere;
et elle pert manifestement, si covient que tu lou cauterizes de ces cauteres que nos avons dit ou chief, et I cautere en som lou neis, et II cauteres sus l’espinee dou col, et VI cauteres sus l’espinee dou dos, et I grant sus la crupie et I autre delez, et II sus les II espaules;	 If the mixture is clearly dispersed, then you must apply the cauterization using the cauteries as we have said above, and the cautery on the neck, and six cauteries on the spine of the back, and one large one and another small one on the crotch, and two more on the shoulders;
et II sus les coutes, et II sus les tendrons dou pis, et I sus chascune jointe des mains et des piez, et sus les fosses des mains;	 and two more on the sides, and two on the tendons of the thighs, and one above each joint of the hands and feet, and over the hollows of the hands.
et te warde des ners que sunt sus lou derrien calcant, que tu ne les bruler;	 And beware of the nerves that are located above the last bone of the foot, do not burn them.
et aucune fois fait om cautere sus l’os dou poignil, et I autre sus l’os de l’estomac, et I autre sus lou foie.	 Sometimes make a cautery on the bone of the knuckle, and one on the bone of the stomach, and another on the liver.
Et saiches que quant plus i fais de cautere, plus li fais d’aide, et mues li profite;	 And know that when you perform more cautery, you provide more help, and it benefits them more.
et saiches que li malaides ne sent point de dolor au cautere si com li sain le sentent, por ce que li cors est ja toz corrumpus.	 And know that the sick do not feel pain from the cautery as much as the healthy do, because the body is already completely corrupted.
Et covient ke li cautere soient grant et petit selonc les membres et les jointures, selonc ceu que vos lou troverez en manieres des fers.	 And it should be great and small according to the members and the joints, as you will find in the ways of iron smithing.
Aprés cure lou leu de farine de veces avec miel et autres cures tant qu’il soit saneis.	 After curing the shoulder with flour several times with honey and other remedies until it is healed.
Quant enfleure vient en aucun membre et est curee par medicines et oiles et emplastres, et il n’est mie sanez, adonques li fai cauteres sus le membre selonc la grandour et la petitece dou membre;	 When swelling occurs in any member and is treated with medicine, oil, plasters and it is not cured, then apply cautery on the affected member according to the size and smallness of the member.
et soit li cauteres un poc entrans en l’espés dou keur;	 and let the cautery be a small incision in the thickness of the skin.
puis le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	 Then, if it is cured with liniments until it becomes healthy.
Et aucune fois fait on cautere et a la main et au piet et au dos, a l’issue dou nerf que muet le membre, et ensi si est ostee li enfleure;	 Sometimes, cautery is done on the hand, foot and back, at the root of the nerve that paralyzes the member, and in such cases the swelling is removed.
et toutevoie ne s’en entremette nuls s’il n’est conoissans des membres et des issues des ners movans lou cors.	 And no one else shall interfere unless he is knowledgeable about the members and the nerves moving the body.
de albaras	Of ulcers or sores
Quant li maladie qui est apelee «albaras» est enveillie, et li engien de medicine n’i valent rien, adonques le cauterize d’un cautere un poc parfont, selonc la quantiteit de l’espés dou keur, tant que li blenchour soit ostee, et soit muee sa color;	 When the disease called "albaras" arises, and the remedy of medicine is of no value, then cauterize it with a cautery of moderate depth according to the size of the wound until the white becomes exposed and its color changes.
puis le cure de farine de veces et de lentilles avec oile roset et foilles de plantain, et sanc de colon et sanc d’alondre, de chescun une partie;	 then cure it with flour and lentils with rose oil and banana leaves, cow's blood and swan's blood, each one in part.
et soit mellez tout ensamble, et soit liiez d’un drapel, et soit aers au leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	 Mix all together, tie it up with a cloth, and apply to the wound until it is healed.
li cure de chancre par cautere	Cure syphilis by cauterization
Quant chancre vient au comencement, et tu lou vues arrester, si le cauterize au cautere qui semble I cercle, tout entor au tour dou chancre.	 When a boil begins and you wish to stop it, if you cauterize, do so with the circular fire cautery all around the circumference of the boil.
Et toutevoie li saige dirent que on faice cautere ausi au mileu dou chancre;	 And wise people would also say that a cautery is made in the middle of the boil;
et toutevoie ceu ne me semble mie boin, car je redous que il ne soit ulcerez et corrumpus, et je l’ai ja veut avenir aucune fois;	 and this does not seem good to me, for I think that it should not be ulcerated and corrupted, and I have experienced it happening once before;
et plus droituriere chose est qu’il soit cauteriés entor, au cautere qui est apelez «circule», si com nos avons dit en mout de cauteres.	 and a more proper thing is that it should be cauterized around, using the cautery called "circule", as we have said in our discussion on cauteries.
de l’enfleure qui ne puet meurer	Of the swelling which cannot grow
Quant aucuns ait une maladie qui est apelee «adubelati», et elle tarde de meurer ou por la superfluiteit qu’ele fait ou por l’eaige dou malaide quant il est decrepites (c’est a dire trop vielz) et il a poc de sanc, ou por lou tens;	 When someone has a disease called "adubelati", and it does not want to heal or because of the excess fluid it produces or because the patient is weakened (meaning too old) and has little blood, or because of the cold;
et tu la vues haster de meurer:	 And you see it hasten to grow:
adonques le cauterize entor de mout de petis cauteres en poignant;	 Then cauterize it with many small cauteries, pricking around:
aprés le laisse ensi.	 After that, let it be as such.
Car elle se hastera de meureir.	 Then it will hasten to heal.
Et se tu la vues percier a tout le cautere, si chaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	And if you see that the wound is pierced completely with all the cautery, heat the cautery in this manner:
Et met ta main en mileu de cele maladie qui est apellee «adubelati» tant que li cauteres ait perciet lou keur, et soit telz li cauteres que li malaides lou sente defuers en teil maniere que li cours de la porriture soit alegis.	 And put your hand in the middle of that disease called "adubelati" as long as the cauteries have pierced through, and let the cauteries be such that the patient feels no pain from them in this manner so that the course of the pustule is clear.
Aprés le cure tant qu’il soit sanez parfaitement.	 After the patient has recovered completely.
li cure dou feu par fer	the fire cure with iron
Une autre maniere de maladie i a qui est apelee «corrodens», et n’est autre chose que une mengeson de membre, car ele menjut les membres ausi com li feus les leignes seches.	 Another kind of disease called "corroding", and it is nothing but an eating away of a limb because it consumes them as fire consumes dry wood.
Se tu vois ceste maladie en leu qui puisse soffrir cautere ensamble feu, adonques eschaufe les cauteres clavile mout petit et grant, selonc ceu qu’il covient au leu ou li maladie est;	 If you see this disease in a place where it can bear the cautery along with fire, then heat the small and large cauteries very hot, according to what is necessary for the place or the disease.
aprés le cauterize de toutes pars tant que tu erraiche toute la corruption, et nen remaigne rien de li, que tout ceu qui est corrumpus ne soit osteit.	 After that, cauterize everywhere until you eradicate all the corruption, and nothing remains of it, so that everything corrupted is removed.
Et puis le laisse III jors, et met sus les leus cauterizez soffre broiet avec oile tant que les eschaudures dou feu soient ostees, et toute li corruption.	 And then leave it for three days and put on the affected areas softened cauteries made with oil until the burns caused by fire are removed, and all the corruption.
Aprés lou cure d’oignemens engendrans char.	 After the cure of ointments generating heat.
Et se tu vois aprés III jors que chars saine ne naisse, c’est boin;	 And if after three days you see healthy flesh not growing, that is good;
et se ceu non, si rencomence le cautere sus ceu qui est demoreit des leus corrumpus.	 and if that's not the case, then begin to cauterize again on the remaining corrupted parts.
Et ceste mengeson est aucune fois esteit curee de medicine ague en leu de cautere de feu;	 And this dislocation has sometimes been cured with medicine instead of fire cautery;
mais toutevoie cautere de feu est de plus grant aide, et j’ai ja dit la cure de la medicine ague en la division:	 However, fire cautery is of greater aid, and I have already said the cure for medicine ague in the section on division:
pren la quant tu en as mestier.	 Take it when you need it.
des porrelz qui vienent as piez	The growing hairs should be allowed to remain long and equal on the feet;
Mout de fois avient que as piez par defuers naist une maladie qui est apelee «clos» selonc nostre entencion, et est une grosse chose fautree qui blece lou piet.	 Often happens that in the foot through an opening comes a disease called "close" according to our intention, and it is a large thing swollen which breaks the foot.
Et li cauteres de ceste maladie si est selonc II manieres.	 And the cauteries of this disease are according to two ways.
C’est a savoir cautere de feu, et cautere d’aigue chaude.	 This is to know fire cautery, and hot water cautery.
Cautere de feu si est que tu eschaufe I cautere cheveit ausi com est une penne de vouteul, et soit fait de boin fer a la mesure qu’il puisse porpenre le clou de toutes pars, et qu’il i ait subtilz marges;	 Heat the fire cautery as you would heat a pen of hot iron, and make it from good iron to the size that can penetrate through all parts, and that it has fine edges;
aprés le met tout chaut sus lou clou, et torne ta main tot entor le clou tant qu’il viegne au font dou clou;	 Afterwards place the heated cautery on top of the nail, and turn your hand all around the nail until it reaches the point of the nail;
et lou laisse ensi III jors tant qu’il encomence giter porriture;	 and leave it like this for three days until it begins to emit pus.
puis li fai un emplaustre de malves savaiges broiies avec seil, et laisse l’emplaustre sus toute la nuit, et li clous cherra et sera desracinez de ses racines.	 Then make a poultice of bad wild herbs ground with oil, and leave the poultice on it all night, and the nails will grow out and be uprooted from their roots.
Puis cure le leu d’oignement enjanrant char tant qu’il soit sanez.	 Then heal the wound with healing salve until it is healed.
Et s’il sont convertit par defuers lou cors, et maintes fois avient et en mains et em piez, si covient que tu i amenistres cautere d’aigue chaude;	 And if it is converted through the body and often occurs in hands and feet, then you must bring hot cautery.
et est en teil maniere:	 and this is done thus:
pren une cainne d’arain ou de fer, ou une penne de vouteul, et met sus lou clou et l’althelul, c’est asavoir porrelz verrues;	 Take a cane of iron or wood, or a feather from a bird's quill, and place it on the nail and the blister, which means for treating warts.
et met la cainne sus si qu’ele porpreigne tout entor, puis i met un poc d’awe chaude, et retien bien ta main, et presse ta main en tornant si que li marge de la cainne viegne a la racine dou clou, et puisse trover l’aigue chaude voie parfonde jusc’a la racine;	 and place the cane on it so that it presses all around, then put some hot oil on it, and hold your hand firmly, and press your hand while turning so that the edge of the cane comes to the root of the nail, and let the hot oil penetrate deeply until it reaches the root.
et soffre li malaides un poc la mordication de l’aigue chaude une houre;	 and let the patient suffer a little bit from the bite of the hot oil for an hour.
puis le laisse ensi, et il se derracinera tous a tout ses racines.	 then leave it like that, and it will rot away completely at its roots.
Ensi fai un aprés autre, tant que tu esraiches toz ces qui sont au cors, puis les cure des oignemens qui engenrent char.	 As another does afterwards, while you cauterize all those on the body, then treat with ointments that soothe pain.
li cure dou trembler	The cure for trembling
Quant aucuns tremble de froidor de ners, ou de fievre quartaine ou d’autre, si covient que tu li faices IIII cauteres ou IV sus l’espinee dou dos, I cautere entre chescune espinee;	 For those who shiver from cold or quartan fever, or any other ailment, it is necessary that you perform four or five cauteries on the spine of the back, one between each vertebra.
et I cautere ou pez, et I sus l’estomac au cautere olivaire;	 And the cautery or flesh, and on top of the stomach the olive oil cautery.
si laissera lou trembler, et se hastera li santez de la maladie froide.	 Allow it to tremble, and hasten the health from the cold disease.
des pustules puans	pus-filled boils
Aucune fois apperent par defuers le cors bathes, ou pustules puans, que vienent de grosses matieres corrumpues.	 Sometimes, from the body's outside appear baths of pus or boils that come from large, corrupted matter.
si covient au premier quant eles apperent que on faice cautere sus chescun chief de la pustule:	 It is necessary at first when they appear that you perform cautery on each head of the pustule:
un cautere subtil de fust de mirte, de coi li pointe soit emprise au feu, ou de racine de aristologe longe, ou au cautere lenticulaire.	 a subtle cautery of myrtle staff, from which the tip is held in fire, or of long root of aristolochia, or to the cautery lenticular.
Et aucune fois les cauterize on au comencement quant il aperent, selonc ceste maniere, et il ne puent croistre des enqui en avant, mais est desrompue li superfluitez dont il vienent, et sont sanez;	 And sometimes you cauterize at the beginning when they appear in this way, and they cannot grow further, but the superfluidities that come from them are resolved, and they heal.
mais il covient que ceu soit fait aprés l’evacuation de sanc.	 but it must be done after the evacuation of blood.
quant li artere est copee	when an artery is cut
Maintes fois avient grans decorremens de sanc de l’artere qui est copee a la plaie que vient au pardefuers, ou a l’incision de l’aposteme, ou au cautere dou membre, et as semblans choses;	 Often there are great outflows of blood from the artery that is cut at the wound which goes to the outside, or in the incision of an abscess, or in the cauterization of a limb, and similar things.
et est mout grief chose d’estenchier.	 and it is a very harmful thing to let it pus out.
Et toutevoie quant ceu avient a aucun, si te haste de mettre ton doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne, et l’estrain mout tant que li sans soit apaisiez desoz ton doi, et que goute n’en isse plus;	 Furthermore, when this happens to anyone, hasten to place your finger on the wound of the vein, and press it very hard so that the blood is stopped below your finger, and no more pus comes out.
puis met au feu les cauteres olivaire plusors petis et grans tant qu’il soient tuit rouge;	 Then put the olive oil cauterization of various sizes, both small and large, until they are all red.
puis empren I, ou grant ou petit selonc la plaie et lou leu en coi li artere est route, et met le cautere sus cele voine ou tu tiens ton doi, et tien le cautere tant sus que li sans soit restainchiez.	 Then take [the tool], whether large or small, according to the wound and the location in which the artery is located, and place the cauterization on that vein where you hold your finger, and hold the cauterization in place until the blood is stopped.
Et s’il saut fuers quant tu lieves ton doi desus la voinne, et li cauteres estint, si pren hastivement .i. autre des cauteres qui sont au feu.	And if it jumps fiercely when you hold your thumb on the vein, and the cautery is extinguished, take hastily another one of the cauteries that are by the fire.
Et ne cesser de faire ceu l’un aprés l’autre tant que li sans soit estenchiez;	 And continue to do this one after another until the wound is cauterized;
et warde que tu n’ardes lou nerf qui est delez, et que autre malice ne viegne sus lou malaide;	 and be careful not to burn the nerve that has been exposed, and that no other harm comes to the patient.
et saiches que quant sans decourt de l’artere, c’on ne lou puet mie bien restenchier meismement quant li artere est grans, se ceu n’est par une des IIII manieres que nos avons dit:	 and know that when an artery is not cut through completely, it cannot be well stopped when the artery is large, unless by one of the four ways that we have mentioned:
ou par cautere, ou par extraction quant ele n’est mie traite, ou par fort liement de fil, ou par medicines mises sus qui ont pooir de restenchier sanc;	 or by cauterization, or by extraction if it has not been treated, or by tightly tying with thread, or by medicine placed on it that can stop the bleeding.
et soit liee et estrainte avennament.	 and it should be tied and compressed immediately.
Qui i amenistrera restenchement de liier estroitement de drapelz ou de metre choses ardans sus, ou autres semblans choses, se n’i profite se poc non.	Whoever administers constriction tightly with fabrics or placing hot things on it, or similar things, does not benefit from it unless otherwise.
Et se ce avient a aucun et il n’ait mie mire ne medicine present, si doit mettre son doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne si com nos avons dit, et bien estrendre tant qu’il soit restenchiez desus la plaie et desus la voinne;	 And if this happens and there is no eye or medicine present, it should place its index finger on the wound of the vein as we have said, and press firmly until the bleeding stops above the wound and above the vein.
et ne remuer lou doit, mais lou moille d’awe froide sovent que soit mout froide tant que li sans soit congelez et engrossiez et restenchiez;	 And it must not move, but the cold moisture should often be applied, very cold until the flesh is frozen and swollen and hardened;
et faice des enqui en avant ceu dont il a mestier de cauteres et de medicines.	 Make inquiries ahead about the kind of cauteries and medicines that are needed.
Ci encomence li secons livre des cures de taille	Here begins the second book of surgical treatments
Nos vos avons dit ou premier chapistre toute maladie en coi il covient cautere de feu, ou de medicine ardans, et les oquisons et les causes et les estrumens et les formes des cauteres;	 We have told you in the first chapter about every disease in which there is need for a fire cautery, or a hot medicine, and the signs, causes, instruments, forms, and methods of cauteries.
et ai mis celui chapistre des lou chief jusc’a piez, et je irai en cest chapistre par celi meisme voie por ceu c’on trueve plus legierement ceu c’on voura.	 I have put that chapter on the head and I will go in this chapter along the same path for those things which are more easily found.
Et ainsois que je encomence ceu, il covient, chier fil, que vos aprenez que en cest chapistre a plus de peril et de paor que ou premier des cauteres, et por ceu il covient plus grant cautele.	Furthermore, as I begin this, it is necessary for you, dear child, to learn that in this chapter there is more danger and fear than in the first of the cauteries, and because of this greater caution is required.
Car en l’ovraige de cest chapistre avient maintes fois evacuation de sanc a l’ovrir la voinne, et a l’incision sus aposteme, et as cures des plaies, et a l’estraction des saiettes, et a l’incision sus la piere, et les semblans choses;	 For in the work of this chapter, there is often the evacuation of blood when opening a vein, and incising an abscess, and in the treatment of wounds, and in the extraction of arrows, and in cutting into stones, and similar things;
ou il a doutance et paor, et en vient li mors a plusors.	 There is doubt and fear, and many die.
Et je vos amoneste que vos n’entreprenez folie.	 And I warn you not to undertake foolishness.
Car mout de manieres de gens vienent en cures.	 For many ways of people come in treatments.
si vienent de telz qui s’aïrent si avec lor maladie qu’il muerent legierement por la forsenerie qu’il trueve de sa maladie, et de la grandour de son malice;	 Those who suffer in such a way that they die quickly due to the perversity and severity of their disease.
et de ces doit on avoir paor.	 And of these one should have fear.
Et de ces i a qui te done son sens, et dit:	 And there are some who give you their sense, and say:
«atendez, je sui garis»;	 "Wait, I am ready.
et li maladie est despitouse.	 "and the patient is obstinate.
Il ne covient mie que vos vos consentez a ces qui vienent a vos qui ont ceste maniere, mais mettez plus grant cusanson en vostre honor qu’en vostre covoitise, et n’ovrez mie folement mais saigement de ceu dont vos estes certain, et dont vos poez avoir pris et los;	 "You should not easily consent to those who come to you who have this manner, but put greater consideration in your honor than in your desire, and do not rashly but wisely from what you are certain, and from what you can take and learn.
et usez de pronostication et de indication en cures de vos malaides a coi salus soit convertie;	 "and use prognostication and indication in the treatment of your patients so that health is turned.
et ceu vos aidera a aquester bone renommee, et gloire, et memoire de loenge.	 "and this will help you to acquire good reputation, glory, and memory of praise.
Tres chier fil, Nostres Sires vos doint boin entendement et droiture, et se vos vuelle espireir de la sainte inspiration de sa main, amen.	Dear child, our Lord grants you good understanding and righteousness; if you wish to inspire from the holy inspiration of His hand, come.
Or je vos ai ordeneit cest chapistre en devisant par chapistres, selonc ceu qu’il est devant ou chapistre des cauteres, que je vos ai deviseit des le chief jusc’a piez, por ceu que vos trovez plus legierement ceu dont vos avrez mestier.	I have divided this chapter for your convenience, speaking one topic at a time, as the cauteries were previously described from head to feet because you will find it easier to understand what you need in this manner.
dou chief plein d’aigue	The head full of water.
Saiches que ceste maladie vient mout de fois as enfans a l’enfanter, et quant li baille estraint trop fort le chief de l’enfant;	 "Know that this disease often comes to children when the head of the child is strangled too strongly.
et aucune fois vient ceu de cause reponue que on ne seit.	 And sometimes comes this from an unknown cause that one may not know.
Et je ne vis onques ceste maladie fuers qu’en enfans, et a toz ces que j’ai veus se hastait li mors;	 And I have never seen this illness in adults, and all those I have seen hastened death.
et por ceu me semble qu’il me vaut mues lassier l’ovraige en teilz cures.	 And because of that, it seems to me that I should abandon the work in some treatments.
Et je vis I enfant de coi li chiés estoit plains d’aigue, et li chief engroissoit chescun jor tant qu’il ne lou pooit sostenir;	 And I see an infant whose shoulders are swollen with water, and the head grows larger every day until it cannot be sustained.
et crut tant li moistor qu’il fut mors, et ceste moistor si est assemblee desoz l’os sus lou syphac, entre lou keur et l’os;	 The moisture grew so much that he died, and this moisture is collected under the bone above the shoulder joint, between the cartilage and the bone.
et li ovraiges si est telz se li moistor est entre lou keur et l’os, et li apostemes est petis, que tu fendes emmi lou chief une fendure large;	 The work is such that if the moisture is between the cartilage and bone, and the abscess is small, you cut a wide incision in the head.
et soit ausi longe com II nous, tant que li mostor corre;	 And let it be as long as he (the patient) does, while the moisture moves.
et vez ci la forme dou spatumile:	 Here comes the shape of the spatula:
Se li moistor est plus creue, et li aposteme soit plus grans, si fai .ij. fendures en maniere d’une croix, selonc ceste forme:	If the moisture is more swollen and the abscess is larger, make two incisions in the shape of a cross, according to this form:
Et se li moistor est desoz l’os, et li signes que tu vois les commissures dou chief overtes de chescune partie, et li aigue saut fuer quant tu la presses de ta main au dedens, et ceu ne t’est mie reponut:	 If the moisture is under the bone, and you see the signs that I show you, the openings of the skull on each part, and it does not respond when you press it from inside with your hand, then:
si covient que tu fendes enmi lou chief III fendures selonc ceste maniere:	 If you must make three cuts into the skull in this manner:
Et aprés l’incision estrai la moistor toute fuers.	 And after incision, remove all moisture from it.
Aprés estraint les fendures de drapelz et de poudres, et i met vin et oile, et laisse ensi jusc’a cinquieme jor;	 After closing the cuts with linen and powder, put wine and oil in them, and leave it until the fifth day.
puis le deslie, et cure la plaie par tentes et par oignemens, et laisse estraindre le chief egaument, et done mengier au malaide viande seche de poc de moistor tant que li membre soit confortez et sanez.	 Then undo the cuts, and cure the wound with bandages and ointments, let the skull grow stronger, and give the patient dry meat of moisture until the limb is comforted and healed.
Et une autre maniere d’incision est que tu regardes ou apert li grandor de l’aposteme, et li assemblé de l’aigue;	 And another way of incising is that you look for the size of the abscess and gather its pus.
car aucune fois est elle devant;	 Sometimes it is before;
aucune fois derrier;	 sometimes it is behind;
aucune fois en destre;	 sometimes on the right side;
et aucune fois en senestre.	 and sometimes on the left side.
Taille donques lai ou li aposteme apert, et l’emplissement de l’aigue, et lou fent selonc ce que tu en as le pooir;	 Therefore, cut there where the abscess opens, empty the pus, and do it according to what you are able.
et warde que tu ne coper l’artere;	 and ensure that you do not cover the artery.
et veigne flun de sanc, si que li malaides muere dou decorrement de sanc et de l’evacuation de moistor.	 And if there comes blood, let the patient die a natural death from bleeding and evacuation of moisture.
de reume	of scrofula (a chronic disease affecting the lymph nodes, often in the neck)
Quant il avient a aucun une maladie qui est apelee «catarre» as eulz ou au pis, et li maladie est anciainne, et li cure de medicine ne profite mie, adonques li derraine cure si est li cauteres avec ceu c’on li copera les .ij. arteres.	When a disease called "cataract" occurs in the eyes or at its worst, and the disease is old, and the medicine's cure does not help at all, then the last cure is the cautery with which they will cut the two arteries.
Il covient donques, cant tu les vues coper, que li malaides faice rere son chief;	 Therefore, when you see them covered, let the patient lie on his back.
aprés li frotte lou leu d’un drapel aspre tant que les arteres aperent, puis estraingne li malaides son col a tout I drapel;	 After rubbing the joint with a rough cloth until the arteries appear, then grasp the patient's neck with the cloth.
puis regarde ou li voine bait, et li leus de l’une et de l’autre sont aprés les oreilles, et poc sont reponues;	 Then look where the veins are biting, and the joints of one and the other are next to the ears, and they are set in place.
puis signe les leus d’enche, puis cope l’une et l’autre d’un spatumile agut de II pars, tant que li taille veigne jusc’a l’os, et ceu soit par lou large dou chief.	 Then mark the joints with a sharp awl of two parts, then pierce one and the other with it to the bone, and let it be through the wide part of the head.
Et se tu vues, boute le spatumile desoz l’artere et la cope au desus, en taillant ausi com .ij. dois au traver.	And if you see it (the artery), push the spatula under the artery and cut it above, cutting through as two fingers apart.
Et quant li voinne est copee, si saut li sans en haut continuelment fuers.	And when the vein is cut, it jumps up continuously without stopping.
Et se li artere n’apert au sentir, si covient que tu mesures la quantiteit de l’espaice de III dois, puis seigne d’enche et fent jusc’a l’os;	 And if the arteries do not open to the touch, it is necessary that you measure the distance of three fingers, then mark the joint and pierce to the bone.
et ceu qu’il covient dou sanc mettre fuers si est VI c/, et par aventure un poc plus ou moins, selonc ce que li malaides puet soffrir, et la repletion de l’artere;	 And it is necessary to force the blood out by 6 cubits [a unit of measurement], and perhaps a little more or less according to what the patient can endure, and the filling of the artery.
puis regarde la plaie:	 Then look at the wound:
s’il remaint sus l’os point dou syphac, si le cope que apostemes chaus n’i veigne, puis estrain la plaie et lie, et la cure d’oignement tant qu’ele soit sanee.	 If it remains on the bone without shifting, if the abscess does not open, then hold down the wound and tie it, and apply ointment until it is healed.
de emigrainne	of migration
Quant emigrainne anciaine vient, et catarre agut, por les moistors des larmes et les chalors en temples et sode anciene forsenee et semblans choses, et il est medicinez par manieres de cures de medicine et tout ceu ne li profite mie, si estraions les arteres des temples et lou cauterizons, si com nos avons conteit.	When the old migraine comes and the acute catarrh, because of moisture from tears and heat in temples and aged senility, accompanied by similar things, and it is treated with methods of medicine, but none of it helps him; then we must open the arteries of the temples and cauterize them as we have said.
Et li maniere de l’estraction d’elles si est que li malaides faice rere les poilz de ses temples, et entende a l’artere qui apert en la temple, car elle apert bien par son batement, et est poc reponue fuers que en aucuns homes qui sont trop froit;	 And the manner of extracting them is that the patient should bend his head backward towards his temples, and listen to the artery that opens in the temple, as it opens well with its beating, and is easily found except in some men who are very cold.
et s’elle est reponue, si estraigne son col li malaides d’aucuns drapelz, puis frote le leu d’aucun aspre drap, et arose le leu d’aigue chaude tant que li artere apere manifestement;	 and if it is found, the patient should pull his neck with some cloths, then rub the place with a sharp cloth, and wash the place with warm water until the artery appears clearly.
puis pren le spatumile de coi ci est li forme:	 Then take the sponge that is of this form:
puis escorche le cuir legierement tant que tu veignes a l’artere, puis la trai en haut as pinceures, et la depart bien des toiles que sont desoz li de chescune partie;	 Then peel the skin lightly until you reach the artery, then pull it up towards the prongs, and carefully remove the cloths that are underneath each part.
et se li artere est subtilz, si la torne a la pointe de l’uncine, puis la cope de celle partie selonc la quantiteit des II chiés.	 And if the artery is thin, turn it at the point of the uncinus, then cut off that part according to the size of the two shoulders.
Car s’elle n’est copee, si ne saut mie li sans dou tout en tout.	 If it is not cut, it will not heal completely in all places.
Et trai dou sanc des VI c/, jusc’a III;	 Draw blood from the six veins, up to three.
et se li artere est grans, si covient que tu la lies en II leus d’un fil double fort de soie, que porriture n’i veigne devant le soudement de la plaie, et veigne decorremens de sanc;	 And if the artery is large, you must tie it with a strong double silk thread so that pus does not come before the wound's stitching, and there is a flow of blood.
puis cope la superfluiteit qui est entre les II liiens en celle houre meisme, et puis, se tu vues, si lou cauterize dou cautere cutellaire jusc’a l’os tant que li chiés soient copez;	 Then remove the excess that is between the two ligatures at that same hour itself, and if you see, cauterize the wound with a hot iron until it reaches the bone, so that the shoulder is cut off.
et c’est li muedre oevre, se li malaides n’a fievre et il est de chaude complexion.	 And it is the grinding work, if the patient does not have fever and he is of a warm constitution.
Car li cauteres est aide por finir les moistors:	 For the cautery is aid to finish off the tumors (or abscesses):
por ceu est il de plus grant aide as moistors.	 because it is of greater aid for tumors (or abscesses).
Ou il covient por l’estraction des arteres que om emplisse lou leu de viel coton et mette on sus tentes bien faites;	 For the extraction of arteries, one should fill the area with old cotton and place strong tents (bandages) above.
et quant on les desliera, si soit curez de medicines seches que font naistre char, et de tentes, tant qu’il soit sanez;	 And when they are dislodged (or dissected), they should be cured with dry medicines that cause a burn and bandages until they heal.
et se sans cort de l’artere tant dis com tu i oevres, si te haste dou coper par cautere, ou tu emple lou leu de vitriole et l’estrain a ta main que li sans soit estainchiez;	 And if you do not stop the flow from an artery as much as you can when dissecting (or operating), hurry to cover it with cautery or fill the area with vitriol and hold your hand so that it does not bleed.
et se tu n’as ceu present, si met sor le leu ton doit tant que li sans soit congelez, et arose le leu d’aigue froide tant que li sans cesse, et soit estraint si com il covient;	 And if you do not have it present (the dislocated joint), place the hand on the joint until the bone is frozen, and irrigate the joint with cold water continually, and hold it in place as necessary.
et ceu qui est muedre et plus legier en l’estraction de l’artere est que tu cauterizes la voinne de cest cautere trenchant de II pars, mais li trenchant soient bien espés por warder plus longement lor chalor.	 And the one that is more swollen and lighter in the extraction of the artery is that you cauterize the vein with this sharp cautery for two parts, but they should be well thickened to keep their heat longer.
Car quant li estrumens est trop tenves, si tient moins sa chalor.	For when the straw is too thin, it holds less heat.
Et doit avoir entre les II coutelz I doit de gros d’espaice, et puis quant tu as signiet d’enche les II leus, et tu mes lou fer ardant sus tant qu’il viegne jusc’a l’os, et cope la voinne en II leus;	 And there should be between the two blades of the instrument a thick space, and when you have positioned them on the two joints, and you press the iron hot upon it until it reaches the bone, and cut through the vein in two parts.
et soient esloigniet entre les II chiés car il n’est mie soudez de cest cautere dou tout en tout;	 And they should be separated between the two shoulders, because this cautery is not entirely soldered from one shoulder to the other.
et c’est li forme dou cautere:	 and this is the shape of the cautery:
des larmes	tears
Quant les larmes des eulz sont dessendans des voinnes que sont sus lou test dou chief de fuer, et il ne profite mie cure de medicine c’on i faice, et tu vois la faice dou malaide enrougir, et sent ou front ambulation si com de fremis;	 When the tears of the eyes flow out from veins that are above the head, and there is no benefit in treating with medicine as one does, you see the patient become agitated, and he feels his forehead tremble like a shudder.
et sui oil sont tenve et moiste si que li poil des papieres sont cheut, et sont eschaufees les papieres, et escorchies de l’ardor des larmes, si ait mestier de ceste cure.	 And if they are thin and moist, so that the hairs of the paper fall off, and the paper is scalded and scorched by the heat of the tears, this treatment is necessary.
Et l’apelerent li ancien «cure contuse», et est que tu faices a rere au malaide qui a ceste maladie les poilz qu’il ait ou front, puis li fai III fendures ou front igalment selonc la longesce dou front;	 And it was called by the ancients "contused cure", and you make incisions at the back of the patient who has this disease in his forehead, then make three cuts on the forehead equally according to its length.
