et soit l’une des fendures ausi com II doi tout emmi lou front en avalant aval jusc’a neif, et les autres II as II costelz par desus les papieres, et te garde de l’incision des arteres que sont as II costez par desus les papieres;	 And one of the openings should be similar to how the entire front is pushed down swallowing towards the neck, and the others are the two chests through the paper, and keep away from cutting the arteries that are near the two chests through the paper.
et aloigne ta main de la continuation des II mandibules, et soit chescune plaie la quantiteit de III dois au traver joins;	 and distance your hand from the connection of the two jaws, and let each wound be the amount of three joined fingers.
et aies apparillie une piece d’esponge et mout de drapelz ses por essuer lou sanc, puis boute le spatumile agut de II pars de coi ci est li forme:	 and prepare a piece of sponge and a lot of linen for washing the blood, then insert the sharp spatula of two parts as shown here.
des l’incision qui est dever la temple jusc’a la seconde incision;	 from the first incision at the temple to the second incision.
et escorche tout le keur qui est entre les II fendures a tot lou syfac qui est sus l’os, puis fai autreteil des la moiene incision jusc’a l’autre seconde, et puis estrai fuer cest spatumile.	 and scrape all the flesh that is between the two openings to the full extent of the siphac on the bone, then do something from the middle incision to the other second one, and then extract this spatula.
si boute en la premiere fendure l’estrument qui est apelez «cultellaire», et est tresbien trenchans d’une part, et d’autre part est souef, ne mie trenchans, et c’est li forme:	Insert into the first cut the instrument called "culter," which is very sharp on one side and soft, not sharp, on the other, and its shape is:
Et met le costeit taillant vers la char aerse au keur, et lou costeit souef vers l’os, et lou boute tant qu’il veigne a la moiene fendure.	 And make the cutting blade pointed towards the chest cavity, and the cut should be soft towards the bone, and push it until it comes to the midline incision.
Et cope toz les vasselz que dessendent dou chief as eulz tant que l’incision soit continue jusc’a ceu qui apert dou keur, et puis autreteil fai en la moiene fendure jusc’a l’autre defuer;	 And cut all the eyelashes that descend from the head with the incision continuing up to where it opens the cavity, and then do another cut in the middle incision up to the other cavity.
et puis estrai dou sanc igalment, et espresse lou leu por le sanc pris;	 And draw out equal amounts of blood, and press the place for blood taken.
puis met en chescune fendure une tente de viel coton, et met sus drapelz moilliez en vin et en oile et en aisil, et garde que apostemes chaus n’i veigne;	 then put a tent of old cotton in each incision, and put on damp cloths soaked in wine and oil and alum, and ensure that pus does not come into them.
et au tier jor deslie lou liien, et i amenistre grant planteit d’aigue tede, puis lou cure d’oignement basilicon avec oile roset, et d’autres cures dont on cure plaies, tant qu’il soit sanez.	 On the third day untie the stitch, and apply a large plant of cooled mustard, then the healing of basilicon ointment with rose oil, and other remedies for wounds, until it is healed.
dou reume des eulz	The root of the hairs
Quant a aucun vienent catarre agut acostumeement, et tu vois les eulz tenves et petis, et afoiblir la veue, et les papieres brulees;	 When any person comes with an acute catarrh, you see the eyes swollen and small, blurred vision, and burned-out paper.
et li poil chieent, et ou chief en parfont a dolor ague, et li malaides esternue;	 and the hair is falling out, and the head hurts with sharp pain, and the patient coughs.
adonques saiches par ces accidens que celles matieres et cil catharre ne vient fuer que de maintes voines, et li muedre cure que i est, si est ceste.	 Then understand by these signs that those matters and this catarrh do not come from any other place except from many veins, and the humors that cause it are those.
Et est que tu comande au malaide a rere son front, puis fai une grant fendure emmi lou front, et une autre dou large I poc.	 And you must tell the patient to recline their head, then make a large incision behind the head and another wide one at the back of the neck.
Et comence des la fendure de la temple senestre a la temple destre, et soit li incision jusc’a l’os;	 And begin from the hollow of the left temple to the right temple, and let the incision go up to the bone;
et esloigne ta main des ners des temples que muevent au mengier;	 and remove your hand from the nerves of the temples that move when eating;
et quant li os est descovers, si essue tout le sanc a une esponge, et puis desevre entre les II levres de la fendure et i met coton viel, et tentes de lin;	 and when the bone is exposed, suck all the blood with a sponge, then open between the two lips of the incision and put old cotton in there, and sew it with linen.
puis lie desus drapelz moilliez en vin et en oile, et te garde d’aposteme chaut;	 Then lay it on top of dampened cloths soaked in wine and oil, and beware of getting cold.
quant il est ostez, si covient que tu frottes l’os tant que chars i comence a naistre, puis le cure de choses exiccatives, que font enjanrer char.	 When it is removed, you must rub the bone until flesh begins to grow around it, then treat with things that promote healing and encourage growth of flesh.
En teil maniere:	 In this manner:
pren II parties de flor de froment, et de colofoine IIII parties, et en fai emplaustre;	 Take two parts of wheat flour and four parts of colophony, and make a plaster with them.
et l’aministre en ces plaies por enjanrer char per tout.	 And administer it on these wounds to heal thoroughly.
de l’estoupement des oreilles	Make a tube of silver or lead, narrow at one small opening and with a lid for distillation; use an instrument of lead well made for this purpose; if you wish to apply it, wrap a small rafer around the tip with cotton; pour your oil or juice, and any medicine of yours into the tube; place the tube in the ear; push the rafer into the cotton completely; press gently until the oil distills or overflows from the ear; heat the distillation with fire as one would distill it in the ear; ensure that it is not too cold, for the medicine will not be good.
Tout ceu que chiet ens oreilles est une des IIII choses:	 Everything that falls into ears is one of the four things:
ou grains, ou beste, ou piere de mine ou semblans chose si com fer;	 or grain, or animal, or stone from a mine, or similar objects like iron.
ou semence, si com jaisses, feves, pois;	 or seed, such as beans, peas, lentils;
ou chose defluans si com aigue et aisilz et semblans choses.	 For fluid flowing like water and syrups and similar things.
Quant il chiet en l’oreille piere ou autre maniere de chose que ne s’ajoste mie a l’oreille, ne ne croist en l’oreille, si met l’oreille au solel.	 When it falls into the ear bone (or any other way that does not align with the ear), does not fit in the ear, or does not grow within the ear, put the ear on a hot surface.
Se tu vois la piere, si distille aucun poc d’oile violet ou oile de sisament, puis i amenistre extraction;	 If you see the stone, if it releases a little drop of purple oil or castor oil, then apply extraction.
et lou fai esternuer de condisi, et li estoupe les narines quant li esternuemens vient, et met entor l’oreille pieces de drapelz ou laine;	 and make him vomit with powdered gum myrrh, and stop the nostrils when vomiting comes, and put around the ear pieces of cloth or wool.
et estent l’oreille au desus.	 raise the ear upward.
Mout de fois vient fuer par ceste cure;	 Many times flatulence occurs with this treatment;
et s’elle ne vient fuer, se li amenistre extraction as pinceures subtilz, de coi ci est li forme:	 And if it does not occur, apply extraction with fine tweezers in the following way:
S’elle saut fuer as pinceures, c’est boin;	 If it jumps out with tweezers, that is good;
se ceu non, si amenistre extraction a l’oncine subtil de petite doubleure;	 if not, apply extraction with the narrow and curved onion of small size.
et s’elle ne saut par ceu, si fai une caine d’arain et boute lou chief de la cainne ou pertuis de l’oreille fort, et estoupe ceu qui est entor la cainne de cire mole si que li vens n’i puisse entrer avec la cainne;	 If it doesn't jump by itself, make a canal of beeswax and push the head of the canal or ear trumpet deeply into the ear, and stop up the area around the canal with soft wax so that the vein cannot enter with the canal.
puis le trai fuer forment, car mout de fois vient fuer si com nos avons dit;	 Then draw it out carefully, as often it comes out forcefully as we have said.
et s’elle ne vient fuer en teil maniere, si prent glut de coi en prent les oisiaus, et met en som aucun estrument qui soit a point por ceu faire, et met un poc de coton entor;	 If it does not come out in that manner, take some kind of implement sharp at the tip and put a piece of cotton around it.
puis presse le glut sus la piere ou quel chose que ce soit, et trai fuer.	 Then press the instrument on the stone or whatever it is, and draw it out forcefully.
Et s’elle ne saut fuer de toutes ces choses que nos avons dit, si te haste de fendre l’oreille ainsois que aposteme chalz i veigne, et spasme;	 If it does not come out from all the things we have said, then quickly cut the ear in such a way that an abscess pus comes out and twitches.
et li maniere de la fendure si est que tu faices premier sainier lou malaide de la cephalique, et estrai dou sanc selonc la mesure de sa vertu, puis fai seoir lou malaide entre tes mains et li torne l’oreille au desus, et fent une petite fendure en la racine de l’oreille a la graisse ou leu dependant;	 And the manner of the incision is that you first let the patient drain his head, and draw blood according to the measure of its potency, then make the patient sit between your hands and turn his ear upward, and make a small incision in the root of the ear at the fat or the place it depends on;
et soit li fendure ausi com une lune, tant que tu viegnes a la piere, puis l’oste selonc ton pooir, et la suce hastanment a ta bouche;	 And let the incision be as a moon, until you reach the bone, then extract it according to your power, and suck it quickly with your mouth.
et la cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	 and the treatment until it is drained.
Et se c’est grains qui est ens et il enfle, si aministre extraction;	 And if it is a grain that fills and swells, administer extraction;
et si’il ne puet issir, si amenistre I spatumile tenve subtil selonc ceste forme:	 and if it cannot be extracted, then administer the thin subtle sponge according to this form:
et amenistre incision de celui grain.	 And make an incision of that grain (of the bone).
Mais ne faire mie ceu quant tu penses que li grains est moistes por la moistor de l’oreille, tant que tu en aies fait maintes pieces;	 But do not do this when you think that the grain is moist due to ear moisture, as long as you have made many pieces.
puis l’estrai as pinceures subtilz et au succier, si com nos avons dit, si que li estractions soit aligie.	 Then remove it with subtle tweezers and warm water, as we have said, so that the extraction is aligned.
En l’aigue donques que chiet en l’oreille covient que li malaides use d’esternuement de condisi premiers, et ample l’oreille de viel coton.	 In the ear, therefore, when water falls, it is necessary for the patient to use eardrops first and then stuff the ear with a large cotton ball.
Et soit gisans sus celle oreille meisme ou li aigue est.	 And let it lie on that same ear where the water is.
s’elle saut fuer per ceu, c’est boin.	 If it jumps out because of this, it's good.
se ceu non, si prent maintes pieres selonc li longesce de ton doit tenves et legieres, et les eschaufe un poc au feu;	 if it does not do this, take many small and light stones according to the thickness of your finger, and heat them a little in the fire.
et em mette li malaides une ou pertus de son oreille, et saille sus i. de ses piez d’autre part, et fiere d’une autre piere sus la piere qui est en l’oreille;	 and place the patient with an earache or abscess in it, and press on one side of it with your fingers from the other side, and push another stone on top of the stone that is in the ear.
et ne cesse de faire ceu de piere em piere tant que li aigue isse toute fuer, et ensi saut elle toute fuer;	 and do not stop doing this with one stone against another until it has completely drained out, and then it will burst out all at once.
et se tu vues, si prent I jonc, et boute l’un des chiés en l’oreille, et l’autre chief emprent de feu tant que li plus dou jonc soit ars;	 And if you see it, take the cord, and push one of the heads into the ear, and hold the other head in fire until the more tender part is burnt;
puis refai autreteil d’autres jons tant que li aigue isse toute, si com nos avons dit en la piere.	 then tie other cords for the rest of the burn as we have said before.
En l’estraction de la beste, s’elle est de petit cors, si com puce et semblans chose, cure la si com nos avons dit en la division;	 In the extraction of the beast, if it is small-bodied like a flea and similar things, treat it as we have said before in the classification.
mais s’elle est de grant cors c’on la puisse sentir, si amenistre extraction de pinceures;	 but if it has a large body that can be felt, bring instruments for extraction of tweezers;
et c’est li chose plus legiere a oster qui soit en l’oreille.	 and it is the easier thing to remove that which is in the ear.
En l’estraction des vers enjanrez as oreilles, quant tu lou cures si com nos avons dit en la division et ou traitier des distillations, et li cure ne profite mie, si covient que tu regardes l’oreille au soleil:	 In the removal of worms from the ears, when you treat it as we have said before and in the section on distillation, and the treatment does not help, then you must look at the ear in the sunlight.
s’il i apert nulz vers, si les trai as pinceures subtilz, et s’il n’aperent, si prent la cainne de coi ci est li forme:	 If there are any open wounds, take subtle forceps to them, and if they do not open, then take the cable from where this form is.
Et soit estroite desoz et large desus.	 And it should be narrow below and wide above.
Et boute lou plus subtil chief en l’oreille selonc la quantiteit de la soffrance dou malaide, puis succe forment a tot la caine;	 And push the more subtle head into the ear according to the amount of pain the patient has, then pull on the entire cable.
fai ceu sovent tant que tuit li ver issent.	 Do this often until all the worms come out.
Et s’il n’obeissent a issir, si estoupe entor la cainne de coton si com j’ai dit en la piere;	 And if they do not obey and come out, stop up the cable with cotton as I said in the previous section.
et s’il ne saillent fuer si com nos avons dit, si aministre distillations que li ancien ont esprovees en l’ocision des vers, et tu les troveras ou traitier des distillations;	 And if they do not come out as we have said, administer distillations that the ancients have proven to be effective in expelling worms, and you will find where to prepare distillations.
et si distille tes oiles et tes medicines en l’oreille a tout cest estrument, de coi ci est li forme si com tu vois:	 And if you pour oil and medicine into the ear with this instrument, it takes this form as you see:
Et soit d’argent ou d’arain estrois desoz a I petis pertuis, et desus overs por distiller;	 Silver or bronze is hollowed out beneath the small holes, and covered with a lid for pouring.
et por presser dedens la distillation a I estrument d’arain bien fait por ceu, et se tu vues pren I raseur et envoloupe entor la pointe avenanment coton;	 and to press from inside the distillation with an iron instrument well made for this purpose, and if you wish, take a scraper and wrap it around the tip with cotton;
puis i giete ton oile ou ton jus, et ceu que tu vues de tes medicines en la cainne, et li caine soit en l’oreille;	 Then pour your oil or juice, and whatever medicine you wish into the tube, and place the tube in the ear.
puis boute dedens lou raseur a tout lou coton, et presse ta main tempreement tant que li oile soit distilleit ou chevement de l’oreille;	 Then push the scraper with all the cotton into it and press your hand gently until the oil is distilled or the ear canal becomes clear.
et lou sente li malaides dedens, et soit li distillations I poc eschaufee au feu ainsois c’on la distille en l’oreille;	 And the patient feels pain inside, and if it is an abscess, heat it with fire in the same way as one distills it in the ear;
et garde qu’elle ne soit trop froide, car li medicine ne seroit mie si bone.	 And keep that it is not too cold, for the medicine will not be good.
de l’estoupement des oreilles	Make a tube of silver or lead, narrow at one small opening and with a lid for distillation; use an instrument of lead well made for this purpose; if you wish to apply it, wrap a small rafer around the tip with cotton; pour your oil or juice, and any medicine of yours into the tube; place the tube in the ear; push the rafer into the cotton completely; press gently until the oil distills or overflows from the ear; heat the distillation with fire as one would distill it in the ear; ensure that it is not too cold, for the medicine will not be good.
Aucun enfant naissent qui n’ont nul pertus ens oreilles;	 No child is born without some deformity in ears;
et ceste meisme chose avient as homes par estoupement de plaie, ou de char nee dedens l’oreille, et cist estoupemens vient aucune fois em parfont en l’oreille, si c’on ne lou puet veoir;	 And the same thing happens in men by discharge from a wound or pus born inside the ear, and this discharge sometimes goes all the way into the ear, if one cannot see it;
et aucune fois avient I poc defuer lou pertus, et lou voit om bien.	 And sometimes the deformity disappears by itself, and one sees it well.
Celle donques que vient em parfont, si c’on ne la puet veoir, est de grief sanation em plusors dispositions, et en cele c’on voit covient que tu mettes l’oreille dou malaide au soleil;	 Therefore, if it goes all the way in and one cannot see it, it is a difficult cure in many situations, and in this case you must put the sick person's ear in the sun;
et regarde dedens:	 And look within:
se tu vois l’opilation apparent, si la oevre a tot cest spatumile de coi ci est li forme:	 If you see the eruption (abscess) apparent, then use this spatula of this form:
Et soit agus et trenchans devant et derrier tout plain, si qu’il ne blece l’oreille;	 And be sharp and pointed at both ends, so that it does not puncture the ear;
se li opilation est de char nee ou cors de l’oreille, si la tien as pinceures subtilz, et la cope legierement, tant que celle chars soit toute ostee.	 If the eruption is of flesh or bone from the ear, then take fine tweezers and gently remove it until all the char (pus) is gone.
Et se li opilations est em parfont en l’oreille, si pren I raseur subtil legier et l’eschaufe un petit au feu, puis li met ou cors de l’oreille.	 And if the opilation (a foreign body) is completely in the ear, take a fine razor and heat it slightly with fire, then put it in the ear canal.
Se tu sens l’opilation dont li malaides sent grieteit a l’oïr, perce legierement, et garde que tu ne grever les ners de l’oreille;	 If you feel the eruption that causes pain in the ear, make a small incision gently, but be careful not to injure the nerves of the ear;
puis met en l’oreille une tente selonc la largesce dou pertus, et la moille en l’oignement egyptien.	 Then place a wick (tampon) in the ear according to the size of the opening and moisten it with Egyptian ointment.
Fai ceu aucun jor tant que li plaie soit soudee, ou tu pren une tente et la moille en aigue rose, et poudre sus vitriole broiet;	 Make a poultice every day until the wound heals, and take a cloth and soak it in sharp vinegar, and powdered vitriol ground upon it.
et se tu vois enflee l’oreille, si couvient que tu traies la tente et remue une autre tente moillie en cerote qui soit fait d’oile roset et de cire, tant que li enfleure soit ostee;	 And if you see an abscess on the ear, then you must draw out the pus and apply another cloth moistened with a salve made of rose oil and beeswax until the abscess is removed.
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	 then let it heal.
Et se decorremens de sanc vient, si plonge une esponge et drapelz en aigue froide, et le met sus l’oreille, et use d’autres cures qui oste lou decorrement de sanc qui sont ou traitier des destillations.	If there comes discharge of blood, dip a sponge and cloth in cold water, and place it on the ear, and use other treatments that stop the blood discharge which are either distillations or cauterization.
de la char des papieres	of paper pulp
Cist althelul que vienent em papieres des eulz quant ils sont moiste et sont sec, si covient que tu les estendes de tenailles et de pinceures, et le cope d’un spatumile de ses racines;	 This is an aphorism that comes in papers about eyes when they are moist and dry; you must stretch them with tongs and tweezers and cut the roots with a spatula.
puis met sor le leu vitriole broiet.	 then apply powdered vitriol to it.
Et se sans en decort, si le cauterize dou cautere lenticulaire subtil, et li cauterizeir aprés l’incision vaut mues;	 And if, without cutting, they burn with the slow cautery called lenticular, then they should be burned after incision is worthwhile.
et maintes fois repairent, cant aucune chose demoure de lor racines;	 and repeatedly repair themselves, no matter what is rooted there;
et quant elles sont cauterizees par feu, si sont arses celles racines et ne revienent mie.	 and when they are burned by fire, those roots are consumed and do not return.
de la gresle	from the hailstone
Maintes fois vienent em papieres des eulz unes choses que semblent gresle en sa forme et en sa duresce, et por ceu est ceste maladie apelee «grandine», et est une assemblee de moistor grosse en la papiere desus et desoz;	 Many times come out of the eyes something that resembles hail in shape and hardness, and because of this, this disease is called "hail," and it is a collection of thick moisture on the paper above and below.
li ovraiges est telz:	 The remedies are as follows:
pren warde se li grandine se muet d’une part et d’autre, et c’est legiere chose a savoir;	 Take care if hail mutes from both sides, it is an easy thing to know.
fent la donques dou large, puis l’escorche de chescune partie legierement, puis la prent as pinceures, et la cope.	 Then pull it open widely, then scrape each side lightly with a knife, then take hold of it with the pliers and crush it.
se tu ne la pues coper sens percier un poc la papiere, si ne grieve rien au malaide;	 if you cannot crush it without piercing the paper slightly, do not worry the patient at all.
et se li fendure est grans, si l’assemble a une costure, et la cure tant qu’ele soit sanee;	 and if the wound is large, gather it together with stitches, and heal it until it is healed.
et s’elle est petite, si n’i faire point de force, car li oignemens la restoure tantost et enjanre char.	 and if it is small, do not apply force, because the ointment will heal it soon enough and prevent scarring.
Et se li grandine est dessendans au dedens de l’oreille vers la partie desus, si enverse la papiere, et estent la grandine a unes pinceures, et la cope et presse d’une part et d’autre;	 If the hail is descending inside the ear towards the upper part, turn the paper, take hold of it with pliers, and crush and press it from both sides.
et se li papiere est esloignie par l’incision, ce ne grieve rien;	 If the paper is dislocated by incision, it causes no harm.
et quant li grandine est copee, si leive l’oil d’aigue salee, et cure le leu de ceu qui enjanre char tant que li malaides soit sanez.	 And when hail is hit, apply oil of salty water, and heal the wound of those who suffer from frostbite until the patient is healed.
de la graisse des eulz	of the fat of the hails
Exinach est une graisse qui est enjanree en toiles des papieres desus, et ce avient plus as enfans c’a nules gens, et grieve mout a lor eulz, et li vienent li catharre as matinees, et ne pueent regardeir la lumiere dou soleil por ceu que les larmes se hastent a lor eulz;	 Exinach is a grease that adheres to the papers above, and it happens more often in children than in adults, and causes much discomfort to their eyes, and they come down with catarrh at dawn, and cannot endure the light of the sun because tears hasten towards their eyes.
et por ceu se couchent il sor lor faices adés, et dorment sus, et sont lor papieres desoz lor sorcilz moistes que li enfleure et li apparance ont covert de l’exinach qui apert en l’oil.	 And because of this, they lie on their faces immediately and sleep above it, and their papers are damp under their eyelids that the exinach penetrates through the oil.
Et quant tu presses lou leu a tes dois et sent l’exirnach entr’ous.	 And when you press the joint with your fingers and feel the exit between them.
Et li maniere de l’ovraige si est que li malaides mette son chief en ton sain;	 And the manner of the work is that the patient places their head on your hand;
et puis pren I drapeil de lin, et appareille une tente em maniere d’un cercle selonc la quantiteit que conteigne exirnach de chescune partie, puis le met sus li;	 Then take a linen cloth and prepare a tent in the shape of a circle according to the size that can contain scorching from each part, then place it on top of it;
et presse a tes dois d’une part et d’autre, si que li exirnach soit assemblez emmi le cercle;	 and press your hands together from both sides, so that the scorching is assembled within the circle;
puis fent em mileu de la moistor au spatumile trenchant une fendure dou large, et ne soit mie plus grans que li plaie c’on fait a la sainie de voinne;	 then make a hole in the middle of the moisture using the spatula with a cut through wide, but not larger than the wound made in opening a vein;
et fent le cuir em parfont tant que tu veignes a l’exirnach;	 and cut the skin all the way to where you see the scorching;
et em plusors dispositions vient exirnach de la fendure, selonc la forme d’une piece de graisse blainche.	 And in various positions, scorching comes out of the hole, in the form of a piece of white fat.
Estrai la donques a tout une piece de drap charpit entre tes dois au defuer, et torne ta main a destre et a senestre tant qu’il soit espars;	 Pull then a small piece of sharp cloth between your hands at the fold, and turn your hand left and right until it is dispersed;
et garde que tu n’ajoster en la fendure, que tu ne viegnes a tout le spatumile jusc’a l’oil, que tu ne le bleces.	 and make sure not to miss in the crack, that you do not come too close to the spurtulum until the oil, that you do not pierce it.
Et se li exirnach n’apert en l’encomencement de la fendure, si acroi un poc la fendure legierement tant qu’il apere;	 And if the incision does not open at the beginning of the crack, raise the crack slightly so it appears.
puis l’estrai si com nos avons dit, puis moille drapelz en aisil et en aigue, et met sus le leu, et estrain de bendelz.	 then draw as we have said, then wet cloths in oil and vinegar, and place it on the area, and press with bandages.
Et si a de tels homes qui broient seil et mettent sus por corrompre cele moistor qui est demoree.	 And for such men who break whey and place it on top to corrupt the moisture that remains.
Puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	 Then heal him until he is healthy.
Et s’il vient au leu aposteme chaut, si lou cure d’emplaustres assouajant tant qu’il soit sanez.	 If the joint becomes an abscess that is hot, then heal it with poultices soothing until it is healthy.
des poilz des papieres	hairs of paper
Quant em papieres naissent poilz ajostez autre que li naturez, et sont enveillit, si nuisent as eulz, et font venir manieres de maladies si com larmes acostumees et mollifications des papieres et albugine, tant que c’est cause de la destruction des eulz;	 When paper growths hair artificially (other than nature), and is nurtured, it harms the eyes, and brings on maladies such as watery eyes, and softening of the paper, and cloudiness, all of which causes the destruction of the eyes.
et est li cure selonc IIII manieres:	 And the care is according to four ways:
ou par cautere ensamble feu, ou par medicine ague selonc ceu qu’il est devant ou chapistre de cautere, et est fais ou par incision et costure ou par caines, selonc ceu que je dirai.	 or by cautery with fire, or by medicinal poultice as described in the previous chapter on cautery, and it is done either by incision and stitching or by cantharides, as I shall say.
Il covient que tu mettes lou chief dou malaide en ton sain, puis torne la papiere de l’oil a ta main senestre;	 You must place the head of the patient in your lap, then turn the paper of the oil in your left hand;
s’elle est convertie, c’est boin;	 if it is turned over, that is good;
se ceu non, si i boute une aguille a tout I fil desus;	 if not, push a needle through all the way on top of it;
et soit ce delez la marge de la papiere ou li poil naissent delez ces poilz, et trai I fil au desus a tout la papiere, et la torne au raseur;	 and pull out the thread from the edge of the paper where the hairs grow under these hairs, and draw the thread up to the top of the paper, and turn it over with the razor;
puis fent en la partie desoz la papiere, desoz les poilz ajostez, a tout le spatumile copant, des le grant larmier jusc’au petit;	 Then they make an incision in the area below the paper, below the hairs, spreading all over with a spatula, from the large tear until the small one.
puis estrai I fil, et met desoz la papiere une petite tente de couton et de drapeil, puis seigne sus la papiere une figure d’enche, si com la fuelle de mirte, et toutevoie il covient que li figure soit selonc la quantiteit que tu vues eslever la papiere qui est devisez a toz.	 Then draw the thread, and put a small tent of cotton and linen under the paper, then make a mark on the paper in the shape of an anchor, just as the mirte thorn, and it is necessary that the figure should be according to the amount you intend to raise the paper, which is designated for all.
Et si a teil qui a mestier c’on cope grant quantiteit de la papiere selonc ceu que li papiere est mollifie;	 And if it is necessary to cut a large amount of paper according to the softness of the paper.
puis fent a tout le spatumile sus les II lignes que tu as signiet, et comence des lou grant larmier jusc’a petit;	 Then spread all over with the spatula on both lines that you have marked, and start from the large tear until the small one.
et soit li une des fendures pres des poilz naturez en la groissece d’un raiz, puis boute l’oncine en l’un des II angles dou keur, puis l’escorche toute;	 And let one of the openings near the natural hairs be by the root, then push the onion into one of the two angles of the wound, then peel off all the skin.
puis assemble les II levres a une costure d’une aguille a tout I fil de laine subtil, et essue le sanc, et fai aerdre la superfluiteit des filz sus les II sorcilz a tout aucunes choses gluans, se tu vues faire ce;	 Then bring the two lips together with a stitch of a needle and all the woolen thread, squeeze out the blood, and remove any superfluous threads on the two scissors to anything sticking, if you wish to do so.
et se ce non, si n’en aies cure, puis laisse la costure et les filz jusc’a III jors ou IIII;	 And if this is not done, then leave the stitch and the threads for three or four days;
puis cure la plaie sens costure de choses sechans et constrignans, car li papiere se relive au soudement de la plaie et l’assemblement de li, mais li costure est muedre (si com dirent li ancien), et c’est ovraiges sens paor;	 then heal the wound without stitching with dry and binding things because paper revives at the edge of the wound and the assembly of it, but the stitch is spoiled (as they say of the ancients), and this is a work without fear.
et si a une autre maniere:	 And another way:
et est que tu seignes la papiere d’une figure qui soit ausi com li fuelle de mirte, si com nos avons conteit, a III oncines desevrez selonc la forme qui est ci:	 and you make the paper of a figure that is like the fennel stalk, as we have said, three times perforate according to the form that is here:
puis cope ceu qui sormonte as petites forces igalment selonc la forme qui est ci:	then make it even on top of the small powers according to the following form:
Et se tu n’as pooir de tenir les tenailles, et li chose n’est mie igalz, si prent une aguille ou il ait I fil, et la boute emmi la figure;	 and if you are unable to hold the pliers and the thing is not even, take a needle with thread, and push it through the figure:
et boute I autre fil delez lou grant larmier, et lou secont fil delez lou petit, et assemble entre tes dois les filz igalment;	 and push the other thread out of the large hole, and the second thread out of the small one, and equally assemble the threads between your fingers:
puis lieve ta main igalment, et lieve tout le cuir sus coi tu as signiet, si com nos avons conteit, puis assemble les II levres de la plaie par costure, et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	 then straighten your hand equally, and lift all the skin as you have signed, as we have said, then sew together the two lips of the wound with stitching, and heal it until it is healthy:
et se aposteme vient a ton incision, si l’apaise de cerote et de semblans oignement assouajans;	 And if an abscess comes to your incision, soothe it with wax and similar calming ointments.
et aucune fois avient que li poil de la papiere sont convertit:	 Sometimes the hair of the head is converted:
si covient que tu uses ceu que nos avons dit de l’incision;	 it is necessary that you use what we have said about incising.
mais li costure en l’une et en l’autre est plus artificialz.	 but stitching in one or the other is more artificial.
Li cure des caines si est selonc ceste forme:	 The cure for dogs is as follows:
et est que tu convertisses la papiere et la fent dedens selonc ceu que j’ai dit, et puis fai II caines par art, et II liiens subtilz ausi lonc com li papiere et li largesce dou spatumile est;	 and you convert the head and make it inside as I have said, then make two dogs from craft, and two thin threads of the same length as the head and the width of a feather.
et cope as II chiés de II pars ou tu tiens les filz;	 and tie up the heads of the two parts where you hold the threads.
puis assemble l’un et l’autre subtilment sus ceu que sormonte de la papiere de l’oil, et estrain les II cainnes des II parties forment;	 then assemble one and the other skillfully above that which covers the head of oil, and hold the two dogs formed by the parts.
et le laisse ensi aucuns jors, et li cuir qui iert estrainte morra et nercira et porrira, tant qu’il cherra par lui.	 And leave it so for some days; the skin that is being stretched will die and rot, as long as it festers through it.
S’il tarde, si le cope a unes forces, puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	 If it lasts too long or if it becomes inflamed again, heal it until it is healed.
et quant li plaie iert soudee, et si ert levee li papiere, et ne poindront plus li poil;	 And when the wound is stitched up and the paper is raised, the hairs will no longer grow.
et c’est li forme des II cainnes que tu feras selonc ceste figure, et selonc ceste quantiteit de lonc et de large:	 This is the form of the two canes that you will make according to this figure and according to this length and width:
li ovraiges est telz que tu preignes une aguille subtil, et i boute I fil de soie souef et subtil;	 The work is as follows: take a fine needle and insert the silk thread into it.
puis assemble les chiés et noe l’un et l’autre subtilment, et soit li longesce des filz une palme de lonc;	 Then connect the heads together delicately and each other finely, and let the length of the threads be a palm in length.
puis ordene en la chasse I autre fil subtil de soie briément, et noe les chief dou fil;	 Then order a fine thread of silk, short, and knot its ends.
puis mette li malaides son chief en ton sain;	 Then place the patient's head on your lap.
et soit delez lou soleil si que li ovraiges soit declairiez, car c’est uns ovraiges subtilz et menus, puis boute l’aguille a tout la chasse en la racine dou poil ajosteit, et la fai percier en la papiere hastanment tant que tu la traies desus lou poil natureil;	 And let the patient's head be exposed to the sun so that the work may be clear, for this is a subtle and delicate work. Then place the needle at the entire length of the thread next to the hair root, and make it pierce the skin quickly through the natural hair as much as you can pull it over.
puis estrai le poil jusque sus la chasse, et boute en la chasse celui poil, s’il en i a I ou II ou III ou plusors;	 Then pull out the hair up to the thread, and insert the thread into the hair, if there is one or two or three or more.
puis estrai ta main tant que li poilz veigne fuers a tout la chasse en la papiere avec lou poil natureil.	 Then pull your hand until the hairs come out through the thread with the natural hair to the skin.
Et se li chasse est traite et li poilz ne vient fuer avec li, si trairas la chasse au desoz a tout le fil que tu i as ordeneit, tant que li chasse veigne fuer dou pertus desus et que tu la voies par la vision de l’oil;	 And if the shoulder is dislocated and the hairs do not come out with it, you will draw the dislocation under all the thread that you have ordered, as long as the dislocation comes out of the hole above and you see it through the oil's vision.
adonques si trairas la chasse et le fil, et clo l’oil et lou laisse clo II jors ou III, tant que li poil s’aerde en son leu et naisse li char sus;	 then you will draw the dislocation and the thread, close the oil and leave it closed for two or three days, until the hairs grow in their place and a blister grows over them.
et se li poilz est petis, si acompaigne I poil lonc des chevoulz naturez, et soit alevez avec celui ou tu le laisse, tant qu’il soit eslongiez et puis le lieve.	 and if the hairs are small, let them grow with long hair from nature, and boil it with what you leave, until it is stretched out and then strain it.
de la porriture de l’oil	of the corruption of oil
Quant ceste maladie qui est apelee «aleacrati» ou li porriture vient en l’oil, si en i a de II manieres:	 When this disease called "alecrat" or "porriture" comes in the oil, it happens in two ways:
l’une natureil, et l’autre innatureil.	 One natural, and the other unnatural.
Et avient par soudement de plaie, ou de tailleure ou de cautere, et par semblans choses.	 And it happens suddenly due to a wound, or by cutting, or by similar things.
Et li maniere de l’ovraige en li est que tu fendes celle soudure, et dessevre les levres de li, et met dedens tentes de lin, et la lie tant qu’elle soit sanee;	 And the method of work is that you cut through the joint, separate the sides of it, put threads of linen inside it, and tie it until it heals.
et ne covient mie que tu uses en la cure de li de choses que sechent et restraignent.	 And you must not use in the treatment of it things that dry and restrict.
Car se tu fais ceu, si revient li maladie pire que li premiere;	 For if you do this, the disease returns worse than the first.
mais i oevre de choses amollissans, si com fenugreic;	 But work with things softening, such as fenugreek;
et l’arose d’aigue ou altee et semence de lin soient cuites, et oignemens dyaquilon fondut en aucun des oiles, et i envoloupe une tente, et le cure de ceu.	 and the arsenic of water or salt, and linseed cooked, and dittany root boiled in any oil, and wrap it in a linen cloth, and treat it with these.
Et li tresors de ta cure si est que tu te dones en garde qu’ele ne soude mie selonc la forme qu’elle fut devant;	 And the treasures of your care are such that you must be cautious not to suture it as it was before;
et cist ovraiges que nos avons dit nen est fuers que adresemens de ceste maladie, qu’elle ne reviegne selonc la forme qu’elle fut devant.	 And this task that we have said is not useful unless adjustment of this disease, so that it does not recur as it was before.
de la char qui vient en l’oil	the pus that comes in oil
Ceste maladie que est desoz qui vraiement est apelee «axacrati», et est naturelz et accidens.	 This disease which is truly called "axacrati", and is natural and accidental.
Li accidens vient de plaie et de fendure et de cautere et de choses semblans;	 The accidents come from wounds and cuts and cauterizations and similar things;
et li voie de l’ovraige en li si est que tu preignes un aguille, en coi il ait I fil double, et la fiche en la char, et li fai percier des le senestre larmier tant c’a destre, si que li filz veigne en II chiés de la char;	 and the procedure in this task is that you take a needle with double thread, and pierce it through the flesh, from the left eyebrow to the right, so that the threads come out into two eyes of the flesh;
puis estent la char au desus a tout l’aguille, et la cope a I spatumile large.	 then pull the flesh up to the needle and hold with a broad spatula.
Et se li figure de la papiere revient selonc ceu qu’il covient, c’est boin;	 And if the shoulder figure returns as it should, it is good;
se ceu non, si pren I raseur et le met en la fendure, et torne la papiere, et fent II fendures ou costeit dedens la papiere;	 If not, take the rasp and put it in the gap, and turn the shoulder, and make two holes on the inside of the shoulder.
et soient li chiés des II fendures des II angles de l’incision que tu as copeit, et soit fais uns angles si que quant elles sont assemblees, que li figure soit ausi com li figure d’une lettre qui a non «I griesche»;	 and the heads of the two holes from the two corners of the incision that you made, should be made at an angle so that when they are assembled, the shoulder figure will be like the figure of a letter which has the name "Greek".
puis oste celle char, selonc la quantiteit que ses costez est agus desoz, de ceu qui enseut la papiere, puis ajoste les II parties desevrees, et les cout d’un fil de lainne;	 then remove that cartilage, according to the thickness of its sides, from what was previously the shoulder, then join the two separated parts with a thread of linen.
puis lou cure de ceu que nos avons dit des medicines mollifians, et de tentes, tant qu’il soit sanez.	 then let it heal according to what we have said about softening medicines and bandages until it is healed.
Et se li maladie vient de fendure ou de costure ou de cautere, si covient que tu fendes une fendure plainne desoz les poilz des papieres, et selonc ceu qui est ci devant;	 And if the patient comes from a cut or stitch or cautery, then you must make a deep incision beneath the hairs of the affected area, as described before.
puis desevre entre les II leivres d’une tente, si com j’ai dit;	 Then sew together the two sides of an opening, as I have said.
et doit on faire l’ovraige selonc la forme de la maladie, car elle est mout diverse en forme, et li saiges maistres appareille engien de tout som pooir coment il faice revenir la figure a sa forme natureil;	 and the work should be done according to the shape of the disease, for it is very varied in shape, and wise masters prepare tools with all their power to restore the figure to its natural form.
et li malaides meisme, selonc ceu qu’il i covient d’ovraige et d’estrumens em plusors dispositions.	 and the patients themselves, according to what work and instruments are needed in various positions.
dou soudement de la papiere	quickly of the paper
Quant ceste soudure avient a mains homes en teil maniere que li papiere desus est sodee avec le blanc de l’oil, et ne puet movoir ne faire ses ovraiges naturez, si covient donques que tu i boutes la pointe d’un raseur desoz la papiere, et la lieve en haut;	 When the suturing occurs in such a way that the paper above is sewn with the white of the oil and cannot move or perform its natural functions, then you must insert the tip of a knife beneath the paper and lift it up.
et l’estent as pinceures, tant que tu copes ceu qui est aert au spatumile subtil, qui ne soit mie trop agus ne trop trenchans, si que li malaides ne puisse soffrir que li spatumile trop agus ne blecent l’oil;	 And the extension is with forceps, as long as you grip what is at the end of the subtle spoon, which should not be too sharp nor too pointed, so that the patient does not suffer from the sharp spoon and harm the eye.
et soit ton incision, dont tu escorche celle assemblee, legierement, si que li papiere reviegne selonc sa forme natureil;	 And your incision, from where you peel off that assembly, should be light so that the skin returns according to its natural form.
et est sanee toute celle assemblee, et font aucune fois en l’oil aigue salee, et le leve d’aigue douce, et de coliere;	 And the entire assembly is healed, and once in acute oil it becomes infected, and from acute sweet milk and pus.
puis met entre la papiere et l’oil une tente de lin, et met sus l’oil laine moillie en abun d’uef;	 Then put a flax tent between the skin and oil, and place above the oil wool soaked in abundance of egg.
et aprés le tier jor use dou coliere et des choses soudans tant qu’il soit sanez.	 And on the third day use pus and things that harden until it is healed.
de l’ungle de l’oil	the tip of a razor blade
Saiches que li ungle est selonc II manieres:	 Know that the nail has two kinds:
elle est nervouse et semblans a I dur syfac, et une autre qui n’est mie nervouse, mais est semblans a blainche moistor congelee, que quant on la touche de fer et on la cuide panre as pinceures, si ne puet om;	 it is nerve-like and resembles hard soap, and another which is not nerve-like but resembles white moisture that has frozen, which when touched with iron and cooked in the tongs cannot be hammered.
et l’une et l’autre semblance encomence devers le grant larmier, et croist poc et poc tant qu’ele cuevre toute la veue et toute la lumiere et le movement de l’oil.	 and both grow towards the large ulcer, and gradually increase until it covers the entire eye and all light and oil movement.
Et li maniere de l’incision si est que li malaides mette son chief en ton sain, puis li oevre les eulz;	 And the method of incision is that the patient places his head on a clean surface, then opens the eyes.
et lieve la papiere a ta main, puis coil l’ungle as pinceures de petite doubleure, et l’estent au desus;	 and lift the paper with your hand, then hold the nail in the tongs of small jaws, and place it above.
puis pren une aguille, et i met I poil de cheval, ou de vaiche, ou de buef, et I fil fort;	 Then take a needle, and put horse hair or ox hair, or strong thread on it.
et double la pointe de l’aguille un poc et la fiche emmi l’ungle, et la perce a tout l’aguille, et lie l’ungle d’un fil et l’estent au desus, et escorche a tout lou poil le costeit de l’ungle qui enseut la prunele et la soie au poil jusc’au chief, puis cope lou remanant en la racine dou larmier a tout lou spatumile subtil et as petites forces, et laisse la char natureil ou larmier, si que par l’incision ne veigne li cors des larmes acostumeement;	 and bend the tip of the needle slightly and push it into the nail, and pierce through with the whole needle, tie the nail with thread and stretch it above, and shave all the skin surrounding the nail, from the root to the nail bed, down to the cuticle and silk, then grind the rest at the root of the armpit with a fine spatula and small forceps, leaving the natural flesh or skin, so that through the incision no sweat comes out normally.
et aucune fois s’estent li ungle a l’oncine soulement, et au fil, si com nos avons dit;	 and sometimes the nail grows into the curve only, and with thread, as we have said.
puis l’escorche on a tout le spatumile souef de coi ci est li forme:	 Then scrape off all the soft putty-like substance that is in this shape: [the original shape was not given, so the translation assumes that the context makes it clear what is meant by "this shape"]
Et garde que li spatumile ne touche la toile charnue et la rompe, et que li prunele ne soit percie;	 And ensure that the soft putty-like substance does not touch the soft flesh and break it, and that the skin is not pierced.
et aprés l’incision giete en l’oil un poc de seil broiet, et dou coliere fait de litargire, et le laisse jusc’a l’autre jor;	 And after the incision pour oil a little bit of boiled egg white is poured, and let the lidarge solution remain until the next day.
puis le cure de ceu qu’il i covient tant qu’il soit sanez.	 Then treat that which is necessary until it heals.
Et se li ungle n’est mie nervouse, et tu ne pues bouter l’aguille, et li uncines n’i puet entrer, maintes fois est curee ceste semblance d’ungle de medicines;	 And if the nail is not nerve-filled and you cannot push the needle, and the unguent cannot enter, this type of nail is often treated with medicine.
et naissent sicom j’ai conteit en la division, et se tu la vues coper, si oevre l’oil dou malaide, et pren le spatumile legier poc agut selonc ceste forme:	 And if they grow as I have mentioned in the section on this topic, and you see it covered, then open the oil from the patient, and take a small amount of soft putty-like substance according to this shape.
Et reis l’ungle desus subtilment, et se tu vois qu’elle amenuise point et li rasion i apresse, si distille de ta bouche en l’oil coliere fait de litargire et dou coliere rouge et seil broiet, et estoupe l’oil jusc’a l’autre jor;	 And scrape the nail above gently, and if you see that it does not soften at all and the reason is pursued, distill from your mouth into the collyrium oil made of litargyre and red collyrium powder and apply the oil until the next day.
puis rencomence l’autre ovraige selonc ceste meisme oevre, tant qu’elle soit toute ostee.	 Then proceed with the other work according to this same method, until it is completely dislodged.
Se aucune chose ne t’est contraire en l’oil, si com aposteme chaus, adonques la lait, et cure premier l’aposteme chaut tant qu’il soit sanez, puis rencomence l’ovraige si com devant, tant qu’il soit sanez.	If nothing contradicts in the oil, as in an abscess, then milk it, and first treat the abscess with heat until it is healthy, then continue the work as before, until it is healed.
Et se li apparance de la chair dou larmier nuit en l’oil par grant nuisement, si la sospent a l’oncine, et en cope une partie et non mie tot, que cors de larmes n’i viegne;	 And if the appearance of the skin around the nail harms the oil greatly, suspend it at the onion, and cut a small part of it and not too much, so that no tears come.
puis distille en l’oil coliere rouge qui est fais de litargire.	 Then distill into the red collyrium oil made of litargyre.
de la char qui naist sus la prunelle	of the flesh which grows over the eyelid
Es eulz d’aucuns homes naist aucune fois char rouge, et cuevre la prunele et restraint sus les papieres et les torne au defuer, et semble une rose de balauste;	 In some men, a red spot sometimes arises, cover the prunelle (anterior chamber of the eye) and hold it with paper and turn it towards the duct, and it looks like a boxwood rose.
et li ovraiges si est que li malaides mette son chief en ton sain, puis li oevre les eulz, et coil toute celle char as uncines convenaubles a ceu, et la sostien a la force;	 And the operation is that the patient places his head on your lap, then he works the eyes, and therefore all that skin around the area should be shaved suitable for this purpose, and hold it with strength.
puis cope la premiere char, et vai tout copant au raseur jusc’a la fin, et te garde que tu ne bleces l’oil a l’ovraige;	 Then take the first piece (of skin) and go all the way shaving to the end, and be careful not to cut the eye during the operation.
et soit li incision dou spatumile que nos avons dit en l’incision de l’ungle et as petites forces de coi on oste lou sebel, si com li forme aprés cest chapistre lou demostre;	 and make the incision with a spathamel (a type of blade) as we have said in the incision of the nail and the small forces of which one separates the skin, as the form after this chapter demonstrates.
et quant li incision est acomplie et ostee toute li char, si emple l’oil de seil broiet ou tu i distille coliere rouge et semblans medicines corrosives, et met sus l’oil defuer coton avec abin d’uef, si qu’il soit asseurez d’aposteme chaut;	 and when the incision is completed and all the skin is removed, apply the oil of oil (liniment) ground or you distill red collyrium and similar corrosive medicines, and put it on top of cotton with egg white, so that it is secure from infection.
et s’il i demore rien, et li sans chaus te sormonte, et tu doutes aposteme chaut, si laisse l’oil et cure l’aposteme de choses apaisant aposteme chaut;	 And if there remains something and the wound is deep, and you doubt about the abscess being hot, then leave the oil and treat the abscess with cooling substances.
puis revien a ton ovraige tant qu’il soit sanez, et ensi fai cant chars est ajostee en l’oil par ceste semblance.	 Then return to your work when it is healed, and thus do as charms are anointed with oil in this manner.
Mais toutevoie il covient que tu aliges la cure de chescun oil foible de la voie natureil;	 But it is necessary that you make the treatment of each oil weak through natural ways.
et de la voie accident, en ovraige de fer;	 and by accidental means, in work with iron.
et ne bouter mie ta main en aucun de ces ovraiges tant que tu voies que cist membres soit soffrans celui ovraige.	 And do not put your hand in any of these works until you see that this member is soft for this work.
des voines des eulz	veins of the eyes
Sebel sont voinnes rouges que sont covertes sus l’oil, et tolent a la veue son ovraige et afoiblissent l’oil toz jors.	 Red veins that are covered by oil become visible and they make their work (the task/affliction) evident and weaken the oil every day.
Mestier est donques au premier que tu regardes se li oil, en coi sebel est, est fors, et n’i a autre maladie fuers que lou sebel;	 Therefore it is necessary to first check if the oil, in which the sebaceous gland is located, is open and has no other disease except the sebaceous gland.
adonques le coil en teil maniere:	 Then, hold the neck in this manner:
comande au malaide qu’il mette son chief en ton sain, puis sospent celles voines a tout l’oncine selonc sa sapience, et soit li oncines subtilz double selonc ceste forme:	 instruct the patient to place his head in your hand, then support the chin all around according to your wisdom, and let the hands be subtle and double in this way:
Et soient dui oncine par degrez en .i. cors selonc ceste forme:	And may there be two openings in one body according to this form:
puis c’on coil as forces celles voinnes subtilment, et essue lou sanc houre aprés autre, tant que tu voies removoir celles voines fuers de l’oil;	 then the hands support the chin gently and carefully, squeezing the blood slowly after that, until you see the veins moving away from the oil.
et garde que tu ne blecier l’oil as pointes des spatumiles, et fai cest ovraige a houre de midi devant lou soleil, et soies mout fervans en ton ovraige si que tu ne copes fuer que celles voinnes;	 and be careful not to pierce the oil with the tips of the spatulas, and perform this work at noon before the sun, and be very eager in your work so that you do not injure anything except the veins.
et quant tu avras ce fait, si distille en l’oil coliere vert et rouge por corrumpre ceu qui est demorez dou sebel.	 and when you have done this, if it condenses green and red oil to cure what remains infected.
Et se tu n’as pooir de coillir tout ceu en celle houre, si fai emplastre sus l’oil de choses apaisans la dolor des eulz, et le laisse aucuns jors tant que li dolors soit apaisie et soit asseurez d’aposteme chaut, puis rencomence selonc ceste maniere qui est devant tant qu’il soit sanez;	 And if you cannot catch it in that hour, apply a soothing ointment over the oil of calming things on the eyes, and leave it for some days until the pain is alleviated and assured that the abscess has healed, then continue as before until it is healed;
et c’est li forme des forces:	 And this is the form of the cautery:
de la fistule de l’oil	of the fistula from oil
Li mire si nomment «arissati» fistule:	 The instrument is called "arissati" (orificator):
quant tu la cures per cautere et par medicine ague ardant selonc ceu que j’ai devant dit, et elle n’est mie sanee, si est engien en li que tu fendes sus l’aposteme, lai ou il doit meurer, et trai toute la moistor que i est, tant que li os soit descovers.	 When you treat it by cautery and burning medicine as I have said before, and it is not healed, there is a tool in it where you make an incision over the abscess, where it should die, and drain all the moisture that is there until the bone is exposed.
Et quant li os iert descovers, et tu verras la corruption et la noiror, si la reis a tout l’estrument de coi ci est li forme;	 And when the bone is exposed, you will see the corruption and blackness; if the knife is ready with all the instruments as described here;
et est apelez «aspre chief», et soit fait de feir inde a I chief reont, et soit pointoiez si com une lime si com il est en la presente forme:	 and it is called "sharp head", and it should be made with iron as the handle of the knife, pointed like a chisel in the shape as presented here:
Et met sus lou leu de l’os corrumput, puis le torne entre tes dois, et presse ta main un poc tant que tu saiches que celle corruption est rese;	 And put it on the rotten bone, then turn it between your hands and press your hand a little so that you feel that the corruption is pierced.
et fai ceu aucune fois, puis restoure lou leu de medicines exiccatives.	 and do this once, then restore the joint with medicinal extracts.
se li leus est soudez, et char i naist, et li cors de la bowe est soudez, et remaint ensi XL jors, et il ne renovele et n’est mie apostemez, et accidens mavais n’i vient, saiches qu’il est sanez;	 if the joints are swollen and pus forms, and the body of the bone is also swollen, and remains thus for 40 days without moving or becoming abscessed, and no serious accident occurs, it is known to be healthy.
se ceu non, si n’i a autre engien que de ramener la fistule au pertus dou neif selonc ceste forme:	 If there is no other remedy, the only device for returning the fistula to its place is according to this form:
et est que tu descuevre de l’os la seconde fois par fer, et par medicines agues, et quant il iert descovers si prent I foret selonc ceste forme, et soit li chiés de fer a III angles, et li fust soit atenuis jusc’a chief si com tu vois ci:	 and it is that you open the bone for the second time with iron, and with hot medicines, and when it is opened, take the iron fork according to this form, and let the iron prongs be at three angles, and the shaft be narrowed up to the head as you can see here:
puis le met sus l’os delez lou larmier, et esloigne ta main de l’oil I poc, puis torne a tot le foret tant qu’il perce l’os et le sent li malaides par ceu que li vens en ist s’il tient sa main sus son neif;	 then place it on the bone by the rim, and move your hand away from the oil hole, then turn the iron fork completely until it pierces the bone and the patient feels it through the vein if he holds his hand on his neck:
et pues restoure lou leu de medicines seches, si com je t’ai ensigniet, et quant li char naist et endurcist li leus, si vait li matiere au neif;	 and then restore the joint with dry medicines as I have taught you, and when the flesh grows hard and stiffens the joint, the matter goes to the neck:
si est plus legiere chose au malaide.	 It is a lighter thing for the patient.
de l’issue de l’oil	From the flow of oil
Quant li eulz apert fuer dou tout en tout, et il ne vient point de destorbier au nef, ne amenuisement, si covient que tu lies lou malaide;	 When all the eyes are open wide in every way, and it does not cause disturbance to the ship or any reduction, then you must bind the patient.
puis le saine, puis li met ventouses ou haterel sens ferir por succier, puis met sus l’oil I liien fait d’acaice et de aloe et d’encens et de sarcocolle, et puis estrain l’oil, et l’emplaustre sus de bendes et de drapelz;	 Then heal the healthy parts, then apply ointments or oil with iron for help, then put oil made of asafoetida and aloe and incense and saracolle on it, then strain the oil, and smear the oil over bandages and cloths.
et li maniere des drapelz si est que tu preignes drapelz assez molz, et double chescun en IIII, et puis met l’un sus l’autre selonc la quantiteit que li eulz en ait mestier;	 and the manner of cloths is that you take soft cloths, fold each one in four, and then place one on top of the other according to the quantity that the eyes need.
puis l’estrain par desus d’un bendeil dur forment, et rencomence les ventouses por succier sens ferir;	 Then strain it from above with a hard bandage and begin to compress wounds without cutting with iron.
puis oste les ventouses et laisse l’oil estraint jor et nuit, et se li liiens amolist, si covient que tu l’estraignes mout;	 Then release the wound oil and allow it to be strained for a day and night, and if it softens, you must strain it strongly.
puis oste lou liien aprés le jor et la nut, et se tu vois l’oil repairier, c’est boin;	 Then remove the bandage after the day and night, and if you see the oil healing, that is good.
se ce non;	 If not;
si rencomence l’emplaustre et les drapelz et lou liien et les ventouses tant qu’il soit sanez.	 Then begin the poultice and cloths and bandage and dressings until it is healed.
dou derrompement de toile uvee	The breaking of a rotten cloth
Quant disruptions vient en la toile uvee, puis apert, et vient fuer des papieres si com I grain de resins, et est espoantauble a veoir;	 When ruptures occur in the inflamed cloth, open it up and bring forth paper as if with the grain of resin, and it is easily visible.
adonques se tu la vues coper, li ovraiges est telz que tu boutes une aguille en la racine des la partie desoz jusc’a celi desus, puis boute une autre aguille ou il ait I fil double des la partie dou larmier;	 Then if you see it covered, the treatments are such that you insert an awl into the root of the affected area from below up to above, then insert another awl or double thread from the side of the wound.
et la fai percier, et laisse la premiere aguille selonc la disposition;	 And make it pierce through, leave the first needle according to its position;
puis cope lou leu dou fil double et lie une partie de l’uve entor, et l’estraint bien, puis estrai l’aguille et met sus l’oil lainne moillie en abun d’uef;	 then take the thread of double yarn and tie a part of the eye around it, tighten it well, then remove the needle and put moistened flaxseed oil on top of it;
et le laisse tant que li filz chiece avec l’uve, puis cure l’oil de choses confortans tant que li plaie soit sanee;	 and leave it until the thread heals with the eye, then heal the oil with comforting things until the wound is healed;
et aucune fois li plaie est restrainte par l’uve chescune part d’un cercle de drap, tant qu’elle soit sanee.	 and sometimes the wound is bound by the eye on each side of a circle of cloth until it is healed.
Et se li eulz done grant apparance, si le perce au spatumile subtil qui viegne em parfont de l’oil, et corre la moistor albuginé et dessende li eulz, et entre ens tantost;	 And if the eyes appear large, pierce it with a fine spatula that comes from full oil, correct the moisture abscess and drain the eyes, and put it in immediately.
puis l’estrai tant qu’il soit sanez.	 Then straighten it until it is sound.
de la bowe de l’oil	of the oil bowl
Ceste maladie qui est apelee «alcunnati» nen est fuers que bowe qui est assemblee en l’oil, semblant a aigue dessendant, et ce n’est mie aigue;	 This disease called "alcunnati" is not far from the eye which is assembled in oil, resembling an ulcer draining, but it is not an ulcer.
et li maniere de l’apparance de l’ovraige si est que tu faices seoir lou malaide sus I siege appareilliet et droit, puis prent le chief entre tes mains de II pars, et lou muef tant que tu voies la bowe venir au desus a tes eulz;	 and the manner of its appearance is that you make the patient sit on a prepared seat upright, then take hold of his head with both hands from behind, and move him so that you see the bone come up to your eyes.
puis soit ens fichie, et ne dessende et soit descombree li lumiere, et voie li malaides les choses si com il soloit;	 then it should be pressed in, without draining and open the light, and the patient should see things as he is accustomed.
et s’elle ne dessent desoz, saiches que c’est aigue, et se li dessendemens de la bowe n’est appareilliez si com nos avons dit.	 if it does not drain below, know that it is an ulcer, and the draining of the bone is not as we have said.
si fai seoir lou malaide entre tes mains, puis prent le spatumile subtil et fent sus la toile cornee I poc par la continuation de la conjunctive avec la toile cornee et la corone, tant que li bowe isse;	 Make the patient sit between your hands, then take the thin spatula and press it against the horny layer of the eyelid at the conjunction with the cornea and the eyeball, until it bulges.
et quant elle ert issue, si distille en l’oil aigue chaude mellee a miel, ou aigue ou fenugreic est boillis et miel, puis soit curee d’autre cure tant qu’elle soit sanee.	 And when it has protruded, let it be distilled in sharp hot oil mixed with honey or aged oil and fenugreek, or hot oil and honey, then let it be cured with another remedy until it is healed.
des aigues de l’oil	waters of oil (literally: "of the oil")
Nos avons jai les semblances des aigues en la division, et ceu qu’il covient por percier;	 We have similarities of the eyes in their division, and that which must be pierced;
si en oevre selonc la santeit.	 if it works according to health.
Il covient que tu faices seoir lou malaide entre tes mains croisiet, fuers de la lumiere por le soleil, et li lie l’oil sain et estreint mout fort;	 You must make the patient sit between your hands crossed, away from light because of the sun, and let him hold the oil and squeeze it very tightly;
puis met la papiere de l’oil a ta main senestre se li eulz est senestres, ou a ta main destre se li eulz est destres;	 Then put the paper of oil on your left hand if the eyes are on the left, or on your right hand if they are on the right.
puis prent en ta main destre, se li eulz est senestres, l’estrument qui est apelez «almagda», ou a ta main senestre, se li eulz est destre;	 Then take in your right hand, if the eyes are on the left, the instrument called 'almagda', or in your left hand, if they are on the right.
puis met la pointe de l’estrument delez la corone par la groissece d’un rait en celle blenchor de l’oil a la partie dou menor larmier, puis boute l’estrument qui est apelez «almagda» vertuousement, et trestorne ta main tant qu’il perce en la blenchor de l’oil, et sente que almagda viegne a la chose vuide;	 Then put the point of the instrument through the crown by the thickness of a thumb in that hollow part of oil to the smaller tear duct, then push the instrument called 'almagda' firmly, and hold your hand until it pierces through the hollow of oil, and feel that almagda enters into the empty space.
et covient que li mesure de la voie almagda soit au parfont de la mesure des l’espaice qui est des la prunele jusc’a la fin de la noirour;	 And it is necessary that the measure of the way almagda should be at the end of the measurement of the space which is from the pupil up to the end of the nose.
et c’est li corone de l’oil;	 And it is the crown of the ear.
si verras l’os en celle papiere por la clarteit de la toile cornee, et pues met l’estrument jusc’a leu ou li aigue est, puis l’espresse desoz une voie aprés autre.	 If you look at the bone in this paper by the brightness of the perforated parchment, then place the instrument up to it or the sharp point, and press down along another way after that.
se li aigue dessent maintenant, si voit li malaides devant lui et l’estrument en son oil.	 The patient should now press down on it (the shoulder), so he sees the instrument before him in its oil.
Aprés repose I petit, et se li aigue remonte la seconde voie, met la fuer avec l’estrument, et quant elle est ens fichie et ele ne monte, si estrai almagda legierement en tornoiant ta main poc et poc;	 After a little rest, and if the sharp point rises along the second way, apply the force with the instrument, and when it is pushed in and it does not rise anymore, gently draw it out by rotating your hand slowly.
et puis remette en aigue un poc de seil gemme, et leive de ceu l’oil dedens.	 Then replace the sharp point a little with beeswax, and cut off that oil inside.
Puis met par defuer l’oil estoupes ou lainne moillie en oile roset et en abun d’uef, et lie avec l’oil sain.	 Then put on it (the shoulder) a cloth or wool soaked in rose oil and egg oil, and bind it with the healthy oil.
Nos, et cil qui sont de nostre tens, mettons sus comin broiet avec abun d’uef.	 We, and those of our time, place on top a mixture made with plenty of eggs.
Et se almagda n’i puet entrer en l’oil par sa duresce, car il i a de teilz homes qui ont trop durs les eulz, si covient que tu preignes l’estrument qui est apelez «alberit», de coi ci est li forme:	If the oil cannot enter due to its hardness, as there are some men who have too hard eyes, then you must take the instrument called "alberit", which is shaped like this:
Et perce donques la conjunctive soulement, et n’aler mie trop em parfont, mais fai I leu subtil, puis i boute almagda, si com nos avons dit;	 Therefore, pierce only the conjunction and do not go too deep, but make it subtle, then push it in as we have said.
et au complissement de l’uevre appareille au malaide I dorteur avenant, en coi il dorme sus son dos en I leu tenebrous;	 And in the completion of the work, the patient, the sleeper, lies down facing his back in a dark place;
et soit deveez de toz movemens, et preigne legieres viandes, et ne mueve son chief ne a destre ne a senestre, et soit liiez selonc sa disposition jusc’a tier jor;	 And he should be kept from all movement, and take light food, and not move his head to the right or left, and tie him according to his position for three days;
puis le deslie en cele maison meisme tenebrouse, et esprueve sa veue, et lou fai veoir aucunes choses, et puis li remet lou lien jusc’a septime jor;	 Then untie him in the same dark house, test his sight, and make him see some things, and then tie him again for seven days;
et ne covient mie que tu faices ceu en l’oure de la cure ou aprés l’incision maintenant, mais il covient que tu aliges ceu, por ceu que li aigue monte hastanment.	 And it is not necessary that you do this during the time of treatment or after incision now, but it is necessary that you lighten it, because the pain increases quickly.
se apostemes chaus vient, que tu desliies l’oil devant le septime jor, et l’adrece de ceu qui assouaige aposteme;	 If an abscess comes up, you should untie the oil before the seventh day, and direct it to that which soothes the abscess;
et quant il est apaisiez, si deslie la veue et met sus sa faice I orilliet por covrir aucun jor, et soit adés en celle maison tenebrouse.	 And when it has been calmed [the dislocated joint], separate the eyelids and place on its face an ointment to cover for any duration of time, and remain there in that dark room evermore.
Et puis isse de la maison poc et poc, et se convertisse en ses cas;	 And then gradually leave the house, one step at a time, and return to his quarters.
et saiches que nulz deciples ne se doit entremettre en cest cas.	 And understand that no disciple should intervene in this case.
Et uns vint a nos qui estoit de la Yrach, qui nos dist que en som pais faisoit om almagda perciet, a coi on succe l’aigue, mais toutevoie je n’en vis onques nul en nostre terre, ne je ne lou lis onques en livres des anciens;	 And one came to us who was from the Yrach [Iran], who told us that in their country they practice the amalgam process, by which the [mercury] juice is drawn, but I have never seen anyone do it in our land, nor have I read about it in the books of the ancients;
et par aventure c’est une novele chose.	 And perhaps it is a new thing.
Et ce sont les semblances des formes de almagda, por ceu que cil qui ne les conoit les voie;	 And these are the appearances of the forms of almadga, because those who do not know them see them.
et soient d’arain proprement:	 and are properly speaking:
Et soient li chief d’aus de ceste meisme subtiliteit, et li derriene en .iij. angles ague.	And the head of oxen of this same subtlety shall have four corners pointing.
de la char sor le neis	On the flesh over the neck
Aucune fois naissent ou neis chars ajostees diverses, de coi il i a aucunes qui semblent scorpions a mout de piez;	 Sometimes there are born or are born worms that are dissimilar, from which some seem like scorpions with many feet.
et si i a de telz ou il ait char enchancree de fuxe color, et si a char souef de bone color.	 and if there are any like this or if the worm is swollen with such color, and if the worm is soft of bone color.
En celle donques de ces chars qui est souef, et ne mie enchancree, covient que tu faices seoir lou malaide entre tes mains encontre lou soleil;	 Therefore, for those worms that are soft and not swollen, you must make the patient sit between your hands facing the sun.
et oevre ses narines, et giete l’oncine a celles chars, et les trai fuers;	 and open its nostrils, and pour vinegar on these worms, and pull them out forcefully.
pues cope ceu que tu em pues sostenir au spatumile subtil agut d’une part, tant que tu saiches que celle char est toute ostee.	 Therefore hold what you can sustain on the pointed spur of a needle-like instrument from one side, as long as you know that the body is completely ossified.
Et s’il en remaint aucune chose c’on ne puisse coper, si l’ovrez a tout I des estrumens subtil legierement, si qu’il n’i demoure rien;	 And if there remains any substance that cannot be held, open it all to the finest and lightest instruments carefully, so that nothing remains.
et se sans te sormonte, ou aposteme chaus, si lou secort si com il covient;	 and if no abscess is formed or pus has collected, use the help as necessary.
et se c’est apostemes malignes, si te haste et lou cauterize tant que li sans soit estainchiez et soient ostees toutes les chars, puis giete ou neis aisil et aigue ou vin.	 and if it is malicious abscesses, hasten and burn them with the cautery until the pus is drained and all the flesh is charred and burned, then pour in oil or alcohol and vinegar.
Se li neis oevre, et moistors en vient jusc’a palais, saiches qu’il est sanez;	 If the urine works, and moisture reaches the palace (brain), know that it is healthy;
et se moistors ne perce si com il covient, saiches qu’il i a char nee en l’os desus, a coi li estrumens ne vient mie por taillier:	 And if moisture does not pierce as it should, know that there is new flesh in the bone above, which prevents the instrument from cutting.
adonques covient il que tu i boutes I fil de lin un poc gros, et soit noez de mains nous, et ait entre chescun nout d’espaice I doit ou moins;	 Then you must insert a small piece of flax thread, and it should be soaked in the hands, with space between each stitch no less.
et mette li malaides lou chiés dou fil en son neif a som pooir, et traie en odorant tant qu’il viegne par lou neif dedens la bouche;	 and place the patient's head in the thread through his nose as far as possible, and pull it out smelling until it comes from the nose.
et maintes fois font ensi li enfant as escoles, et c’est legiere chose a celui qui le vuet faire;	 and many times children in schools do this, and it is easy for anyone who wants to do it.
puis tien le chief qui vient par lou neif a une main, et l’autre chief qui vient par la bouche a l’autre main, et saiche l’un aprés l’autre en soiant as nous qui sont ou fil.	 Then hold the head that comes through the nose with one hand, and the other head that comes from the mouth with the other hand; know which is which among us who are the thread.
Fai ceu tant que tu saiches que li nout ont corrompue celle char, puis trai lou filz, essue le sanc, et moille lou fil en oignement egiptien, et le remet derechief au neis si com devant;	 Make it so that you know that the flesh has been corrupted, then draw out the cord, squeeze the blood, and moisten the cord in Egyptian ointment, and put it back in place as before.
fai ceu III jors ou plus, tant que li oignemens corrode tout ceu qui est demorez de char;	 keep it for three days or more, until the ointment corrodes everything that remains of flesh;
et puis met ou neis une caine de plonc aucuns jors tant qu’il soit sanez, et s’il a mestier de medicines sechans, si en use;	 and then put a piece of flax in its place for some days until it is healed, and if there is need for drying medicines, use them.
et c’est li forme de l’estrument por purgier lou chief, a coi on distille les oiles et les medicines ou neis:	 and this is the form of the instrument to purge the head, where oil and medicines are distilled.
Et soit d’argent ou d’arain, semblant a une lampe overte, si com une cainne, et li conduis ausi;	 And it should be made of silver or copper, resembling an open lantern, similar to a piece of flax, and lead it thus.
et se tu vues, si fai une cainne close, et soit li estrumens plains por espurgier lou chief;	 And if you see, make a narrow channel, let the instrument be full for cleansing the head.
et ait I mainche au chief por lou tenir quant on chaufe l’oile ou aucune liquor.	 and hold the receptacle at the head when heating the oil or any liquid.
de la char sor le neis	On the flesh over the neck
Maintes fois naist au chief dou neis une maladie qui est apelee «telul», et croist et devient grans adés, tant qu’il est vis chose au regarder;	 Often in the head, a disease named "telul" arises, which grows and becomes large over time, until it can be seen with the eye.
et por ceu covient que tu lou copes au comencement, et l’oste tout fuer, puis met sor leu lou cautere ou la medicine ardant;	 And because of this, you must cut it at the beginning and completely remove it, then place the fire cautery or burning medicine on it.
et s’on le tarde a coper tant qu’il soit grans, si pren warde s’il est durs, de fuxe color, de povre sens:	 And if you delay cutting it until it becomes large, beware if it is hard, of such a color, and poor sensation.
si ne lou touchier mie de fer car c’est uns apostemes enchancrez, car quant on le cope aucune fois, si en vient grant malice au malaide;	 Do not touch it with iron because it is an abscess hardened, for when you cut it once, much harm comes to the patient.
