et se li apostemes est de soef touchement, non mie de fuxe color, et tu vois c’on le puisse tout coper, si vuide le malaide et lou cope sens paor, et cure le leu de choses sechans et restraignans.	 If the abscess is touched with softness, not of a fire color, and you see that it can be completely covered, empty the patient and soothe him with fear, and treat the area with drying and constricting things.
quant li neis est copez et cosus	when the neck is cut and sewn
Saiches que quant solutions de continuation vient en une de ces cartillagines ovraiges, i profite poc, fuer que en aucuns homes.	 Know that when swelling comes in one of these cartilage joints, it is of little use for most men.
Il covient donques cant ceu avient a aucun, si regarde se li plaie est fresche a tout son sanc;	 Therefore, it should be noted that if this happens, observe whether the wound is fresh with all its blood;
et adonques ajoste les II levres a une costure, puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	 then press the two lips together in a stitch, and treat it until it heals.
et se les levres sont ja desevrees d’une part et d’autre, si covient que tu escorches toutes les parties de lor keur tant qu’elles sainent, puis assemble les II levres a une costure, et l’estraint, et poudre sus poudre de sanc de dragon, et encens broiet;	 If the lips are already separated from both sides, you must excise all the affected parts until they heal, then press the two lips together in a stitch, bind it and apply powder of dragon's blood, and incense crushed.
et met sus les poudres une piece d’emplaustre de fort ou d’autre emplaustre soudant, et le laisse tant qu’il chiece par lui, puis le cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	 And put on top of the powder a piece of plaster of strong or another adhesive plaster, and leave it until it hardens by itself, then cure it with ointment until it is healed.
Li maniere de la costure si est que tu assembles la solution:	 The method of stitching is that you gather the solution:
ou par aguilles, si com nos avons dit en la costure dou ventre;	 or with needles, as we have said in the belly stitching;
ou par fil, si com je le t’ai fait savoir.	 or with thread, as I have told you.
des apostemes des levres	of abscesses of the lips
A mains homes avient dedens les levres aposteme dur, semblans a grains de veces, et menor et plus grant;	 In men there often occurs an abscess hard within the lips, resembling grains of various sizes, both small and large.
adonques couvient que tu tornes les levres, et fendes sus chescun nout, et le prent as pinceures et le cope en chescune partie;	 Then you must turn the lips, cut above each one, take them with forceps and crush them in each part;
puis emple lou leu aprés l’incision de vitriole broiet, tant que li sans soit estainchiez;	 Then apply the mortar of vitriol after the incision, while the wound is still bleeding.
et puis lou leive d’aisil, et cure lou leu de choses seches tant qu’il soit sanez.	 And then soothe the wound with dry remedies until it heals.
de la char des gencives	of the chin
Maintes fois naist sus les gencives char ajostee, que li ancien apelent «albulus»;	 Often, a bladder-like growth appears on the gums, which the ancients called "albulus".
si covient que tu la sostienes as tenailles, et la cope a sa racine, et laisse corre la bowe ou le sanc;	 You must hold it with forceps and cut off its root, leaving the bone or blood vessels exposed.
puis met sor le leu vitriole broiet, ou autres poudres restraignans et desiccatives;	 Then apply powdered vitriol or other constricting and drying agents to the wound.
et se celle char revient aprés l’incision, et maintes fois avient, si la cope la seconde fois, et la cauterize:	 If the growth returns after the incision, which often happens, you should cut it a second time and cauterize it.
si ne revient mie aprés le cautere;	 if it does not return after cauterization.
et ce sont les formes des estrumens por coper.	 And these are the shapes of the instruments for covering [or bandaging].
des sordens	of sores
Aucunes fois sont assemblees au chief des dens, dedens la bouche entre les gencives, escorces qui sont laides et aspres;	 Sometimes, pieces are assembled on the jaw bones, within the mouth between the gums, which are ugly and harsh.
et aucune fois sont li dent noir et citrin et vers, tant que li corruption vient a la gencive, et sont li dent puant;	 And sometimes teeth turn black, yellow, and decay as corruption comes to the gums, and the teeth rot.
si covient que tu faices seoir lou malaide entre tes mains, et ses chiés soit en ton saint, et reis les dens ou les escorces aperent, tant qu’il n’i demore rien;	 You must make the patient sit between your hands and hold his head in your lap, and pull out or scrape the teeth where they appear until there is nothing left.
et ensi fai de la noiror et de la verdor, et de la jaunice et des autres taiches, tant qu’elles soient mondees;	 And do the same with blackness and greenness, yellowness and other stains, until they are cleaned.
et s’on oste ceu que i est a la premiere rasion, c’est boin;	 If you remove those that are at the root, it is good.
se ceu non, si rencomence a rere le secont jor et lou tier, tant que tu aies tout reis;	 If not, start again on the second or third day and continue until everything has been pulled out.
et saiches que li dent ont mestier de diverses formes d’estrumens por reire, selonc ceu que li oevre lou demoustre, por ceu que li raseur dont on reit defuer les dens ont autres formes que cil dont on reit entre les dens;	 Know that teeth require different shapes of instruments for pulling out, according to what the work shows, because the puller who removes teeth has different shapes than those who remove between the teeth.
et cestes formes et autres soient avec toi appareillies.	 And these forms and others are ready for you.
Il covient quant tu cures lou dent de sa dolor que tu tardes dou traire tant com tu pues, car ce ne doit om mie faire;	 It is necessary when curing the tooth of its pain that you delay drawing it out as much as you can, for this must not be done at all.
car c’est une substance mout haute jusc’a donc c’on n’ait point d’excusation dou raier.	 because it is a very high substance up to which there is no excuse for cutting.
Adonques quant li malaides est constrains dou traire, si covient que tu soies certains dou dent doillant.	 Therefore, when the patient is forced to draw teeth, you must be certain about the pulling tooth.
Maintes fois desoit li dolor lou malaide, et cuide qu’elle soit ou dent saint, et fait traire le boin dent;	 Many times the patient feels pain and believes it is a holy tooth, and draws the good tooth.
et toutevoie ne se depart mie li dolor per ceu, tant que li malvais estrais, car nos l’avons ja veut faire a ces sainors;	 nevertheless, the pain does not go away even then, until the bad one is removed, for we have seen it happen with holy people.
et quant tu es bien certains dou dent doillant, si covient que tu escorches entor lou dent a tout i. spatumile fort por warder la gencive de toutes pars;	 and when you are certain that the tooth is rotten, it is necessary that you scrape around the tooth in all places. Spathulum strongly to protect the gums from all sides;
puis le mues a tes dois ou as tenailles subtilz au premier poc et poc, tant qu’il soit bien eslochiés, puis i afferme bien les tenailles;	 Then move it at your elbows or subtle tweezers at the first poke and poke, until they are well dislocated, then firmly hold the tweezers.
et soit li chiés dou malaide en ton saint entre tes genous, et lou tien bien si qu’il ne se mueve.	 And have the patient's head between your knees, and hold it steady so that it does not move.
Aprés estrai lou dent droitement sens brisier, et s’il ne saut fuer, si prent aucun de ces estrumens et le boute dedens de chescune part legierement, et lou remuef si com tu as fait premier.	 After straightening the tooth correctly to break it, if it does not come out, take any of these instruments and gently push it in from each side, and move it as you have done before.
Et se li dens est perciez et mengiez, si covient que tu l’emplisses de drapelz, lai ou li pertus sont;	 If the teeth are pierced and eaten, you must fill it with cloths where the wounds are.
et si l’estraint subtilment as tenailles, que il ne brise a l’estraindre;	 And if you hold it gently with tweezers so that it does not break while being pulled out.
et covient mout saigement ovrer entor la gencive por deschaucier lou dent.	 You must cautiously work around the gum to loosen the tooth.
Et te done bien en warde que tu ne le brises, et en remaigne une partie, et reveigne au malaide par la malice de la racine plus grans dolors de la premiere.	 And be careful not to break it, and leave a part behind, and the pain for the patient will return from the root even greater.
Et te warde que tu ne faices mie ensi com font li ignorant sainor, qui par lor haste et par lor hardiesce brisent aucune fois le charreit, et n’i amenistrent mie ceu que nos avons conteit;	 And beware that you do not act like the ignorant men who, through their haste and recklessness, break the cart [shoulder] sometimes, and do not bring what we have mentioned.
mais font venir aucune fois par l’oquison de ceu grant maladie por les racines que i demorent, ou por lou charreit qu’il brisent, si com nos avons sovent veut;	 But sometimes, due to the root cause of this great disease, it comes through the urine or because the cartilage breaks, as we have often seen;
et quant li dens est trais, si lavez lou leu de vin ou d’aisil et de seil;	 and when the tooth is pulled out, wash the place with wine or vinegar and salt;
et se decorremens de sanc i vient, que sovent avient, si emple lou leu de vitriole broiet;	 and if bleeding continues from the wound, which often happens, use the place with ground vitriol;
et se ceu ne vaut, si le cauterize.	 and if that does not work, cauterize it.
Les formes des estrumens, a coi om muet les dens premier, soient a longes pointes et a gros mainches, qu’il ne doublent mie quant tu trairas le dent;	 The shapes of instruments that initially quieten the tooth should have long points and thick handles, so that they do not double back as you pull out the tooth;
et ce sont les formes:	 these are their shapes:
Et soient de gros membres si qu’il ne ploient mie au traire, et soient de fer inde bien fait, et soient dentez por mues tenir.	And be large enough that they do not bend when drawing the tooth and made of good iron, and be pointed to hold the tooth in place.
de la racine des dens	of the roots of the teeth
Quant li racine demoure au traire, si covient que tu mettes sor le leu coton moilliet em burre I jor ou II, tant que li leus soit amolis, pues i boute les tenailles qui sont apelees «algefri», de coi li chiés semblet bec de soigne;	 When the root remains after pulling out the tooth, it is necessary to put cotton moistened in butter for a day or two on the place until the place is softened, then insert the pliers called "algefri", which give the appearance of a beak;
et soient dedens faites ausi com une lime et c’est li forme:	 And within it (should) be made similarly as a chisel, this is its shape:
Et se les racines ne vuellent issir a tout ces tenailles, si covient que tu descuevre la char tot entor la racine, et i met l’estrument qui est apelez «althali», c’est a savoir palainche, de coi ci est li forme:	And if the roots do not wish to come out with all these tongs, you must peel back the skin entirely around the root, and place the instrument called "althali," which is known as a palindrome, in its place.
Et soit fors et gros si qu’il ne brise mie, et se li racine saut par ceu, c’est boin;	 And it should be long and thick so that it does not break easily, and if the root jumps through it, that's good;
se ceu non, si t’aide de toz les estrumens, de coi les formes vienent ci aprés:	 If that is not the case, help yourself with all tools, from which these shapes will follow afterwards:
Et si s’aide on de cest estrument qui ait .ij. rains, de coi ci est li forme:	And if one uses the instrument with two prongs, its form is as follows:
et d’autres ferremens qui sont devant en la rasion des dens, et de cest estrument qui semble unes grans tenailles, dont ci est li forme:	And other instruments that are in front of the teeth, for this tool appears to be large pincers. Here is its shape:
Et soit cist estrumens fors qu’il ne puisse brisier, et saiches que mout d’estrumens de dens sont;	 Let this tool be long so that it cannot break, and know that many dense tools are required;
et ausi d’autres estrumens, qui ne sont mie contez;	 and also other tools, which are not counted.
et li saiges maistres subtilz trueve par soi meisme son estrument, selonc ceu que ses ovraiges et li maladie li demoustre, car il i a de teilz maladies ou li ancien n’enseignerent point d’estrument por la diversiteit d’au;s et s’om brise point dou charreit ou des autres os, ou il porrit, si i cerche as estrumens qu’il i covient, que je t’ai dit, et t’aide des gestes, de coi ci est li forme:	 and the wise masters will find their own tool by themselves, according to what their work and the illness indicates, because there are some diseases where ancient teachings did not mention any tool due to diversity among them; and if it breaks the cart or other bones, where it could be, he should search for the tools that are needed, which I have told you, and help himself with gestures, from which this shape follows:
Et soient gros et bien tenant por tenir l’os, qu’il n’eschaipe, mais le puisse tenir et oster;	 And let them be large and firm to hold the bone, so it does not slip away, but rather can be held and removed.
et puis restoure lou leu de medicines convenant a ceu, et s’il ait en l’os porriture, et elle est petite, si la reis a tout cest estrument:	 And then restore the joint with the appropriate medicine, and if there is putrefaction in the bone, and it is small, remove everything.
Quant li dent apperent ne mie selonc lou cors natureil, et li forme est laide, et meismement en femmes puceles, si covient que tu saiches se li dens est neis aprés lou dent, et n’est mie en droit leu, et on ne lou puet soier ne limer:	 When the teeth appear not according to natural shape and the form is ugly, especially in girls, it is necessary that you know if the teeth are misplaced after the tooth has come out, and it is not in the correct position, and they cannot be straightened or filed.
adonques lou raie;	 Then remove the tooth.
et s’il est aers avec lou dent, si prent cest estrument dont ci est li forme, et est semblans a I petit bec, et soit de fer inde agut en som:	 If it is in front of the tooth, take this tool whose shape is like a small beak, and made of sharp steel at the end.
Et lou cope poc et poc em mains jors por la duresce dou dent, et por ceu que tu ne mueves les autres, et s’il est apparans c’on le puisse limer, si lou lime d’une teil lime com ci est li forme:	And the handle of the forceps should be used gently for many days due to the hardness of the tooth and because you do not move the others, and if it is possible, file it down with a small file in the shape as shown here:
et est ausi com li lime de coi on fait les aguilles;	 And it is similar to the limb from which they make needles;
et en lime lou dent poc et poc em mains jors legierement, si qu’il ne se mueve tant qu’il chiece;	 and in the limb, let the tooth grow slowly day by day gently, so that it does not move until it falls out;
puis la plaine en la fin a tout aucun raseur, et se li dens est trop trenchans et il blece la lengue, si covient limer l’aspreteit tant qu’il soit igalz, si qu’il ne blece la lengue ne ne corrompe la parole.	 then the plane at the end with any grinder, and if the tooth is too sharp and it bites the tongue, you must file down the sharpness until it is even, so that it does not bite the tongue or corrupt the speech;
quant li dent lochent	When the teeth fall out.
Quant li dent devant lochent, ou par percussion ou par cheoir, et li malaides ne puet presser sus ceu qu’il menjue qu’il ne chient, et tu les as curez de medicines restrignans, et ceu ne vaut;	 When the tooth falls out in front due to percussion or falling, and the patient cannot chew food without it falling out, and you have treated them with constricting medicines, that is of no use;
si les covient restraindre d’un fil d’or, car li filz d’argent devient vert et porrit, mais li ors ne se mue onques;	 therefore they should be held together with a gold wire, for the silver threads become green and rot, but gold does not change.
et soit li filz moiens ne trop gros ne trop menus, selonc la quantiteit de l’espaice entre les dens;	 And let the size of the thread be neither too thick nor too thin, according to the space between the teeth.
et se tu vues adrecier les dens, si pren lou fil et lou boute double entre les II dens sains, puis met les chiés entre les dens meus, s’il en i a I ou plusors, tant que tu veignes saigement jusc’au dent sain d’autre part;	 And if you wish to align the teeth, take the thread and double it between two sound teeth, then place the cheeks between the front teeth, if there is one or more of them, as far as you see soundly up to the tooth on the other side.
puis rencomence la coverture jusc’a la partie ou tu encomensas, et estrains ta main subtilment et saigement, tant qu’il ne se mueve point;	 then resume the covering until the part where you began, and hold your hand gently and carefully, so it does not move.
et soit ta lieeure a la racine dou dent si qu’il ne puist eschaper.	 and tie the thread to the root of the tooth so it cannot escape.
Puis cope les chiés dou fil a unes tenailles, et les assemble, et les repont entre le dent sain, et le met ensi qu’il ne blece la lengue;	 Then hold the cheeks with the thread using tweezers and assemble them, and insert them between the sound tooth and place it so it does not pierce the tongue.
et puis le laisse ensi estroit tant com il puet demorer, et s’il deslie, ou li filz ront, si l’estraint d’un autre fil;	 And then leave it as tight as it can stay for a while, and if it dislocates, or the tendons run, hold it with another thread.
si demorrait et servira ensi tout son tens, et c’est li forme des dens et li figure de l’adrecement des II dens sains, et des II meus, si com tu vois:	 If it lasts and serves thus for all its time, and this is the form of the teeth and the alignment of the two healthy teeth and the two roots, as you can see.
Et quant li dent chiet, si lou remet on en son leu, de fres en fres, si com nos avons dit;	 And when a tooth falls out, put it back in its place freshly, as we have said.
et ne s’en entremette mie qui n’est saiges et soffrans, et aucune fois fait on la forme d’un dent d’os de vaiche, et lou met on au leu ou li defaute est, et l’estraint on si com nos avons dit, et demore et sert ensi lonc tens.	 And do not interfere with it if one is not wise and patient; sometimes the form of a tooth made from ox bone is done and put in the place where it lacks, and it is held as we have said, and it lasts and serves for a long time.
de coper lou liien de la lengue	To cover the ligament of the tongue
Aucune fois est cist liiens qui vient desoz la lengue ou naturez, que on naist ensi;	 Sometimes this link comes from beneath the tongue or naturally.
ou par accident de plaie soudee;	 by accident of a welded wound.
et li ovraiges est telz que tu oevre la bouche dou malaide, et ait sa teste en ton sain, et li lieve la lengue;	 and the procedure is such that you open the patient's mouth, hold their head still, and pull the tongue.
puis cope lou liien nervous dou large, tant que li lengue soit desloie de son tenement, et se il i a duresce ou nout, et c’est de soudement de plaie, si i boute l’uncine et cope dou large celui liement;	 then catch the nervous link firmly with a wide instrument, as long as the tongue is dislocated from its position, and if it is hard or notched, which is a deep wound, press the forceps and tightly grasp the linked part.
et garde que li fendure ne soit mie trop em parfont, por l’artere qui est desoz;	 and make sure the cut is not too deep, as there is an artery beneath it.
et quant tu as fait, si leve le leu d’aigue rose et d’aisil, ou d’aigue froide, puis met desoz la lengue une tente de lin;	 and when you have finished, lift the red and warm or cold piece upwards, then put a tent of linen under the tongue.
et la teigne li malaides chescune nuit, que li leus ne puisse soder.	 And the worms the patient every night, so that the limbs cannot heal.
Et se decorremens de sanc vient, si met sor le leu vitriole broiet;	 If there is a discharge of blood, put on the wound Vitriol powder.
et se li sans te vaint, si le cauterize au cautere lentiginout, qui est boin a ceu;	 And if the wound opens up, cauterize it with the cautery known as lentiginout, which is good for this purpose.
puis le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez,	 Then heal it with another remedy until it is healed,
et se tu lou vois de fusse color ou noir ou dur, si que li malaides ne lou sent, si n’i touchier point, car c’est chancre;	 And if you see a spot of pale, black or hard color, which the patient does not feel, do not touch it because it is a cancer.
et s’il est declinans a blenchor, et il i a moistor, si i giete l’oncine, et lou fent d’un spatumile subtil, et lou delivre d’une part et d’autre;	 And if it is swelling with pus and there is moisture, throw in onion juice, and with a thin spatula, loosen it from both sides.
et se li sans te vaint a ton ovraige, si met sus vitriole broiet tant qu’il soit estainchiez, puis revien a ton ovraige tant que tu traies tout fuer;	 And if the bone protrudes in your work, place boiled vitriol on it until it is burned, then return to your work when you have drawn all fire.
puis leve lou leu d’aisil et de seil, et le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	 Then raise the limb and cover with linen and let it heal with other treatments until it is healed.
des apostemes de la gorge	Abscesses of the throat
Aucune fois vient dedens la gorge boces qui sont apelees «godath», et les apele on proprement les II amandres, et quant tu les cures, si com nos avons dit en la division, et elles ne sont sanees, si pren garde:	 Sometimes boils come inside the throat which are called "godath," and they are properly called almonds; when you treat them as we said in the division, and they are not healed, take care.
se c’est apostemes dur de petit sens et de fusse color, si ne lou touchier mie de fer.	 If it is a hard abscess of small size and dark color, do not touch it with iron.
Et s’il est rouges et li racine est grosse, si ne lou touchier mie de fer, ausi por lou decorrement de sanc;	 And if it is red and the root is large, do not touch it with iron, also for the flow of blood.
mais lou laisse tant qu’il soit meur, et adonques tu lou partiras, ou il rompirait par soi;	 But let it (the dislocated joint) remain until it dies, and then you will separate it, or it will break by itself;
et s’il est de blainche color reont, et li racine est subtilz, si aies apareilliet l’estrument por coper, mais regarde premierement se li apostemes chalz repose et est apaisiez.	 And if it (the abscess) is of white color again and the root is subtle, prepare the instrument to cover (it), but first check whether the abscess pus has subsided and been pacified.
Adonques fai seoir lou malaide devant lou soleil, et ses chiés soit en ton sain, et li oevre la bouche et lou preigne li serjans entre ses mains, et presse la lengue desoz a tout l’estrument, de coi ci est li forme;	 Then make the patient sit in the sun and his hands should be in your clean ones, open his mouth and take him by the jaw with the tongs between his hands, press his tongue under the entire instrument, as shown here.
et soit d’argent ou d’arain subtil ausi com uns coutelz:	 and made of silver or fine brass like a knife:
Cant tu presses la lengue a tout cest estrument, et tu vois l’aposteme, si pren l’oncine et lou fiche en l’amandre, et la trai fuer au desus plus que tu pues;	 Do you press the tongue with the entire instrument and see the abscess? If so, take the awl and push it into the anus and pull it out above as much as possible;
et trai aucune chose des toiles avec, puis la cope a l’estrument, de coi ci est li forme, que semble unes forces;	 And pull no thing with the thread, then tie it on the instrument, as shown in this form, which seems like a loop.
et toutevoie li chief sont corbé, et l’un endroit l’autre, et sont molt agut, et est fait de fer inde ou d’andainne:	 And if the head is curved and twisted to one side or another, and they are very sharp, and it is made of iron or steel.
Et se tu n’as cest estrument present, si lou cope as tenailles, de coi ci est li forme:	And if you do not have this instrument present, hold it with pliers of this shape:
Et soit trenchans d’une part, et d’autre part nom;	 And on one side it shall be called "pull", and on the other side "push".
et quant tu as copeit l’une des amandres, si cope l’autre selonc cele meisme maniere, et aprés l’incision gargarize li malaides aigue chaude, et aigue et aisil, et se decorremens de sanc avient, si gargarize li malaides aigue, ou escorces de pomes grenates soient cuites, ou fuelles de mirte, et semblans choses, tant que li sans soit estainchiez;	 And when you have bound one of the nuts (knuckle bones), bind the other in the same manner, and after making the incision, gargle the patient with strong hot, sharp, and warm water, and if bleeding occurs, continue gargling the patient with strong hot water, or cooked apple cores or myrtle leaves, and similar things, until the wound is stopped.
puis lou cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	 Then let the treatment continue until it heals.
et aucune fois naissent en la gorge autres apostemes que les II amandres, si les cope donques ensi com les II amandres igament.	 And sometimes other abscesses are born in the throat besides the two tonsils, so treat them accordingly.
Et je medicinai une femme d’un aposteme que li estoit neis dedens la gorge, c’est a savoir I aposteme de petit sens;	 And I treat a woman with an abscess that was born within the throat, to be specific, the small abscess.
et avoit jai bien pres close toute la gorge, si que li femme ne pooit expirer por le conduit qui estoit estoupez, et ne pooit ne mengier ne boivre, et fust morte s’elle demorast ensi I jor ou II.	 And I had tightly closed the throat so that the woman could not exhale due to the blocked passage, and she could neither eat nor drink, and would have died if she had stayed like that for a day or two.
Et li apostemes estoit jai si montez qu’il avoit fuer mis II rains par les II pertuis dou neis.	 And the abscess had risen so much that it had burst through both openings of the nose.
Je hastai donques tantost, et fichai en l’un I oncine, puis lou traï fuers, et en traï grant porcion de bowe;	 I therefore hastened and pierced one of the tonsils, then pulled it out forcefully, taking out a large piece of pus.
puis refis autreteil en l’autre pertus dou neis, et li ovrai la bouche et li pressai la lengue;	 Then, you should reset the other side of the dislocated neck, and open the mouth and press the tongue.
aprés fichai l’oncine en ces apostemes, et en copai une partie, et n’en issit fuers que un poc de sanc;	 Then, you should cauterize this abscess, cut a piece of it out, and let only a little blood come out.
et ensi fut destoupez li conduis de la gorge la femme, et comensa maintenant a boivre aigue et puis vin, et ne cessai de taillier de cel aposteme par lonc tens;	 And thus the conduit from the woman's throat was cut open, and she began to drink cold water and then wine, and continued to cut away at this abscess for a long time.
et li apostemes recroissoit adés, et remplissoit lou leu que je avoie vuidiet, tant qu’il refut mout gros;	 The abscess grew again and filled the place where I had made the incision, becoming very large.
adonques je l’engignai et lou cauterizai dedens la gorge:	 Then I trapped it and burned it inside her throat.
ensi demora sens croistre;	 It grew slowly with pain.
et me partis de ces parties, et ne soi que Deus fist de li aprés moi.	 And I separate these parts, let God heal them after me.
de l’uve	of the eye
Quant reume dessent a l’uve, et elle est enflee et elle est longe, si est apelee «perpendiculaire»;	 When the vein retracts to the anus and is swollen and long, it is called "perpendicular".
et s’elle est desoz grosse et reonde, si est apelee «uve».	 And if it is beneath large and round, it is called "vein".
Quant elle est curee si com nos avons dit en la division, et li cure ne profite mie, et tu vois que li chaus apostemes est apaisiez, et elle est subtilz, si covient que tu la copes;	 When it is treated as we said in the previous section and the treatment does not help, and you see that the deep abscesses are calmed, and it is subtle, then you must lance it.
et celle qui est reonde assemblee et n’est mie longe;	 And the round one which is not long is called "cyst".
et elle est sanguine ou de fusse color ou noire, si covient que tu eschues l’incision de li.	 If it is bloody or of yellowish color or black, then you must make an incision on it.
Car il i a grant peril sus lou malaide.	 For there is great danger for the patient.
Il covient donques, quant tu la vois, selonc la maniere que j’ai dit, de sa blenchor et de sa longesce, que tu faices seoir le malaide devant lou soleil, et li presse la lengue a l’estrument dont nos avons fait la remembrance ci devant;	 Therefore, when you see it, according to the manner I have said about its color and length, make the patient sit in front of the sun, and press the tongue with the instrument we described earlier.
puis fiche l’oncine en l’uve, et la trai desoz, et la cope a I des II estrumens que j’ai dit en l’incision des II amandres.	 Then insert the needle into the eye and pull it through, and cut it at the level of the two anvils that I have mentioned in the incision of the two almonds.
Et covient que tu ne coper mie fuer que la superfluiteit qui est outre le termine natureil;	 And you must not cover anything beyond the natural boundary.
car se tu en copes plus, si grieves a la voix, et a la parolle;	 for if you cover more than that, it harms both the voice and speech;
et aprés l’incision, use de ceu que nos avons dit en l’incision des II amandres, et le cure tant qu’elle soit sanee.	 After the incision, use what was said in the incision of the two almonds, and heal it until it is healed.
Et se li malaides a paor dou coper, si covient que tu i use d’engien a la cauterization de li sens paor.	 And if the patient fears to be covered, then you should use an instrument for the cauterization of the senses to alleviate fear.
Et li maniere dou cautere si est aigue ague.	 And the method of cautery is sharp fire.
Et est que li malaides mette son chief en ton sain, et puis li presse la lengue a l’estrument que nos avons dit ou chapistre de cautere, et confis avec aigue vive chaus, si qu’elle ne soit mie trop espesse ne trop clere;	 The patient must put his head in your hand, and then press the tongue against the instrument we have said in the chapter of the fire cautery, and bind it with hot boiling pitch, so that it is not too thick or too clear.
et en emple le chevement de cest estrument, de coi ci est li forme:	 And using the lever of this tool, as follows:
Et ait ou chief une cheveure ou om met la medecine, si com li chevemens d’une cuillier, et met l’estrument a tout la medicine sus l’uve;	 Place one end of the lever on the hair or the medicine and set the tool on top of all the medicine in the eye.
et li malaides soit gisans sus son costeit, si que li salive et li muscillaige corre de sa bouche de la medicine dedens, si qu’ele ne dessende a la gorge, et lou blece;	 And the patient should lie on his side, so that the saliva and mucus flow from his mouth into the medicine, but not to the throat or the nose.
puis tien ta main a tout la medicine et la presse sus l’uve, la quantiteit de la moitiet d’une houre, tant que tu la vois nercie et li mordications de la medicine soit apaisie;	 Then hold the entire medicine with your hand and press it on the eye for half an hour until you see it become swollen and the biting of the medicine is relieved.
et se tu vues, pren coton et l’envoloupe sus aucun estrument, et moille lou coton en la medicine, et boute l’estrument a tout le couton en la cainne desus, tant que li coton s’aerde sus l’uve;	 And if you see, take cotton and wrap it around some instrument, wet the cotton in the medicine, and press the instrument on top of the cotton in the canal above, until the cotton adheres to the eye.
et fai ceu sovent, tant que li cauteres soit parfais, puis la laisse elle seche, et chiet aprés IIII jors ou V.	 And often do this as long as the cautery is perfect, then let it dry, and lie afterwards for 4 or 5 days.
Et se tu as mestier de rencomencier lou cautere de la medicine, si le rencomence, et aprés le cautere l’essue entor l’uve, de couton embut em burre, et mundifie ceu qui est entor de la medicine;	 If you need to repeat the cautery of this medicine, do it again, and after the cautery let the blood flow out around the eye with a swab made of cotton in butter, and clean what is around the medicine.
et soit arosez d’aigue froide, et soit curez de gargarismes tant qu’il soit sanez.	 And it should be anointed with cold water, and cured with gargles until it heals.
Ceste cure est plus save de l’incision, ne que li cautere;	 This cure is better than incision, not the cautery.
s’elle est curee de fumigation selonc ceste maniere, pren calament et ysope et origanum et rue et camomille et avronne et semblans herbes, et les assemble toutes ou aucunes d’eles en I pot, et i met aisil, et fai bullir;	 If it is cured by fumigation in this manner, take camomile, yarrow, rue, and chamomile, and assembled them all or some of them in one pot, add ashes, and make it boil.
et li potz soit bien gluez de fort terre, et enmi le pot ait I estrument cheveit selonc ceste maniere:	 And let the head be well glued with strong earth, and within it have a hair-shaped instrument according to this manner:
Et soit d’argent ou d’arain, et soit li uns des chiés boutez en la bouche dou malaide tant que li vapor monte a l’uve par la caine, tant que li uve soit mortifie;	 And let it be of silver or iron, and push one of the heads into the patient's mouth until the steam rises to the eye through the canal, until the eye is putrefied:
aprés lou rencomence sovent, tant que li uve seche, et garde que tu ne faices ceu au comencement de l’avenement de l’aposteme chaut, car plusors choses i avienent;	 After the beginning often occurs, as long as the eye dries up, and ensure that you do not perform this at the onset of the abscess's eruption, for many things may occur.
et ne faire mie ceu fuer que a la declination d’aposteme chaut.	 and do not perform it before the decline of the hot abscess.
Et se cist estrument n’est presens, si pren une caine et met dedens lou chief une craiffe d’uef, si que li bouche au malaide n’ait mie trop chaut;	 And if this is not present, take a cane and put inside the head of an eggshell, so that the mouth of the patient does not become too hot.
car li craiffe d’uef ne lait mie la vapor grever la bouche, et c’est bone cure ensamble salut.	 for the eggshell does not let the vapor burden the mouth, and it is good care along with health.
Maintes fois s’aert a la gorge os ou espinee de poisson, ou aucune chose;	 Many times it happens in the throat that a bone or fish spine, or any other thing;
si covient donc que tu traies ceu que tu pues veoir, et li presse la lengue au soleil a tout l’estrument, si que tu voies mues la chose;	 therefore you must draw out what you can see, and press the tongue against the sun with all instruments, so that you may see movement of the thing;
et ceu que ne t’apert mie et est reponus en la gorge, covient que tu faices vomir le malaide ainsois que li viande soit cuite en l’estomac;	 And if it does not open by itself and is replaced in the throat, you must make the patient vomit as soon as the food is cooked in the stomach;
par aventure si istra li chose aerse par le vomissement;	 possibly if the matter arises through vomiting;
ou li malaides englutisse une piece d’esponge, ou une piece de navel, ou une racine de laitue, ou I morceil de pain sec;	 or if the patient swallows a piece of sponge, a piece of naval, a radish root, or a dry crust of bread;
et lie a l’esponge I fil, et puis la transglutisse;	 and tie thread to the sponge, then swallow it;
et quant elle venra au leu, si s’aerdra, et puis trairas fuer;	 and when it reaches the place, it will be drawn out, and then you will pull it out;
et s’elle ne vient fuer de ceu que nos avons dit, si pren I estrument de plonc selonc ceste forme:	 and if it does not come out as we have said, take the instrument of yew wood in this shape:
Et soit li estrumens corbés au chief si qu’il puist plus legierement entrer en la gorge, et ait le chief en haut leveit;	 And let the instrument be arched at the top so that it can enter the throat more easily, and let the handle be raised;
et warde que tu ne touchier l’epiglote, que li tous ne li viegne, ne ne bouter mie l’os dedens;	 And beware not to touch the epiglottis, let it remain intact, nor push any bone inside.
et mues vaut que li malaides i boute l’estrument, por ceu qu’il seit mues ou li chose est aerse;	 It is beneficial for the patient to move the instrument, because it must be moved or the thing will be damaged.
si la boute aval, ou il la traie fuer a tout l’estrument igalment, tant qu’elle soit fuer.	 if you push it downward, or pull it out fully so that the instrument is equal on both sides, until it comes out.
de la sansue de la gorge	from the throat vein
Aucune fois est medicinee li sansue, si com j’ai dit en la division, par la cure de medicines;	 Sometimes the juice is used as a medicine, as I said in the division, through the use of medicines.
et quant ceu ne profite mie, adonques regarde en la gorge dou malaide au soleil, puis que tu li presses la lengue a l’estrument que je t’ai dit.	 And when it does not help at all, then look in the throat of the patient towards the sun, then press the tongue against the instrument I told you about.
Et se tu vois la sansue, si la trai a tout I petit uncine, ou as tenailles subtilz que valent a ceu.	 And if you see the blood, draw it out very slowly with a small lancet, or fine tweezers suitable for this purpose.
Et se ceu ne vaut, si pren une caine chevee, et la boute en la gorge dou malaide, puis boute ou chevement de la caine I fer chaut, et fai ce sovent.	 And if that does not work, take a thick cane and push it into the patient's throat, then push or pull on the end of the cane with hot iron and do this frequently.
Et se teigne li malaides d’aigue toute jor.	 And let the patient be treated with water throughout the day.
puis pren plein I voirre d’aigue froide, et oevre la bouche, et la giete ens sens englutir, et la mueve a sa main sovent;	 Then take a full glass of cold water, open the mouth, and pour it in without swallowing, and move it around with your hand frequently.
et si tost com li sansue sent l’aigue, si chiet.	 And as soon as the wound feels cold, it collapses (or falls).
Et s’elle ne chiet si com nos avons dit, si subfumige lou malaide d’asefetide, a l’estrument que j’ai dit en la fumigation de l’uve;	 And if it does not collapse as we have said, you should suffocate the patient with certain means, using the instrument that I mentioned in the fumigation of the eye.
fai ceu maintes fois, car elle cherra sens targier.	 Do this often, for it will heal quickly.
Et li maniere de la fumigation si est que tu preignes I pot ou il ait charbons vis, et soit li pos covert d’un coverseil perciet en mileu, et en celui pertus soit li chiés de l’estrument;	 And the method of fumigation is that you take the pot in which there are hot coals, and it should be covered with a cloth pierced in the middle, and in that place put the head of the instrument.
puis i giete ta fumigation, et li malaides mette lou chief de la cainne en sa bouche, et cloie la bouche, si que li fumee n’en isse mie, mais viegne jusc’a la sansue;	 Then throw your fumigation, and the patient places the head of the cane in his mouth, and closes the mouth so that the smoke does not come out at all, but comes to the nostrils.
et la sansue cherra maintenant, et s’elle ne chiet, si rencomence la fumigation par maintes fois;	 And the nasal cavity should now be filled, and if it does not drip, the fumigation should be repeated many times.
et soffre li malaides soif, et menjuce choses salees et als, et ne boive point d’aigue;	 The patient should suffer thirst, eat salty and sour things, and not drink water.
et adonques li iert mestier qu’elle isse fuer par cest governement.	 And then it will be necessary for the dripping to cease by this means.
Et li forme de l’estrument a coi on trait la sansue, si est, quant on la puet veoir, semblans a tenailles corbés por mues entrer en la gorge;	 And the shape of the instrument with which the nasal cavity is treated is as follows: when it can be seen, resembling curved tweezers to enter the throat.
et ait semblance au bec de soigne, et i ait asperiteit de lime, si que ceu qu’elle prent, elle ne puet lassier;	 And let it resemble a beak of a saw, and it shall have abrasiveness of lime, so that what it takes, it cannot release.
et vez ci la forme:	 And here is the form:
li chapistres des apostemes	The chapters of abscesses
Mout de semblances d’aposteme sont, selonc ceu que li remembrance vient ci aprés d’un et d’autre en cest livre, et sont diver en perforation et en taille;	 Many forms of abscesses are similar to those recalled from this and the other book that follows, and they vary in piercing and cutting.
et c’est en II manieres dont l’une est en sa semblance meisme, et de ceu qu’il tient moistor.	 And it is in two ways, one of which resembles the same, and from what holds moisture.
Et li seconde maniere si est por les leus ou il sont au cors.	 And the second way is for the cavities that are in the body.
car li apostemes dou chief est autres que cil dou fondement, et li apostemes dou leu charnut est autres que cil qui vient en jointures, et chescuns ait son jugement en l’uevre.	 For abscesses in the head are different from those in the cavities, and abscesses in hollow bones are different from those that come at joints, and each has its own judgment in the work.
Et si a apostemes c’on ne doit mie percier, tant que li bowe est meure selonc son acomplissement;	 And if abscesses are not to be pierced, until the bubble is ripe according to its completion;
et si a de telz qu’il covient percier quant il sont crut, et ne meurent mie selonc lor acomplissement, si com aposteme qui sont delez jointures.	 And if of such kind that they must be pierced when they are ripe and do not die according to their completion, like abscesses near joints.
Car quant apostemes vient delez jointures, et on le laisse tant qu’il est porris entor, par aventure si sont corrumput li liien et li nerf de la jointure, par coi ce est cause de contraction en celui membre.	 When an abscess comes near to a joint, and it is left until it bursts around it, in case the ligament and the nerve of the joint are corrupted, this is the cause of contraction in that limb.
Ou li aposteme est delez lou membre principel, et se tu tardes la perforation tant qu’il soit meurez, si nuira au membre principeil;	 For when an abscess is cut open in the main member (body part), and you delay the perforation until it is dead, it will harm the main member.
ou il est delez lou fondement, si le perce on ainsois qu’il soit meurs;	 If the bottom (base) is cut open, then one should pierce it while it is still alive.
et ne covient mie que tu perces aposteme crut sens digestion acomplie, fuers que celui qui est delez lou fondement, qu’il ne porrisse em parfont, et soit alongiez dedens, et i viegne fistule;	 and it is not good that you pierce an abscess without digestion being completed, except for one that is at the bottom (base), which should not perish entirely but should be opened up, lengthened inside, and a fistula should come forth.
et ne puisse saner en grant termine.	 and cannot heal in a long time.
Et covient que tu saiches l’oure de la perforation de l’aposteme qui est meur selonc l’acomplissement, et c’est quant li dolor est apaisie, et li departemens de la fievre, et l’amenuisement de la dolor et de la roujor, et dou debatement et de l’aguisement dou chief de l’aposteme, et les autres signes;	 And it is necessary that you know the time of perforation of the abscess that is dead according to its completion, and this is when the pain is relieved, the disappearance of the fever, the decrease in pain and redness, the subsiding and reduction of swelling and hardness of the abscess head, and the other signs.
et covient que tu faices seoir la perforation ou plus dependant leu de l’aposteme, et la ou il apert mues;	 And you must make it sit (the patient) where the perforation is or more closely to the abscess, and where it has opened up (the wound).
et soit li perforation dou lonc dou cors, et se li apostemes est as mains ou as piez, ou en jointures et au ners et as arteres, et en toz leus igalz ou il n’a point de ploieure.	 And the perforation should be along the length of the body, and if the abscess is at the hand or foot, or in joints and nerves and veins, and in equal places where there is no swelling.
En ces que ploient, par selonc celui membre.	 In those that break, according to the same member. (direct translation)
Et quant apostemes est en leu charnut, si vaut mues que tu laisses la perforation tant qu’il soit confermez en digestion acomplie, si com nos avons dit.	 And when an abscess is in the charnel (or putrid) place, it is beneficial to let the perforation remain until confirmation through complete digestion, as we have said.
Car se tu lou perces devant ceu, si iert alongiez li cors dou venim de lui, et est plains de mout d’ordure;	 For if you pierce ahead of this (the abscess), it should be aligned with the body along the path of the pus, and filled with much filth.
et par aventure endurcissent les levres et li parfondetez de lui.	 And by chance, harden the lips and plunge deeply into it (the abscess).
Et si a aucun aposteme que sont perciet selonc le large dou cors, selonc ceu que li membres en ait mestier.	 And if any abscess that is pierced according to the width of the body, according to what the limb requires.
Et covient que tu amenistres em petis apostemes, petis pertus;	 You must bring small abscesses, small pustules (or boils).
et en grans apostemes, grans pertus, et maintes fendures selonc la semblance de la grandor de l’aposteme;	 And in large abscesses, large wounds, and many splits according to the likeness of the size of the abscess.
et si a de tels apostemes ou il covient chever lou keur, et coper;	 and if such abscesses require incision and covering.
quant il est jai devenus ausi com I drapelz, et est amortis, si covient faire ausi com on fait as bubes:	 when it becomes as a rotten cloth, and is spoiled, you must treat it as one treats babies:
et si a de telz que sont fendut en III angles, et si a de telz dont on cope ausi com la fuelle de mirte, si com apostemes des angres;	 and if such have been cut into three angles or are treated like the thorny plantain, such as swollen abscesses from the armpit;
et si a de telz ou on fait une reonde taille, et autres tailles et semblant copeure.	 and if such have been cut in round shape, or other shapes and seem to be covered.
Cil qui n’ont point de chief, si com aposteme souef superficial, il covient que tu lou perces plainnement;	 Those without a head, like a superficial abscess, must be pierced completely;
et covient quant li apostemes est gros, et il a coillit grant bowe, et tu lou perces, si ne traire mie toute la bowe en celle houre, mais en trai une partie;	 And when the abscess is large and it has collected much pus, and you pierce it, do not draw out all the pus in that hour, but draw out a part of it;
puis estoupe l’aposteme jusc’a l’autre jor, puis en trai aucune chose derechief;	 Then stop the abscess until the next day, then draw out nothing wrongly;
fai ceu par maintes fois de greit en greit, tant que li bowe isse toute;	 do this several times in large amounts, until all the pus comes out;
meismement se li malaides est de foible vertut, ou femme portans, ou petis enfes, ou viez hons decrepites.	 always for a person of weak vitality, or a woman, or small children, or old men in decline.
Car li esperis tressaut aucune fois avec l’issue de la bowe, que par aventure muert li malaides, et tu ne t’en persois.	 The pus may sometimes spasm with the discharge of it, which may happen that the patient dies, and you need not worry.
Eschuez donques cest chapistre par grant cautele, et quant tu as perciet ton aposteme, si essue la plaie, et regarde se li plaie de l’aposteme est petite;	 Therefore, beware of this chapter with great caution, and when you have pierced your abscess, clean the wound, and look if the wound from the abscess is small;
et se c’est une tailleure plainne, si amenistre tentes de lin ou de viez coton;	 And if it is a deep wound, bring in linen or old cotton bandages.
et se c’est uns grans apostemes, et il i a mout de pertus, si covient que tu boutes en chescun une tente si qu’ele viegne l’une contre l’autre;	 And if it is a large abscess with much corruption, then you must pack in each one a bandage so that they come against each other.
et se tu as copeit en l’aposteme une partie dou cuir, et tu l’as cheveit entor, si covient que tu l’emplisses de viel couton ou de rasure de dras de lin sens moistor, et le lie jusc’au tier jor;	 And if you have cut into the abscess a part of the skin and shaved it around, then you must fill it with old cotton or flax reeds without moisture, and tie it until the third day.
puis l’oste, et le cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	 Then open (it) and treat the wound with ointment until it heals.
Et se decorremens de sanc avient a ton ovraige, si amenistre aigue froide et aisil, et moille I drapeil, et met sor le leu decorrant par maintes fois.	 And if bleeding occurs during your work, bring cold water and apply it to the cloth, wetting it repeatedly.
Et se li decorremens de sanc persevere, se i amenistre governement et cure, et les poudres que j’ai dit em mains leus en cest livre, et se c’est ou tens d’iver, et li leus ou li apostemes est est mout nervous, si couvient que tu mettes sus tentes et drapelz moilliez en vin et en oile chaut;	 If the bleeding persists, bring government and care, and the powders that I have mentioned in this book, and if it is winter, and the limbs or abscess are very nervous, then you must put hot wet bandages and linens soaked in wine and oil on top.
et se c’est en esteit, et li leus est charnus, si covient que tu mes sus drapelz moilliez en aigue et en oile, ou en vin et en oile froit, jusc’au tier jor, si com nos avons dit;	 And if it is a dislocation and the joint is fleshy, then you must put it on linen soaked in cold water and oil, or vinegar and cold oil, until the third day, as we have said.
et puis deslie l’aposteme et l’essue et le cure, si com il covient, tant qu’il soit sanez.	 Then drain the abscess, clean it, and treat it, as necessary, until it is healed.
Et ceu covient il conoistre universement en cures des apostemes:	 And one should know universally about treatments of abscesses:
or vos ai dit coment on doit aler avant as cures des apostemes, et vez ci le chapistre.	 Or I have told you how to go before the treatment of abscesses, and here is the chapter.
des soros	of sores
Ou keur dou chief vienent petis apostemes, et sont manieres de nous que sont en toiles, ausi com li josier d’une geline, et mout en i a de semblances.	 For small abscesses coming from the head, there are ways that are in bandages, similar to the bag of a linen sack, and there are many similarities.
Il en i a de gras et de telz ou il a moistor ausi com poulz;	 There are some that are fat and others that have moisture like boils.
et si a de telz qui sont dur et pierous au taillier, et n’i a point de doutance se li artere n’i fait contraire.	 And there are those that are hard and stony at the base, and there is no doubt if the artery does not contradict it.
Et li ovraiges de la taille si est que tu esprueve a tout I estrument qui est apelez «entromissoire», de coi li forme vient ci aprés, quel chose il contient.	 And the work of cutting is that you explore with all instruments called "intermissor", from which the form comes afterwards, what it contains.
Car s’il contient moistor, si lou fent par desus dou lonc.	 For if it contains moisture, they make a long incision.
Et quant li moistor est vuidie, si escorche sens rien laissier la peil qui contient celle moistor, car il revient adés quant on i laisse rien;	 And when moisture is emptied, scrape without leaving any skin that contains the moisture, for it will return again if left something;
puis plonge coton en oignement egiptien, s’il est presens;	 then immerse cotton in Egyptian balm if available.
se ceu non, en aigue et en seil, et en emple la plaie, et la laisse jusc’a l’autre jor;	 if not, use water and salt, and apply to the wound, leaving until the next day.
et ceu corront ceu qui est demorez dou nit.	 and cure those who remain alive.
Et pues rencomence lou coton, si com devant, le second jor, et lou tier, tant que tu saiches bien qu’il ne demoure point dou nit;	 Then repeat the cotton, as before, on the second day, and the third, until you know for sure that it does not remain alive.
puis cure la plaie d’oignement a ceu convenauble, tant qu’il soit sanez.	 then heal the wound with appropriate ointment until it is healed.
Et se li apostemes tient I nout gras, si le cope selonc ceste forme, dou lonc;	 If the abscess remains fatty, press according to this form, long.
et i giete tes oncines, et l’escorche de toutes pars, et met toute ta cure de traire fuer la cotte ou il gist;	 And you throw out your intestines, and strip all parts, and put all your care into drawing force from outside where it lies;
et se li artere te fait contraire, si fai ceu que je t’ai dit aprés.	 If the arteries make you constricted, do as I have told you afterward.
Et ausi fai de l’aposteme s’il est pierous, et dou taillier et dou curer si com je t’ai dit.	 And likewise treat the abscess if it is hard, and of cutting and caring for it as I have told you.
Et li taille sus l’aposteme pierous et le moiste, si est plus legiere, car il sont de poc de sanc.	 And cut above the hard abscess and moist it, it will be easier because there is little blood.
Et si a aucuns de ces apostemes ou chief ou il n’a point de moistor, et de ces fut I apostemes que je copai ou chief d’une vielle femme;	 And if any of these abscesses or boils has no moisture, and these are the abscesses that I treated or boil of an old woman;
et trovai l’aposteme ausi com une piere xourde, aspre et blainche, et ne pooit brisier;	 And found the abscess like a hard stone, harsh and white, and could not burst.
et s’on en eust ferut aucun, on li eust ausi bien fait plaie com d’une piere.	 If they had struck it with anything, they would have made the same kind of wound as from a stone.
En autres apostemes venans ou chief, fuer que ces qui vienent as chief des enfans et as racines des oreilles, li overture si soit toz jors au plus dependant leu, por mues issir la bowe;	 In other abscesses or boils coming from the head or ears roots, they should be opened every day depending on location, to stimulate drainage.
et les cure si com il covient.	 And heal as required.
des scrophules	of scrofulas
Maintes fois avienent cist aposteme au col, et desoz les asseles, et ens angres, et aucune fois vienent autre part ou cors, et sont mout, et sont enjanrees l’une avec l’autre.	 Often this abscess appears at the neck, beneath the chin, in armpits, and sometimes it appears elsewhere on the body, they are swollen and connected with each other.
Et chescune scrophule est proprement dedens sa cote, si com li nout et li aposteme dou chief, si com nos avons dit;	 Each scrofula is properly within its side, just like the knot and the abscess of the head, as we have said.
et les semblances de ces scrophules sont maintes.	 And the appearances of these scrofulas are many.
Il i a de teles que contienent moistor, et si a de malignes qui ne vuellent obeir a santeit.	 Some contain moisture, and there are some malicious ones that do not want to obey health.
en celle donques que tu vois de bone disposition au tochier, et est semblans a la color dou cors, et muet de chescune part et n’est mie aerse as ners dou col ne a l’artere ne au conduit, et n’est mie parfonde;	 In the one that you see with good position on the body, and resembling the color of the body, silent from all parts and not hard at the neck or the artery or the vein, and not swollen.
si covient que tu la copes par desus, et l’escorche de chescune partie, et estent les II levres dou keur as oncines, se tu en as mestier, si com nos avons dit en apostemes dou chief;	 If you see it in this condition, you should cut through the top and peel off each part, and spread the two lips of the incision, if necessary, just as we have said about abscesses of the head.
et la trai poc et poc, et soies seur que tu ne coper lou nerf ne la voine, et ne soit mie li spatumile agus ne trenchans, que li mains n’eschaipe, et ne voise trop avant, que tu ne coper mie ceu que tu ne dois.	 And pull slowly and surely, make sure you don't cover the nerve or the vein, and let it not be the spatula-shaped instrument nor a scalpel that escapes the hand, and look not too far ahead, so as to not cover what should not be covered.
Et se tu copes la voinne ou l’artere, et ceu ne te laisse ovrer, si met en la plaie vitriole broiet, ou aucunes poudres que restainchent sanc, et estraint la plaie;	 And if you cover the vein or artery and it doesn't heal over, place vitriol powder or some stopping powders into the wound, and close the wound.
et la laisse tant que li apostemes soit apaisiez, et soit amollie li plaie, et encomence a porrir.	 And let it be until the abscess is calmed down, and the wound softened, and let it start to rot.
Et quant li sans est estainchiez, si revien a ton ovraige, tant que tu l’acomplisses;	 And when the blood has stopped, return to your work until you complete it.
puis quier a ton doit indice s’il i demoure nules petites scrophules, si les cope et les munde.	 Then, examine if there are any small scrofulas present on your indication, and wash them.
Et s’il a en la racine de la scrophule voinne grant, si ne covient mie que tu copes celle scrophule en sa racine, mais la lie d’un fil double fort, et la laisse cheoir par li, sens nuisement;	 And if the root of the scrofula opens widely, do not cut that scrofula at its root, but tie it with a strong double thread and let it hang through it, without harm.
puis emple la plaie de viel coton plongiet en oignement egiptien, puis la cure.	 Then apply the wound with old cotton dipped in Egyptian ointment, then heal it.
Et se tu copes toute la scrophule, si covient que tu assembles les II levres de la plaie, et les cout maintenant, puis qu’il n’i a point demoreit de superfluiteit por la grandor de la scrophule.	 If you excise the entire scrofula, it is necessary that you bring together the two lips of the wound and sew them now, for there will be no excess remaining due to the size of the scrofula.
si covient que tu entendes a coper la racine de li, et traire fuer, et la cout si com nos avons dit.	 It is necessary that you understand to cover the root and pull out the pus, and sew it as we have said.
Celles scrophules que tienent superfluiteit, perce lai ou il apert meure;	 Those scrofulas that are superfluous, pierce them where they have closed shut.
et la perce ensi com celle devant dite, en dependant, puis i amenistre tentes avec oignement et semblans choses, si qu’elle corrompe ceu qui est demorez de la corruption;	 and pierce them in the same way as the one mentioned above, depending on it, then apply tents with ointment and similar things so that what remains of the corruption is corrupted.
et quant li plaie est bien mundee, si la cure d’oignement enjanrant char, tant qu’il soit sanez.	 And when the wound is well cleaned, anoint it with soothing ointment until it heals.
de squinance	The meaning seems to be about treating a scrofula (a chronic inflammatory condition), specifically when it becomes necrotic (rotten) and needs to be drained and sewn up. The term "de squinance" in the following sentence is not explicitly explained in this text, but it could potentially refer to the same condition or a related one based on the context. Here's the translation for this line:
Li ancien dirent et parlerent de la tailleure de la gorge;	 The ancients discussed the shape of the throat;
mais je ne vis onques en nostre terre qui la feist, et c’est li escripture de lor parole.	 But I never saw anyone in our land who did it, and this is the writing of their speech.
A ces qui ont squinance, il covient que li fendure de la gorge qui est apelee «epiglote» soit eschuee;	 To those with swallowing difficulty (squinance), it is necessary that the choke (epiglottis) be removed.
et c’on ne faice aide par ceu, por ceu que toutes les voines et li pormon dou malaide sont a ces qui ont aposteme chaut en la bouche, ou en la gorge ou en II amandres.	 And this should not be attempted by anyone, since all the veins and the mouth of the patient are near those who have an abscess in the mouth or throat or both.
Quant li maladie est en la chenal dou pormon, il covient coper l’epiglote por fuir la perdition qui vient de l’estranglement.	When the sickness is in the channel of the passageway, it is necessary to cover the epiglotte to avoid the danger that comes from strangulation.
Il covient donques, quant nos volons fendre l’epiglote, que nos le fendons desoz III cercles ou IIII une petite fendure dou travers, entre les II cercles ou par la quantiteit de la fendure dou syfac, ne mie en la cartillaige;	 Therefore, when we want to cut the epiglottis, it is necessary that we cut it below three circles or four, a small transverse slit between two circles or by the amount of the incision according to the size of the hyoid bone (syfac), not in the cartilage;
et cil leus si est covenaubles a la section de l’epiglote qu’il n’i a point de char, et li vasseil sont lonc d’enqui.	 And if the loins are contracted at the section of the epiglottis where there is no cartilage, the veins are long in that area.
Et se li maistres est paourous, si covient qu’il estende le cuir de la gorge a tout l’oncine, puis fende lou keur tant qu’il viegne a la cheneil;	 And if the master is afraid, then it must extend the skin of the throat in full length, then cut the vein until it reaches the trachea.
et eschue les vasselz de sanc, se tu vois aucune chose, et puis cope lou syfac, si com nos avons dit;	 and remove the blood vessels if you see anything, then tie off the vein as we have said.
et est demostrez par la section dou fleume de la cheneil ki saut fuer par le leu qui est rompus, et par la defaute de la voix;	 and it is demonstrated by the section of the trachea that gushes out through the broken place, and by the lack of voice.
et laisse la plaie overte une piece.	 Leave the wound open for a while.
Et quant li houre est passee de coi on doute l’estranglement, assemble les II levres de la plaie dou keur, et la cout toute soule sens la cartillaige;	 And when the hour has passed where there is doubt about strangulation, gather the two lips of the wound around the vein, and sew everything closed except for the cartilage.
puis aministre medicines qui font naistre char, tant qu’il soit sanez.	 Then administer medicines that cause pus formation, while it is healthy.
Albucasim dist c’on ne faice ce jusc’a tant que li gorge est toute estoupee, et li malaides est jugiez a mort, et li defaut li alaine.	Al-Zahrawi says not to do this until the throat is completely stopped up, and the patient is judged dead, and the wings are cut off.
Adonques cope on l’epiglote por ceu que li malaides ne puet alener, et il respire par la plaie, et ensi est gardez de mort;	 Then perform a tracheotomy because the patient cannot swallow, and they breathe through the wound, and thus are kept from death;
et por ce commanderent li anciain a laissier la plaie overte tant que li malice de la maladie soit passee, et elle est passee en III jors ou en IIII Et adonques il comanderent a coudre la plaie et curer, tant qu’elle fut curee;	 and for this reason the ancients would leave the wound open until the evil of the disease has passed, which it will pass within 3 or 4 days. Then they would command to sew up the wound and heal it, until it is healed;
et je vos dirai ceu que je vis.	 And I will tell you what I have seen.
Je vis que une damoisele prist I coutel, et le ficha en sa gorge, et copa partie des chenelz dou pormon;	 I saw a maiden take a knife and stick it in her throat, cutting part of the windpipe;
et je fui apelez por li curer, et la trovai ausi com morte.	 And I was called to heal her, but found her already dead.
Je descovris la plaie, et trovai le sanc qui en estoit issus, et soi bien qu’elle n’avoit mie copeit voine ne conduit fuer que la gorge, et li vens issoit fuer par la plaie.	I found the wound and saw that blood was coming out of it, and I knew that it had neither opened nor conducted air except through the throat, and the veins were flowing through the wound.
Je me hastai, et cousi la plaie, et la curai tant qu’elle fut sanee;	 I hurried up, stitched the wound, and cured it until it healed.
et n’avint a la damoisele fuer qu’elle fut roge de voix, et revint aprés a sa disposition;	 And it happened to the lady that her voice was hoarse, but she returned to her normal condition afterward.
por ceu di je que en la tailleure de l’epiglote n’ait mie paour.	 For this reason, I say that in the case of the epiglottis one should not be afraid.
de la grosse gorge	in the throat.
Cist apostemes est apelez «hernie de gorge», et est uns grans apostemes en color d’une jaisse, et est molt en femmes;	 This abscess is called "throat hernia," and it is a large one with a yellowish color, and it is often in women.
et est selonc II manieres:	 and there are two types of it:
naturez, et accidens;	 Nature and accidents;
ou natureil n’a point d’engien.	 and accidental has no trickery.
Et li accidens est selonc II manieres, de coi l’une est semblans a gras nous, et li autre maniere est semblans a aposteme qui vient de nous d’artere;	 And the accidents are according to two ways, one is like a fatty tissue and the other way is like an abscess that comes from us through an artery.
et il i ait paour, et ne covient mie ovrer de feir fuers que en celi qui est petite, et le prueve et cerche a tout l’intromissoire:	 and there is fear, and it should not be done forcefully except in the small one, and prove and examine carefully at every incision.
se tu le trueves ausi com I nout gras, et ne pent a nulle voine, si le cope, si com on cope les nous, et le trai a tout sa coife, s’il en i a point;	 if you find it as fatty tissue, and it does not have any way out, hit it like one strikes the nose, and draw it out completely, if there is any.
et encerche bien tot, et le cure si com il covient, tant qu’il soit sanez parfaitement.	 and examine carefully in every direction, and cure as necessary, until it is perfectly healed.
des nous	from us
Maintes manieres de nous sont, dont je dirai toutes les semblances;	 Many ways there are of us, which I will tell all their likenesses;
et or covient que je die toute la difference qui est entre nout et issue.	 and it is necessary that I tell the difference between knot and dislocation.
Je dis que issue est chalors et fievre tenans, tant que li ebulicions est passee, et est acomplie li porriture;	 I say that dislocation is heat and fever lasting, until the boil is passed, and the pustule is completed.
adonques repose li fievre et li chalor.	 Then the fever and heat subside.
Avec lou nout n’a ne chalor ne fievre ne dolor, et contient I syfac, qui est ses propres sac et est selonc la color dou cors, et encomence ausi com une jaisse, et devient gros;	 With the knot there is no heat, nor fever, nor pain, and it contains pus, which is its own sac and is according to the color of the body, and begins as an abscess and becomes large.
et sont selonc II semblances, ou grais, ou moiste, et mout de color sont si com j’ai dit en la division.	 And they are like this, either fat or moist, and very much of their color are as I said in the classification.
Il covient, quant tu viens a la cure dou nout, que tu esprueves et l’enquier premierement a tout l’estrument qui est apelez «entromissoire», selonc ce que sa forme venra ou chapistre qui est aprés.	It is necessary, when you come to the treatment of the newt, that you test and examine first everything in the instrument called "entromissoire", according to what its shape comes or the chapter which follows.
Et li maniere de l’inquisicion des apostemes des nous est que tu preignes ou plus moiste leu que tu trueves en l’aposteme, et torne tes dois poc et poc, tant que tu saiches que li estrumens ait perciet le keur, puis que ce soit selonc la grandor de l’aposteme;	 And the method of incision for abscesses is to take or more moist place that you find within the abscess, and turn your fingers little by little, until you feel the instrument has pierced through, then according to the size of the abscess.
puis estrai l’entromissoire, et pren garde en ceu que saut fuer.	 Then extract the contents, and be careful that it does not spurt out.
Se moistor corrans cort, queil color elle ait, si le fent si com j’ai dit des autres apostemes;	 If moisture runs out, let it coagulate, as I have said for other abscesses.
et se aprés l’entromissoire nen vient moistor, saiches qu’il est gras, si le fent donques en croix, et le prent as pinceures, et l’escorche legierement de chescune part et warde la cotte ou il gist que tu la traies saine avec le nout;	 If after extracting the contents no moisture comes out and it appears to be fat, then make a cross-shaped incision and take hold of it with tweezers, carefully peel it off gently from both sides and draw out the sac containing it.
et se tu ne la pues traire saine, si la trai par pieces si qu’il n’i demoure rien.	 And if you cannot draw it out healthy, draw it out piece by piece so that there remains nothing.
Car s’il i demoure rien, si revient li nous par maintes fois;	 For if there remains something, it returns many times;
et s’il en demore un poc, et li sans te grieve, si emple la plaie d’aucunes poudres corrosives agues, et estraint la plaie, et met sus choses apaisans aposteme chaut, et le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez;	 And if a little remains and does not distress you, use the wound with some corrosive powder, hold the wound tight, place something hot to ease the abscess and heal it with other treatments until it is healthy.
et se li nous est grans, si cout les II levres de la plaie, et le cure de ceu qui enjanre char.	 And if the abscess is large, make two holes in the wound, and treat it with lard or other appropriate ointment.
et se li voine batans t’est contraire ou autre si te haste et emple le leu de vitriole broiet, et lou laisse liiet II jors ou III, tant que li plaie porrisse, et repose li ebulicion dou sanc;	 And if the vein beats against you or another, hasten and use broken vitriol on the place, leave it for two or three days until the wound purges, and let the boiling of the blood subside.
puis revien au coper ceu que i est demoreit dou nout.	 Then return to the original state of what has been dislocated.
Vez ci les formes des estrumens entromissoires, et sont de III manieres:	 Here are the forms of the cautery instruments, and they are of three kinds:
grans et moien et petit;	 large, medium, and small;
et s’en i a III quarrez qui sont apelez «albaret», et I qui est apelez «breb», et s’en i a de III manieres:	 And there are three squares that are called 'albaret', and one that is called 'breb', and there are three ways of them:
grant, moien, et petit, por encerchier les apostemes de fistule;	 large, medium, and small, to surround the abscesses with fistulas;
et sont ausi com les aguilles dont on cout les sorceles, et sont d’arain citrin, ou de fer, ou d’argent, et mues valent cil qui sont jaune, et sont plus esprovez de plonc noir por encerchier les corbeures de fistule;	 and they are like the needles with which you sew sacks, and they are of citron wood, or iron, or silver, and those that are yellow are more effective, and they are sharper for surrounding the swellings of a fistula with a black plug;
et sont de III manieres:	 they are of three types:
grans, moiens, et petis, selonc la quantiteit de la largesce des pertus.	 large, medium, and small, according to the width of the wounds.
Les formes des oncines sont de mout de semblances, si com tu vois ci:	 The shapes of the onions are very similar, as you see here:
grans, moiens, et petis;	 Large, medium, and small [things]
et si a oncines qui ont II corbeures de III manieres ausi;	 and if they have one hump with three forms alike;
et si a oncines qui ont III corbeures, et sont ausi de III manieres;	 and if they have three humps, and are the same in three ways;
et si a oncines qui ont II corbeures, et oncines d’une corbeure soulement, et sont de III manieres;	 and if they have two humps, and one hump only, and are of three kinds.
et tuit cist sont necessaire en lor leu.	 and all these are necessary in their place.
Li chief de ces a coi on fent sont trenchant, et de telz i a qui ne taillent mie fuer que d’une part, dont on escorche les nous, por ceu c’on ne cope la voine ne le nerf;	 The head of these things is sharp, and those who do not cut at all from one side, which we scrape the nails with, because one does not strike the vein or the nerve;
et de ces intromissoires sont les alemeles reponues en mainches, si que li malaide ne s’en persoivent a l’overture des apostemes;	 And from these incisions the ulcers are tied up in bands, so that the patient does not harm himself at the opening of abscesses.
et sont de III manieres:	 They are of three kinds:
grant, petit, et moien, si com tu vois;	 large, small, and medium, as you see.
et n’en use on mie fuer que en leu charnut, si com jambes, et bras, et mameles, et as angres, et en semblans leus;	 Only use it in the flesh of a man, such as the limbs, arms, breasts, and in similar places.
et aucune fois fait on I autre estrument petit, semblant a escorces de fistices, selonc ceste forme, a coi on estainche sanc:	 And sometimes another instrument is made small, resembling fists of plasters, in this form to drain blood.
et le met on aucune fois au leu qui saine a copement des voines, et as arteres, et aucune fois reont selonc ceste grant forme:	and it is placed at the site that heals quickly, at the veins, and sometimes returns according to this large form.
Aucune fois enflent les mameles d’aucuns homes quant cil encomencent estre corrumput, tant qu’eles semblent mameles de feme;	 Sometimes the breasts of some men swell when they begin to rot, until they resemble breasts of a woman.
et demorent laides et enflees, et qui les vuet curer, si le covient soier selonc ceste forme des ceste ligne .b. jusques a .g.:	 They remain ugly and swollen, and whoever wishes to cure them, it must be done according to this form of the line b.j to g.
puis escorche la graisse, et emple la plaie de medicine enjanrant char, puis assemble les II levres de la plaie a costure, et la cure tant qu’ele soit sanee;	 Then scrape off the fat, apply medicine to the wound with soothing balm, then bring together the two edges of the wound for stitching, and heal it until it is healed.
et se li mamele cline aval, et est amolie por sa grandor si com il avient as femmes, si la fent en II costelz desus, par II semblans fendures;	 and if the limbs bend downwards due to their size, like it often happens in women (when they become wide), then divide them into two pieces above, with two similar cuts.
de coi l’une soit tenans a l’autre a la fin de l’une et de l’autre, si que li plus grans ligne conteigne la menor selonc ceste forme, des ceste ligne .b. jusc’a la ligne .g.;	 in this way one piece will be holding the other at the end of both pieces, so that the larger piece encloses the smaller one according to this shape, from this line "b" up to the line "g".
puis escorche le cuir qui est entre les II levres, et oste la graisse, et i amenistre ceu que nos avons dit de costure et de poudres, et ceu qui est necessaire en la cure, tant qu’il soit sanez;	 then scrape the skin between the two pieces, remove the fat, and apply what was said about stitching and powders, and whatever is necessary for healing, until it is healed.
et s’il n’est sanez, ou li incision n’est mie toute faite, por ceu que li malaides ne vuet reposer, ou por le decorrement de sanc, si covient que tu emplisses la plaie de coton moilliet en oignement corrosif;	 If the patient is not healthy or if the incision is not fully made because the patient does not want to rest, or due to bleeding, you must fill the wound with cotton wadded in a corrosive ointment.
et le laisse tant qu’il menjuce le remenant et la graisse, puis le cure tant qu’il soit saneis.	 And let it heal as it consumes the remaining meat and fat, then treat it until it is healed.
des apostemes des asselles	From abscesses of the saddle (a type of boil)
Cist apostemes que vienent desoz les asseles sont manieres de scrophules dures ou il ait cotes, et s’en i a que contienent moistor.	These abscesses that come under the saddle are types of hard scrofulas with ridges, and if they contain moisture within them.
Cil donques qui contienent moistor covient qu’il soient copez selonc ceste forme, des la ligne .b. jusc’a la ligne .g.:	 Therefore, those containing moisture should be cut according to this form, from the line b up to the line g:
Et quant toute li bowe qui est en l’aposteme est vuidie, si emple la plaie de viel coton, et la laisse jusc’a l’autre jor, puis oste tout le coton, et cure d’oignement avenant a ceu tant qu’il soit sanez.	And when the whole boil which is in the abscess is emptied, place old cotton on the wound, and leave it until the next day, then remove all the cotton, and apply an ointment to it until it heals.
Et se li apostemes est de semblances de scrophules, si le fent si com nos avons dit en fendures des scrophules, et se li plaie rent bowe, si amenistre cautere si com nos avons dit devant.	And if the abscess resembles scrofula, make incisions in it as we have said for scrofula, and if pus forms in the wound, apply fire cautery as we have said before.
de la routure de l’artere	of the cutting of the artery
Quant li artere est route, et li cuir est soudez qui est sus, si en vient maintes fois apostemes, et tout aussi avient il a la voine enflee et aposteme;	 When an artery is cut and the skin above it becomes sutured, there often occur abscesses, and the same happens with a vein that swells and forms an abscess.
et si le conoist on ensi quant c’est por l’artere, si est li apostemes lons em parfont;	 And if it is recognized in this way when it concerns an artery, the abscess will be long and deep.
