et covient qu’il mette le cornet de l’estrument au desus, et qu’il teigne l’estrument.	 And you should insert a cotton swab into it and stain the wound.
Et quant li apostemes apert, et on lou fent a la main mol, si le covient coper au chief, au spatumile leit;	 When an abscess opens and it is soft to the touch, it should be covered with linen cloth and treated with sputum.
et quant li bowe est vuidie, si covient que tu mettes en la plaie tentes moillies en oile roset, ou en oile vert sec;	 And when the bladder is emptied, you should place soaked and oiled linen bandages or dried green oil-soaked linen in the wound.
et met la tente fuer de la plaie au parfont de la marris, et met par defuer sus la marris et sus le poignil lainne nette moillie en aigue ou malves soient cuites;	 Place the linen fabric deep into the wound, place it outside the wound and above the wound a clean linen bandage moistened with vinegar or honey.
puis le cure aprés II jors d’oignement avenant a ceu, tant qu’il soit sanez;	 Then treat it after two days of ointment application, when it is healthy.
et aucune fois leve on la marris et la plaie par clistere d’aigue et de miel, et puis d’aigue ou racines de lis et aristologe longe soient cuites;	 And sometimes lift the wound and the limb with cleansing of water and honey, then with water or licorice roots and long arum roots are boiled.
puis reveigne a l’oignement.	 Then return to ointment application.
Et se li plaie est reponue en la marris, si covient que tu te gardes de cuire de fer, mais cure la si com nos avons dit en la division.	 And if the wound is healed in a marriage (scar tissue), you must be careful not to burn it with iron, but rather treat it as we have said in the previous section.
de l’enfantement	Of childbirth
Mestier est premier a la baile qu’elle conoisse la figure de l’enfantement natureil, et li signes si est quant tu vois la femme apresser aval, et desire odorer l’ar:	 Firstly, in delivery, it is necessary to recognize the signs of natural childbirth, and when you see the woman dilate down below, and desire to smell the area.
adonques se haste li enfes de fuer issir;	 Then the child hastens to be born.
adonc saiches que cil enfantemens est selonc la figure natureil, et est li issue soz son chief, et li secondine avec lui;	 Then you recognize that the delivery is natural according to its form, and the infant comes out with its head, and the afterbirth follows.
et quant tu vois ces signes, si covient presser legierement son ventre, si que li enfes isse tost;	 And when you see these signs, it is necessary to gently press on his stomach so that he urinates quickly.
car quant il dessent sus son chief, si ist li secondine avec lui, et est mondee li marris de ses superfluitez par bone mundification;	 for if he is vomiting on his head, then the child is born with him, and the husband cleanses himself of his superfluidities through good cleansing.
et cist qui vient autrement ne vient mie naturelment.	 and this that comes in another way does not come naturally.
Car il vient aucune fois sus ses piez, et vient fuer li cors ou li chiés, et les mains, ou il vient sus son ventre, ou sovin, et est convertis par aventure sor son col, et par autres figures malvaises;	 For sometimes it comes on his feet, and the intestines or shoulder, or hands, or on his belly, or backside, and is turned by accident on his neck, and in other bad forms.
si est mestier a la baile qu’elle soit saige et subtilz en ces choses, et se warse d’error et de decevement, et je vos mostrerai toutes les figures coment on li doit aidier.	 it is necessary to consult with someone wise and skillful in these matters, and beware of error and deception, and I will show you all the forms of how to help them.
Se li enfes vient sus son chief par issue natureil, et li femme enfante griement, et li vertus de li est foible, si la fai seoir sus une selle, ou les femmes la tienent;	 If the child comes out naturally on the head, and the woman gives birth with difficulty, and the strength of the child is weak, make her sit on a saddle, or let the women hold her.
et arose sa nature d’oile ou fenugreic soit cuit, et puis boute li baile entre ses dois le petit spatumile dont ci est li forme:	 and mix its oil or fenugreek with boiled water, and then insert the little spatula-shaped plaster into the mixture:
et fende la secondine, et cope a son ungle tant que li moistors qui est ens corre fuers;	 and cut the second skin, and scrape it with your nail as far as the moisture that is inside escapes;
et preint lou ventre de la femme tant que li enfes dessende, et s’il ne dessent, si covient clisterizer la femme de muscillaige de fenugrec avec oile de sisament;	 and bind the woman's belly until the child descends, and if it does not descend, then you must cleanse the woman with muslin of fenugreek and oil of mummy:
puis la fai preindre et esternuer de condisi, et tien sa bouche et son neis une houre:	 then make her bind herself and fast for forty days, and hold her mouth and nose for an hour:
si istra maintenant l’enfes.	 Instructions for the thigh.
Et se les II mains issent fuer, si covient que tu les ramoinne legierement poc et poc;	 If the hands come out (of the joint), you must gently pull them back a little at a time.
et s’elles n’i puent entrer, si met la femme sus I siege, et li lieve les piés en haut;	 and if they cannot go in, place the woman on the bed, and lift her legs upwards.
puis deboute le siege sus terre, et teigne on la femme, qu’elle ne chiece au deboutement;	 then tilt the bed onto the ground, and bind the woman so she does not slide when tilting it downwards.
et se li mains n’i puet entrer, et li enfes muert, si li cope les mains au couteil qui est ci devant mis, et estrai l’enfant, et ramoine igalment.	 and if the hands cannot go in and the thigh is dead, cut the hands with the knife placed before you, extract the child, and reset the dislocation evenly.
de l’issue de l’enfant sus ses piés	 of the birth of the child upon its feet
Quant li enfes vient sus ses piez, si lou covient bouter en haut;	 When the thigh comes upwards on its legs, push it upwards.
et puis le torne poc et poc, tant qu’il soit igalz;	 and then turn it a little at a time until it is level.
puis preigne I des piez et l’estende poc et poc.	 Then take the piece [of bone] and extend it little by little.
Cant il saut jusc’as cuixes, si la comande a preindre, et la fai esternuer de condisi;	 If it can jump up as high as the hips, command him to take hold of it, and make it vomit out with force.
si saut fuer, se Deus vuet.	 if it jumps forward, may God will it.
Et s’il n’ist fuer si com nos avons dit, si le torne poc et poc, tant qu’il soit selonc la figure natureil.	And if it is not as we have said, turn it bit by bit until it is according to the natural shape.
Car adonques ist il legierement.	Then it will be easily.
Et s’il ne vient fuer si com nos avons, dit si pren muscillaige de altee, et oile de sisament, et gomme fondue, et broie tout en I mortier;	 And if it does not jump forward as we have experienced, say take mustard of great height, oil of cumin, and melted resin, and grind them all in the mortar.
et met sus la nature de la femme dedens et defuer cest oignement, puis la fai seoir en aigue tede jusque desoz les costelz;	 and place the nature of woman inside it [the mixture] and spread this ointment outside, then make her sit in a cold bath until below the ribs.
et quant elle est moillifie desoz, se li fai I coliere de mirre, et li met desoz, et li laisse une houre;	 and when she has been softened [by the bath], apply the collar of myrrh to her, put it on, and leave it for an hour.
puis la fai seoir sus I siege, puis la fai esternuer et estraint sa bouche et son neis, et li preint le ventre legierement, car li enfes saut maintenant.	 Then make him sit on the chair, then make him cough and hold his mouth and nose, and he shall gently press his stomach, for the child is about to be born now.
de l’issue de l’enfant sus ses genous	of the child's excrement over its knees
Quant li enfes vient en ceste forme, si i mette li baile ses mains poc et poc;	 When the baby comes in this way, place the midwife's hands here and there.
puis soit sovinee sus son col, et li pendent li piez aval, et soit gisans sor I lit;	 Then support his neck and hang his feet below, and he lies on the bed.
et plie ses mains poc et poc, et puis li preint les mains sus lou ventre, et li oste les cussins desoz, tant qu’elle soit appareillie aval;	 Fold her hands here and there, then hold her hands above on the stomach, and push the cushions aside until she is prepared below.
et se li enfes ne saut, si pren ses piez et li muef forment, puis li muef lou ventre amont, puis i boute tes mains;	 If the child does not come out, take its feet and pull it gently, then push the stomach upward, then put your hands there.
et ewe l’enfant poc et poc;	 Pull the baby little by little.
et comande a la femme qu’elle se preigne tant que li enfes isse.	 Command the woman to take herself when the child is issued.
de l’issue de l’enfant qui vient dou large une main pendant	From the delivery of the child that comes forth with one hand wide.
I covient engignier a ramener la main:	 It is necessary to skillfully reattach the hand.
s’on ne la puet ramener, si fai lever la femme, et aler;	 If you cannot reattach it, make her stand up and go.
s’elle ne puet aler, si la fai gesir sus I lit, et li deboute les jambes forment;	 If it cannot walk, place it on a bed, and bend its legs.
puis amenistre lou muscillaige que j’ai conteit;	 then administer the mustard plaster as mentioned before;
et s’elle n’enfante, si la fai seoir sus I siege, puis estudie au rameneir la main;	 and if it does not give birth, make her sit on a chair, then study to bring back the hand.
et ewe l’enfant selonc la figure natureil, et la fai esternuer, et li comande qu’elle se preigne tant que li enfes isse fuer.	 and deliver the child according to its natural shape, make it vomit, and tell her to hold it until it becomes firm.
de l’issue de l’enfant sus son col, et ait espandues ses mains, et sa faice tornee devers lou dos sa mere	Of the birth of the child on its neck, and if it has spread its hands, and its face turned towards the back of its mother.
I covient que li baile teigne sa main, puis le torne poc et poc, et l’ewe legierement;	 You must press its hand, then turn it little by little, and extract it gently.
et quant il est igalz, si met sus la nature muscillaige de altee et oile, si com nos avons dit, puis li comande qu’elle se mueve poc et poc;	 and when it is equal, place the natural mustard plaster of high altitude and oil on it, as we have said, then tell her to move little by little.
et quant tu avras ce fait, si la fai seoir sus I siege, et li comande k’elle se preigne;	 And when you have done this, make her sit on the chair, and command her to take hold of herself.
et la fai esternuer.	 Make her vomit.
de ceste meisme maniere a tout la secondine	in the same way, support her all the second time.
Quant il vient fuer en ceste maniere a tout la secondine, si cope la secondine a ton ungle, tant que li moistors soit vuidie;	 When the feces come out in this manner for all the digestion, take the feces with your nail until the moisture is voided.
et se li enfes pent sus sa faice et sus son col, si la cope des la boude, qu’elle ne soit retenue, et muere li enfes;	 And if the infant presses against its face and neck, take it by the buttock so that it is not retained, and let the infant die.
puis boute l’enfant dedens, tant que tu l’aies mis si com il covient, et comande a la femme qu’elle se preigne aucune fois:	 Then push the child back in, as much as you have placed it, and command the woman to take hold of herself once.
adonques si istra legierement.	 After that, pull it gently.
de l’issue des gemelz	of the issue of twins
Saiches que gemeil naissent maintes fois, et aucune fois en naissent III ou IIII;	 Know that twins are born often, and sometimes four or five are born at once.
et ceu n’est mie estrainge chose, et poc avient.	 And this is not a strange thing, happening often.
Dui sont estrainge chose, et ne vivent mie, se poc nom;	 Dislocation is an issue arising from any disjointment of its place, which prevents it from moving, and the limb is misaligned, causing the patient great pain and injury. The head of the shoulder dislocates due to moisture, and when it is reset but cannot stay in place, repeatedly dislocating with slight movement as we have experienced, then you must first reset the dislocation. In the work of this chapter, there is often the evacuation of blood when opening a vein, and incising an abscess, and in the treatment of wounds, and in the extraction of arrows, and in cutting into stones, and similar things; where there is doubt and fear, many die. For in the fire cautery, instruct the patient to let the hairs grow long and even; and if they prick at their base, hold the eyes steady so they do not move until they grow. And this is not a strange thing, often happening.
je sai ceu, qu’il soient multipliiet, et sont desevrez par lou syfac qui les devise, qui est liiez a la boude;	 I know that they multiply and are driven away by the leech who discovers them, which is tied to the bowl.
et aucune fois issent ausi naturelment com uns tous sous, si com nos avons dit.	 And sometimes they emerge naturally like teeth under the skin, as we have said.
Et s’il issent griement, si la cure si com nos avons dit, et soit li baile subtilz, et faice tost et legierement ceu qu’elle fait;	 And if it [the dislocation] protrudes forcefully, treat it as we have said, and let the balm be subtle, and do quickly and gently whatever it does.
et faice ensi com il vaut mues a salut.	 and perform such actions that bring salvation.
de plusors enfans	of many children.
Aucune fois sont formez en la marris I ou II ou III ou IIII ou V ou VI ou VII, ou plusors jusc’a XV, et sont tout formeit en forme d’enfant par le mesurement dou saige glorious, et couvient que li baile saiche tout ceu, car par aventure semblans chose li avient;	 Sometimes they [dislocations] are formed in the hand or in the foot or in the arm or in the thigh or in the back or in the chest or in the neck, or more often up to the fifteenth, and they are all formed like a child by the measurement of the sage man, and it is necessary that the balm knows all this, for sometimes similar things happen.
si faice selonc ceu qu’il covient.	 do as it requires.
de l’enfant mort	of a dead child.
Quant tu cures la femme de l’enfant mort ou ventre, si com j’ai dit en la division, et il ne vient fuers, et tu es constrains d’ovraige de mains;	 When curing the woman of a dead child or an empty womb, as I have said in the division, and it does not come out naturally, and you are forced to work with your hands.
si covient que tu saiches se li femme est de saine vertut, et n’ait accident ou elle ait paor de mort;	 It is necessary that you know if the woman is of good health, and has no illness or fear of death.
si covient que li femme soit sovinee sus son dos, et soit ses chiés enclins aval, et les jambes levees;	 The woman must lie on her back, with her head inclined downwards and legs raised.
et li ministre la teigne de II pars, ou elle soit liie au lit si qu’elle ne soit traite au dessendement de l’enfant;	 The minister should hold her by both arms, or tie her to the bed so that she is not treated in the delivery of the child.
puis frotez la bouche de la marris d’oiles moistes avec muscillaige de altee et de fenugrec et semence de lin, puis oigne li baile ses mains de ces oiles et de ces muscillaiges;	 Then anoint the mouth of the woman with moist oil mixed with myrrh and cumin, and then anoint the midwife's hands with those oils and musks.
puis les boute en la marris legierement, puis quiere I leu ou elle boute les oncines que soient covenaubles a ceu, et pren warde se li enfes est apparilliez qu’il dessende sus son chief;	 Then push gently into the woman, seeking the place where she pushes out the afterbirth that is suitable for this purpose, and be careful that the infant is prepared to be delivered on top of its head.
si fiche les oncines en ses eulz ou en son col ou en sa bouche ou en som palais ou desoz la barbe ou en la forcele ou pres des costez, et se li dessendemens est sus piez, se li fiche ou poignil et as costes moienes;	 If the onions are inserted into his eyes or neck or mouth or palate or under the beard or in the armpit or near the sides, and if the insertion is below the nipples, it is pierced or pricked and the sides are injured.
et covient qu’il teigne l’oncine a sa main destre, et mette la corbeure entre ses dois de la senestre main, et li boute a tout sa main legierement, et fiche l’oncine en aucun de ces leus que nos avons dit, tant qu’il viegne a la chose vuide;	 And it is necessary that you squeeze the onion with your right hand and place the shell between your left hand fingers, and push it gently to the full extent of your hand, and pierce the onion in any of the places mentioned above until it reaches an empty state.
et c’est li forme de l’oncine:	 and this is the form of the onion:
puis fiche encontre I autre oncine, ou le tier se tu en as mestier, si que li estractions soit igalz;	 then pierce it opposite the other onion, or the third if needed, so that the extraction is equal.
et puis l’estent igalment en movant d’une part et d’autre, por mues issir, et soit li oncines dentez por mues tenir, si com ci est li forme:	 And then equal it by moving from one side to the other, so that it moves out, and hold the humerus (upper arm bone) in place with teeth, as shown in this figure:
Et s’il en demoure une partie, si oigne li baile aucuns de ses dois d’oile, et les boute en celle partie, et traie l’autre partie;	 And if there remains a part of it, the healer should press some oil from his fingers and push that part into it, and pull the other part.
et s’il en i demoure point, si met cest oncine ou plus haut leu, et fai ceu tant qu’il s’en isse tout fuers.	 And if there remains no part, place this splint or higher up, and continue until it completely comes out.
Et se l’une mains vient devant l’autre, et il ne puet ramener por l’estreignement, si covient que tu envoloupes sus I drapeil, tant qu’il isse tote;	 And if one hand comes in front of the other and cannot be returned by squeezing, then you must wrap around it with cloth until it comes out completely.
puis la cope en la jointure de la plante ou au coute, et ensi covient que tu faices en l’autre main, et as II piés.	 Then put the thumb in the joint of the flat part or at the side, and you should do the same with the other hand to both feet.
Et se li chiés de l’enfant est gros et il est estrois en l’issue, ou il ait ou chief aigue assemblee, si covient que tu boute le spatumile espinous entre tes dois, et fent le chief et estrai l’aigue;	 And if the child's head is large and it is narrow at the birth canal, or if there is a sharp assembly of the head, then you must thrust the pointed spatula between your fingers, and push and draw out the head;
ou tu la ront a l’estrument qui est apelez «almidach», de coi li forme vient avec les estrumens ou chapistre qui est aprés cestui;	 or you grind it with the instrument called "almidach," from which the form comes with the instruments or chapter that follows this one;
et ensi meisme faice se li enfes a grant chief naturelment;	 and in the same way do so if the infant has a large head naturally;
et puis traie fuer les osses as tenailles, et se li chiés saut fuer et il estraint a la forcele, si soit fendus, tant que li moistors qui est ou pis issue fuer;	 then pull out the bones with the pliers, and if the head pops out and it is held by force, it should be cut until the moisture that is in or near the birth canal is removed;
et s’elle ne puet issir, si le cope par pieces au mues que tu pues;	 and if it cannot come out, you crush it into pieces where you can.
et s’il est enflez au ventre ou desoz les costez, si covient que tu lou perces tant que li moistors corre.	 If [the patient] is swollen in the belly or beneath the ribs, you must pierce it until the moisture subsides.
Et se li enfes est sus ses piez, si est li attraction legiere, et li adrecemens a la bouche de la marris est legier.	And if the child is on its feet, it is a light attraction, and the direction towards the mouth of the womb is gentle.
Et s’il est estrois au ventre ou au pis, si couvient que tu l’estraies a I drapeil envoloupeit sus la main;	 If [the swelling] is hard to the touch or over the ribs, you must probe it with your hand.
et fent le ventre ou le pis, tant que li moistors qui i est corre;	 And they make the abdomen or the anus, as long as the moisture inside it is corrected;
et se li autre membre sont osteit, et li chiez demoure, si boute li baile sa main em parfont de la marris, et le traie jusc’a la bouche de la marris;	 And if another member has been broken and the joint remains, then push the bale's hand fully into the incision of the hernia, and pull it out until it reaches the mouth of the hernia;
puis i boute I oncine ou II, et le trai fuer;	 then insert one finger or two, and pull forcefully;
et se li bouche de la marris est retrecie por aposteme chaut qui i est venus, si n’i covient mie travillier, ains covient amenistrer choses moistes et grasses;	 and if the mouth of the hernia is narrowed due to hot abscess that has come there, then it is not necessary to work on it, instead, you should provide moist and fatty substances;
et li amenistre emplaustres, et siece en aigue mollifians et amoistans.	 and apply plasters, and soak in warm, softening, and moistening substances.
Et se li enfes est sus son costeit, et tu le pues mettre igal, si amenistre ceu que nos avons dit en l’enfant vif;	 And if the intestines are on the side, and you can place it evenly, then apply what we have said in the live child.
et s’on nen ait pooir, si lou trai fuer par pieces, et n’i laissier rien de la secondine.	 And if they do not have power over it, pull it apart into pieces, and leave nothing of the remaining part.
Et quant tu avras ce fait, se li amenistre ceu que nos avons dit ens apostemes chaus que vienent en la marris;	 And when you have done this, apply as we have said in abscess poultices that come during marriage.
et se decorremens de sanc vient, si soit mise en aigue restraignant, et li amenistre autres cures.	 And if bleeding occurs, bind it tightly and apply other treatments.
Et je vis une femme en cui ventre uns enfes avoit esteit mors, puis consut .i. autre sus celui, et refut mors li autres.	I saw a woman whose womb had been dead due to an infant being born, then another one was placed on top of it, and the death of the other was prevented.  (This line is referring to the survival of a second fetus after the first fetus died in the womb)
Aprés lonc tens li vint uns apostemes en la boude, et enfla tant qu’il ovrit, et comensa a grant porreture.	After a long time, an abscess came into the armpit, and swelled until it opened, and began to suppurate greatly.
je fui apelez a la cure, et i pensai lonc tens, et ne pot soder li plaie.	I was summoned for treatment, and for a long time, I could not heal the wound.   (Literal translation)
Je mis sus emplaustre de fort attraction, et en issit uns os, et aprés aucuns jors uns autres.	I applied a strong adhesive plaster, and an bone came out, and after some days another one did.
Je me mervillai mout, por ceu c’ou ventre n’a point d’os.	I marveled greatly because the stomach has no bones.
Si pensai que c’estoit des os d’un enfant mort.	If I think it is the bones of a dead child.
Je quis la plaie, et en traï mains os, tant que li femme fut em millor point;	 I wish to treat the wound, and remove the bone as much as the woman is in a better condition.
et vesquit li femme lonc tens ensi, et issoit adés un poc de bowe dou leu;	 And if the woman recovers for a long time, then a small amount of vinegar on the wound can be applied.
et je n’ai recordeit cest chapistre fuer que por ceu que, quant li maistres trueve une estrainge chose, qu’il i saiche mettre aide.	 And I have never heard this chapter to be for any other reason than when the master finds something strange that he knows how to treat.
dou ramener la marris a son leu	To bring the dislocated joint back to its place
Ci aprés vient li forme dou pressor, a coi on ewe les livres;	 Here comes the form of the pressor, which is used in books;
et a II tornans as II chiés des II liiens.	 and turning the heads of the ligaments.
Toutevoie, li cornes soit plus subtilz dou restrictoire, et soit fais de ebene ou de bux;	 However, the horns should be more subtle than the restrictor, and made of ebony or boxwood;
et soit li bouche dou fust I doi de large, et li marge des arbres I doit, et de lonc une palme et demi;	 and the mouth of the rod should be wide, and the sides of the trees should be, and long one and a half palm;
et enmi les II liemens soient dui ajostemens de cest meisme fust, qui soient fermeit en l’un et en l’autre, de demi palme de lonc ou un poc plus;	 and between the two ligaments there should be two joints of this same rod, which are fastened on both sides, half a palm or a little more in length;
et cist dui ajostement sont bouteit en la bouche de la marris por ovrir quant on torne les II cornes.	 and these two joints are pushed into the mouth of the mallet to open when turning the two horns.
Une autre forme, a sa semblance plus subtilz et plus legiere, soit faite de fust de ebene ou de bux, selonc la semblance des tenailles;	 Another form, resembling more subtle and lighter, should be made of rod of ebony or boxwood, as the resemblance of pliers;
et ait as II chiés II ajostemens, si com tu vois, d’une palme de lonc, et II dois de large;	 and tell the patient to make two shoulder rests, as you see, of one palm length, and two fingers width.
et quant tu vues ovrir la marris a tout l’estrument, si fai seoir la femme sor I lit, les piez pendant et les jambes overtes, puis boute les II ajostemens ajostez ensamble en la marris, et tien le chief de l’estrument desoz entre ses cuixes;	 and when you are about to open the woman's privates with all the instruments, make her sit on the bed, legs hanging down and knees apart, then place the two shoulder rests beside her in the opening, and hold the head of the instrument under her thighs.
puis oevre ta main a tout l’estrument, si com tu as fait as tenailles igalment, selonc la quantiteit que tu vues ovrir la bouche de la marris, tant que li baile faice ceu qu’elle vuet.	 then take your hand with the instrument and make equal incisions, according to the amount that you see the opening of the woman's privates requires, until the man does what she wishes.
Cist estrument sont tuit sormontez, et sont multiplies lor semblances;	 This instrument is covered entirely and has multiple similar forms.
et quant li mires les ait apareilliez, tant est plus hastans li oevre, et plus haute as homes por lor quantiteit.	 And when the mirrors have been prepared, the work becomes more urgent, and higher for humans because of their quantity.
Si ne despire mie l’estrument que tu ne l’aies apparelliet, car lor necessitez n’est mie escusauble.	Do not disperse the instrument unless you have arranged it, for its necessity cannot be excused.
Quant li secondine est retenue a l’enfantement, si covient que tu comandes a la malaide qu’ele reteigne son alaine, et puis la fai esternuer de condisi, et li estraint tes mains a la bouche et au neis;	 When the afterbirth is retained during childbirth, you must instruct the patient to hold back her breath and then make her vomit bile, and then hold her hands at her mouth and nose.
et s’elle saut per ceu, bien est.	 If she jumps due to this, it's good.
Se ceu non, si prent I pot, et fai I pertus ou cuvercle, et i met herbes que puissent ovrir la bouche de la marris, si com calament, rue, anis, camomille, cassialigne et centoire;	 If this doesn't happen, take the pot, and make it perforated or covered, and put therebs that can open the mouth of the mother, such as rue, anise, chamomile, wormwood, and centaury.
toutes ces herbes, ou aucunes d’eles, soient cuites ou pot en aigue sus le feu;	 All these herbs or some of them should be boiled in water on the fire;
puis met une caine ou pertus dou pot, et l’autre chief en la bouche de la marris, et la teigne tant que li vapors viegne dedens la marris;	 Then put a chain or pipe through the hole (pot), and hold the other end in the wife's mouth, and heat it until the vapors enter the wife.
puis la fai esternuer, si com nos avons dit.	 Then make her vomit, as we have said.
Si saut li secondine hastanment.	Then immediately apply the second one.
Et s’elle remaint aprés ceste cure, et n’ist mie fuer, si comande a la baile qu’ele moille sa main senestre en oile de sesement ou en muscillaige de altee, et puis la boute en la nature, et quiere la secondine;	 And if she remains after this cure and does not defecate, as commanded by the lady, tell her to moisten her left hand in oil of sesame or musk-scented water, and then apply it to nature (anus) and encourage her to defecate again.
et quant elle l’avra trovee, si la preigne et l’estende poc et poc droitement, si que li marris ne chiece a l’estraction;	 And when she has found it, take it (feces) and stretch it out little by little, so that the wife does not object to extraction.
mais la covient movoir legierement a destre et a senestre, et puis traie;	 But you must move it gently from right to left, and then pull it.
si venra et se desaerdra.	 If it comes out (of place) and dislocates.
Et se li bouche de la marris est jai estrecie, nos avons dit la cure d’esternuer, et de fumigation des herbes;	 And if the mouth of the womb is stretched out (dilated), we have said the treatment for expulsion (miscarriage), and the fumigation of herbs.
et s’elle n’ist de tout ceu que nos avons dit, si garde que tu ne foloies au traire;	 And if it is not all as we have said, make sure you do not pull (on the fetus).
mais il couvient que ceu qui est a la bouche de la marris, que tu le lies a la cuixe de la femme, puis la clisterize d’oignement tetrafarmaçon;	 But it is necessary that he who is at the mouth of the womb, you tie him to the woman's thigh, then cleanse (the area) with a pessary ointment.
si la porrira et remettra, et venra fuer;	 If it gives birth and comes forth (the baby).
mais toutevoie, quant elle porrist si en vient male odor au stomac et au chief, et blece la malaide.	 However, if she gives birth but a bad smell comes from the stomach and head, burn the patient.
Si covient donques fumigations covenaubles a ceu:	 Therefore, it is necessary to use appropriate fumigations for this:
aucun des anciens ont esproveit fumigation de cresson et de figues seches.	 any of the ancients have tried the fumigation of dill and dried figs.
Li forme de l’estrument a coi on fumige la femme a la retenue des flors et de la secondine si est ceste:	The form of the instrument with which one fumigates the woman to retain the flowers and the afterbirth is as follows:
Et est de voirre semblant a une caine, et met on le chief subtil en la nature, et les chiés larges sus le feu;	 And it appears like glass, and put the thin head in the nature [i.e., the fire], and the broad parts above the fire.
et soit li fumigations sus les charbons, et la teigne tant qu’elle soit gastee, et rencomence une autre.	 and let the fumigation be over the coals, and let the tar be burned until it is spoiled, and start another one.
de percier lou fondement	To pierce the foundation.
Maint enfant naissent qui n’ont mie le fondement perciet, ains l’ait estoupeit uns subtilz syfac:	 Many children are born who do not have the foundation pierced, but rather closed with some subtle stopper.
si covient donques a la baile qu’ele perce celui syfac a son doit, et ne lou perce mie de spatumile agut, et garse le lacement qu’elle ne le touche;	 therefore, at the birth it is necessary to pierce the stopper with a suitable tool, and not with a sharp stylus, and make sure that the afterbirth does not touch it.
puis met sus lainne moillie en vin et en oile, puis la cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	 Then put a soft linen cloth soaked in wine and oil on it, then treat with ointment until it heals.
Et se tu doutes qu’il ne restoupe, si met ou pertus une caine de plonc, et li laisse mains jors, et soit ostee quant li enfes vuet aler en chambres.	If you doubt that it will not reform, then put or pierce a plaster of lead, and let it remain for many hours, and remove it when the wound appears to heal in rooms.
Et aucune fois vient cist estoupemens de soudement de plaie ou d’aposteme;	 And sometimes this stoppage of a sudden wound or abscess comes...
si covient coper celui soudement:	 you must cover the sudden wound:
si soit curez, si com nos avons dit de la caine de plonc.	 if it is treated, as we have said of the willow bark poultice.
de la fistule dou fondement	of the fistula from the foundation
Fistules qui vienent desoz le fondement sont nodation, et groissor que vienent delez lou fondement defuer, ou en l’espaice des II parties, si a une fistule ou plusors;	 Fistulas that come under the foundation are nodes, and those that come out from under the foundation and go in the space between two parts, or more than one fistula;
et quant celle nodation est anciene, si aoeuvre, et encort moistor awouse blainche ou subtilz bowe, et aucune fois sont ces fistule persans;	 and when that node is old, it works, and also moisture awakens swelling or subtle boils, and sometimes these fistulas are persistent;
et sont conues par ceu qu’il en ist ou egestion ou ventositeit quant li malaide fait egestion, et par aventure en saut uns vers.	 And are recognized by those who are aware of either evacuation or windiness in the patient when he makes an evacuation, and possibly jumping a step.
Et si a fistules que percent jusc’a la vessie, et jusc’a la moitiet de la verge;	 And if the fistulas that perforate reach up to the bladder, and up to half of the penis;
et parvienent jusc’a la jointure de la cuixe, et jusc’a nout de la kowe.	 and reach up to the knee joint, and up to the ankle of the leg.
Et ensi conoist on la fistule persant au fondement, et ne mie persant:	 And thus, one recognizes a fistula persisting at the base, but not persisting:
et est que tu boutes ton doi indice ou fondement, et boute une aguille subtil d’arain ou de fer en la fistule quant il n’i a tortuositeit.	 and it is that you insert your index finger or base into the fistula, and insert a fine needle of ivory or iron into the fistula where there is no twisting.
Et s’il ait tortuositeit, si i boute une tente de plonc subtil, ou I poil de cheval, tant que tu sentes la tente ou le poil a ton doit;	 If it has twisting, then you insert a tent of fine fabric, or horsehair, as far as you feel the tent or hair on your finger.
et se tu ne le sens, et il ne vient dou pertus egestion ne ventositeit ne ver, si com nos avons dit:	 And if you do not understand it, there will be no purulent discharge, no windiness or worms, as we have said.
saiches qu’elle ne perce mie;	 know that it does not pierce at all;
si te haste dou curer.	 hurry in the treatment.
Et quant li fistule est persans jusc’a la vessie ou jusc’a conduit de l’urine, si en saut li urine, et ne puet soudeir par medicines.	And when the fistula is open up to the bladder or up to the channel of urine, if it gushes out urine and cannot be sealed with medicines.
S’elle est percie jusc’a la jointure de la cuixe, si est li tente venans jusc’au leu;	 If it is pierced up to the knee joint, it is coming out at the level.
s’il n’i a tortuositeit et li invention de la dolor entor, si est qu’il en ist adés bowe, et n’i vaut medicine ne soudement par oignement;	 if there is no curvature and the pain disappears around it, then it is already bowed, and neither medicine nor salve will help.
et en ces fistules persans n’a point de cure fuer que labor, et vaniteit des folz mires qui s’en entremettent.	 And in these Persian fistulas, there is no remedy except hard work and the folly of those who meddle with them.
En celle qui n’est mie persans et n’est mie anciene, a esperance de saniteit par fer, si com j’ai esproveit, et est que li malaides gise entre tes mains sus son dos;	 In those that are not Persian and are not old, in the hope of health through fire, as I have experienced, the patient lies on his back before you.
et li lieve les jambes jusque sus ses cuixes, et ait ses cuixes enclinees a son ventre;	 And raise the legs up to the thighs, and have the thighs inclined towards the stomach.
puis boute une tente d’arain, ou de plonc s’il i a tortuositeit, tant que tu saiches ou li tente vient.	 Then push a tent of pitch or wood, if there is curvature, as far as you know where the dislocation comes from.
Se li malaides la sent entor le fondement, si covient que tu i boutes ton doi indice, se sens adonques que li tente l’ait perciet;	 If the patient feels it around the base, then you must push your index finger in, then if it feels as though the dislocation has passed.
et soit descoverte ou tu sens entre ton doit le syfac ou la char, adonques saiches qu’elle est persans;	 and be discovered or feel through your finger the socket or the bone, then know that it is passed.
si n’i travillier mie c’on ne la puet saner.	 if one does not work it no can heal it.
On dist toutevoie c’on em puet bien saner aucuns, mais ce avient poc;	 It is said that one can heal some, but this happens rarely.
et li aide c’on i fait, si est c’on eschaufe le cautere subtil selonc la largesce de la fistule, si com il est devant dit;	 And help that one does, if it is heating the cautery thinly according to the width of the fistula, as it was said before.
et le boute tout chaut en la fistule, tant qu’il viegne delez le fondement;	 And push everything hot into the fistula, until it comes out from the bottom.
et faice ceu II fois ou III, tant que tu saiches que ces chars fautrees soient arses, qui sont semblant a une penne d’oiseil;	 And do this two or three times, as long as you know that these charred objects resembling a bird's feather should be burnt.
et puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre, tant que celle chars isse fuer, puis le cure d’oignement enjanrant char et soudant.	 And then heal it with moistened tents in butter, until the charred object is gone; then heal it with ointment made of burning char and resin.
S’il est ensi sanez, c’est bien.	 If it is thus healed, it is well.
Se ceu, nom autrement ne puet estre sanez;	 If this cannot be healed otherwise;
et se li tente entre, et ne perce jusc’au doit qui est ou fondement, et a entre ton doi et la tente une coverture espesse de char ou de syfac, et tu vois la fistule a ceu qui enseut la coverture dou keur;	 and if the tent penetrates but does not reach the bottom where the fistula is located, place a thick covering of charcoal or soap between your finger and the tent, so that you see the fistula through the cover made from charcoal.
si le cope des l’encomencement de la fistule, et boute adés avant la tente, et pues le cautere aprés, tant qu’il viegne au chief de la tente;	 If the head of the fistula at its beginning, advances towards the tent and then applies the cautery afterwards, until it reaches the tip of the tent.
et sera delivré li tente, et cherra;	 The tent will be released, and pulled out.
puis mondefie celles chars fautrees que semblent une penne d’oisel, et n’en remaigne niant.	 Then cut away those hardened charred areas that resemble a bird's feather, and nothing remains.
Et si li sans te vaint, et cort entre toi et l’uevre, si le cauterize de feu ou de medicine ague.	And if the limb goes away by itself, and breaks through [the skin], you shall cauterize it with fire or medicine.
Car li cauteres de feu assemble II bones choses:	 For the fire cautery brings about two good things:
c’est a savoir, l’arsure de ces chars ajostees, et l’esteinchement de sanc et la sechor de la moistor;	 which is to say, the burning away of these hardened areas that are joined together, and the stopping of blood and the drying out of moisture.
puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre ou en choz broiez, tant que li leus giete bowe, et isse fuer li chars arse en la bowe;	 Then treat moist tents with butter or coarse oatmeal until the limbs swell, and the charred areas burn in the butter or oatmeal.
puis cure la plaie des oignemens soudans enjanrans dure char, et sont les medicines seches.	 Then treat the wound with ointments made of hard charcoal, and these are the dry medicines.
Car quant il est restoree, si est sanee et ne revient mie.	And when it is restored, it heals and does not return.
Et se fistule vient jusc’a parfont dou fondement, et est esloigniez dou cors, se li boute ton doi ou fondement, et enquier ceu.	If a fistula comes up to the full depth of the foundation and is removed from the body, push your finger or foundation into it, and examine it.
Se tu sens la tente, et entre II est li toile ou li syfac ou chars, ou il est pres a percier, si n’i ait fuers que voie de fiance et d’esperance, par l’aministrement de l’une des III manieres:	 If you feel tempted, and between them is the cloth or linen or charcoal, which is almost to be pierced, there should not be outside it any means of deceit and false hope, by the administration of one of the three ways:
ou tu le cauterizes si com nos avons dit, ou tu le cope jusc’a fons, ou se tu pues si i met tentes et cure si com premier;	 or you cauterize it as we have said, or you strike it to the bottom, or if you can boil it and treat it as first recommended.
et n’aler mie trop em parfont, que tu ne coper le tenement qui tient le fondement, et viegne li egestions par lai sens volenteit;	 and do not go too deep, so that you cover the foundation holding structure, and let the exudations come out through the will of the wound.
puis le cure, si com nos avons dit;	 then treat it as we have said.
par aventure si sera sanez, ou tu esloigne celle coverture et la munde puis qu’elle est copee delez lou fondement, ou par tente ou par autre estrument apointé;	 By chance, if it is healthy, remove that covering and clean it when it is cut away from the foundation, either by force or by some other instrument pointed.
puis mondefie cele char fautree qui est en la plaie, tant com tu pues;	 then disinfect the infected flesh in the wound as much as possible;
puis estudie a restorer la plaie, et a demorer la fistule en la partie defuers le fondement:	 then study to restore the wound, and keep the fistula in the part farther from the foundation.
si iert plus legiere chose au malaide.	 if it is easier for the patient.
Et aucune fois sont fistules selonc ceste maniere:	 And sometimes fistulas are like this:
et est quant tu boutes la tente en la fistule, et elle est ou costeit dou fondement delez lou cuir desus, si pren une tente percie au chief selonc ceste forme:	 and when you push the tent in the fistula, it is where it touches the foundation of the skin above, take a pointed tent like this shape:
Et i boute .i. fil tort en .ij., et boute la tente a tout le fil en la fistule tant qu’il soit au chief.	And insert one twisted thread into two, and push the tent with the whole length of the thread through the fistula as far as it reaches on the head.
S’elle est persans en la marge dou fondement dedens, adonc estrai lou fil de celui pertus, ensi que tu boutes ton doi ou fondement;	 if it is pierced in the margin of the foundation inside, then pull out the thread of that perforation, so that you push your finger or foundation.
et trai le chief dou fil, et assemble les II chiés ensamble, et estraint l’un a l’autre, et le laisse I jor ou II;	 And draw the head with thread, and bring together the two shoulders together, and hold one to the other, and leave it for a day or two.
et le restraint aucune fois, tant que li filz cope ces chars que sont entre dous, et chiecent;	 And keep it restrained until the threads hold the joints that are between together and heal.
puis cure la plaie tant qu’elle soit soudee et sanee.	 Then heal the wound until it is healed and sound.
Se li fistule ne perce, si la fai percier en toutes les manieres que tu pues, s’ele n’est trop em parfont.	If the fistula does not burst on its own, make it burst in all possible ways, unless it is too deep.
Car il ne covient mie faire por le lacement coper si em parfont, et puis le cure, si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	For it should not be covered with a plaster if it is too deep, and then heal it as we have said, until it is healed.
Li forme dou spatumile espinous dont on fent la fistule si est mout agus d’une, part et trenchans;	 The shape of a spindle with spikes for making a fistula is very sharp at both ends and cuts.
et d’autre part non, por ceu c’on ne cope mie ceu c’on ne doit mie copeir, si com tu vois ci:	 And not sharp on the other side because one should not hit what one should not hit, as you can see here:
des emorroydes	hemorrhoids
Emorrydes sont selonc II manieres:	 The emoires are according to two kinds:
ou elles sont dedens le fondement, ausi com grain de resin, et s’en i a petites et grans, et en cort adés sanc, et s’en i a une ou plusors, et sont defuer le fondement et au chief dou fondement;	 or they are inside the foundation, like resin, and there are small and large ones, and near the surface there is blood, and there is one or more, and they are pushed away from the foundation and at the head of the foundation.
mais celles qui sont defuer si ont poc de moistor, et encort adés ou un poc d’aigue citrine ou un poc de sanc, et ont la color dou cors;	 But those that are dislocated have little moisture, and yet there is still some citron juice or blood, and they have the color of the body.
et li cure de ces qui les ont dedens le fondement, si est que tu comandes au malaide qu’il s’espreigne por aleir en chambres, tant que li fondemens li isse fuer, et c’aperent li filz;	 And the treatment of those with them inside the foundation, is that you instruct the patient to strain for urine in rooms, until the foundation subsides and the urine appears.
si te haste, et le pent as tenailles, ou tu le tien a ton ungle, puis le cope en ses racines;	 hurry up, and pierce it with tweezers, or hold it with your nail, then strike at its roots.
et se li uncine ne les pueent tenir por ses moistors, si les prent a I drapeil, ou a couton, ou d’une piece de chamelot;	 and if the tweezers cannot hold it because of moisture, take a cloth or cotton, or a piece of camel skin.
et les estrai a tes dois, puis les cope, et poudre desus aucunes chaudes poudres que soient en leu de cautere;	 stretch them with your hands, then strike and sprinkle some hot powders in place of the cautery.
ou tu les cauterize si com il est dit ou chapistre de cautere, pues les cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez;	 or you cauterize them as said in the chapter on cautery, afterwards you treat them with other treatments until they are healed.
et se li fondemens ne puet issir, si clisterize le malaide de clistere mordant et aspre por laver ceu qui est ou fondement, si qu’il puist issir apertement;	 and if the foundation cannot come out, you must clisterize the patient with biting and harsh clisteria to clean the area where the foundation is, so that it can come out openly.
cant li malaides se preint, et se li fil sont fuer dou fondement, si est li cure legiere;	 but if the patients do not prepare themselves, and if their threads are too long for the foundation, the treatment is easy.
et est que tu les preignes a ton ungle ou as tenailles, et les cope, puis les cure si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez, et qu’il redoute l’incision par fer.	 and it is that you grab them with your fingernail or pliers and break them, then treat them as we have said, until they are healed, and until they fear the incision by iron.
Si covient que tu amenistre la costure selonc ceste maniere:	 It is necessary that you make the stitching in this manner:
pren I fil tort, et le boute en une aguille, et puis trai le fil au desus et fai percier l’aguille d’autre part, et torne les II chiez dou fil desoz l’aguille, et si soit dou large;	 Take the twisted thread and stick it in a needle, then pull the thread above and pierce the needle from another side, and twist the two ends of the thread below the needle, making sure it is wide enough.
et estraint le fil forment, puis noe le fil, et estrai l’aguille, et fai ensi de toz les autres, et en laisse I por corre la superfluiteit dou sanc;	 and straighten the thread, then knot it, pull out the needle, and do the same for all of them, and leave some space for blood flow.
puis met sus le fondement I drapeil moilliet en oile roset ou en cerote, et met sus le fondement, et comande au malaide k’il repose;	 then place the damp cloth soaked in rose oil or wax on the foundation and cover it, and instruct the patient to rest.
et puis le laisse tant qu’il chiecent, et quant il seront cheut, si les cure d’oignement et d’autre cure, tant qu’il soit sanez.	 and leave it until it stops bleeding, and when it has stopped, heal the wound and other treatments until it is healed.
dou sechement dou fiens ou fondement	the drying of the wounds or foundation
Maintes fois avient sechement de fiens en l’intestine, et par constrignement de nature, et quant li maladie est vielle et medicine n’i vaut.	Often the drying of wounds occurs in the intestines due to natural constriction and when the disease is old and medicine no longer helps.
Si covient que tu reses a la point d’un spatumile ou a ton ungle l’escorce desus, qui ne le laisse a moistir;	 It is necessary that you scrape off the skin with a spatula or your nail, so it doesn't become wet.
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sodez si com il covient;	 Then heal him when he becomes healthy as needed;
et s’il ne puet soder, si rencomence la rasure plus fort que devant, tant qu’il saine mout, et soit escorchiez;	 and if it cannot heal, then start the shaving more forcefully than before, until it heals well, and blisters;
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	 Then heal him when it becomes healthy.
dou fremit	great trembling
Formice est une petite apparance fautree antor le cors, et va mout em parfont;	 Fissure is a small appearance hollowed out before the body, and goes in deep;
et aucune fois la trueve li frois, et le sent on ausi comme mort de fremit, et vient en tout le cors, et plus as mains que autre part.	 And sometimes it strikes the breast, and one feels it like death trembling, and spreads through the whole body, and more in the hands than elsewhere.
Et li cure si est que tu pren une cainne d’une penne d’oie, ou une penne de vultul fort, et met celle caine sus le fremit, tant que li cercles porpreigne le fremit tot entor;	 And the treatment is that you take a reed from an ostrich feather or a strong bird feather, and place it on the trembling, until the purple circles encompass the trembling everywhere;
puis torne ta main a tout la cainne tant que tu copes tout entor le fremit, et le met em parfont, et esraiche le fremit de ses racines.	 Then turn your hand all around the neck until you grasp it entirely; and put it in fully, and pull out the neck from its roots.
Et se tu vues, si fai ceu d’une caine d’arain ou de fer selonc ceste forme, et soit subtilz desoz et traians desus:	And if you wish, do this with a chain made of iron or steel according to this form, and be careful beneath and pull above.
ne mie perciet, por mues tenir au doi, et mues presser.	 Do not pierce, rather hold tightly and press.
Et se tu vues, si cauterize lou fremit, si com il est devant ou chapistre de cautere.	 And if you see, cauterize the neck, as it is described in the chapter on cautery.
de la forme dou clistere	of the shape of a clyster
Aucune fois fait on clistere d’argent ou d’archaut, ou d’arain fondut ou mailliet;	 Sometimes, one does a silver or pitch clisterium, or melted wax or plaster.
et aucune fois fait on de ces estrumens petis et grans, selonc ces a cui il sont amenistrez.	 And sometimes they make these small and large instruments, according to those for whom they are made.
Cil donques c’on amenistre en la cure des enfans et qui sont foible et dolorous, sont petis.	Therefore, when it is used in the treatment of children and those who are weak and suffering, they are small.
Li forme dou clistere petit et grant si est desus large, ou li ventres est liiez selonc ceste maniere:	The form of the enema, whether it is large or small, should be above wide, or the belly should be bound in this manner:
et i ait une desevrance ou li ventres soit liiez, si com tu vois, et li chiez soit dedens perciez;	 and there should be an opening or the abdomen tied, as you see, and the head inside pierced;
et ait a l’un des costez II pertus, et en l’autre I;	 and on one side they should be punctured, and on the other.
et soit li ventres ou om met les medicines d’une vessie de beste ou de parchemin, et soit perciez tout entor de menus pertus, et ait entre chescun pertus I doit d’espaice, puis boute en ces pertus I fil fort de fil crut tort en X ou enqui entor, et assemble le ventre si com est une chievre;	 And let the belly or the one put the medicines from a beast's bladder or parchment, and it should be pierced all around with small holes, and there should be space between each hole, then put strong thread through these holes, twisted in X or around, and assemble the belly like a goatskin.
et quant li medicine est dedens, si la lie a l’estrument devant d’un fil fort, puis clisterize;	 And when the medicine is inside, tie it with a strong thread to the instrument in front, then cleanse (it).
et c’est li forme dou cercle:	 And this is the shape of a circle.
Et soit li medicine ne trop chaude ne trop froide, et oint le chief dou clistere d’oile ou d’aubun d’uef, ou de semblant chose, puis le boute ens legierement;	 Let the medicine not be too hot nor too cold, and anoint the head of the cleansing cloth with oil or egg yolk, or similar thing, then put it gently inside.
puis l’espreigne li ministres a ses II mains ensamble, tant qu’il soit toz vuis, puis estrai lou clistere, et lieve li malaides ses jambes a la paroit, et se li medicine vuet issir, si la teigne tant com il puet;	 Then the minister pulls it out with both hands until it is completely visible, then remove the cleansing cloth, and make the patient lie on his back, and if the medicine appears, press it as much as possible.
et s’il dort une nuit atot, si est plus grans aide.	 And if (the patient) sleeps for an entire night, it is (more of) help.
Et se tu le clisterizes em maladie de decorrement de ventre, et li medicine se haste d’issir, si le rencomence tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if you cauterize it in case of disease of the intestines, and the medicine hastens to heal, keep applying it until it is healed.
Et se li emorroide sont ou fondement, ou aposteme, si soit li clistere ausi subtilz com por I enfant;	 If the hemorrhoids are either foundation or abscess, then let the enema be as subtle as for a child.
et c’est li forme dou clistere subtil sus coi li cuir soit estraint:	 and this is the form of the subtle enema when the skin is tightened:
des plaies	wounds
Nos avons jai dit en la division la cure des plaies;	 We have said in the division, the treatment of wounds.
or vos dirons les cures de mains et de medicine, selonc l’acomplissement.	 Or you will be told about remedies for hands and medicine, according to the completion.
Je dis que les plaies sont diverses selonc ceu qu’elles sont faites, et selonc les leus ou les plaies sont faites, et de coi elles sont faites.	I say that wounds are diverse according to what they are made, and according to the places or wounds where they are made, and from how they are made.
Les choses par coi plaies sont faites sont par gitement de piere, et taille d’espee et de couteil, ou de lance ou de fust ou de siette, ou de semblans choses;	 Things by which wounds are made are by impact of stone, cutting with swords and knives, or spear or staff or arrow, or similar things.
ou que sont faites selonc les leus dou cors, si com plaie que chiet sus le col, ou sus le chief, ou le peis, ou le ventre, ou le foie, et semblans membres;	 or those that are made according to the rules of the body, such as wounds that fall on the neck, or head, or chest, or stomach, or liver, and similar limbs;
et je vos dirai la cure de chescune plaie, et encomencerai as plaies dou chief simples, car li remenbrance venra en son chapistre.	 I will tell you the treatment for each wound, and I shall begin with the simple wounds of the head, for this reminder will come in its chapter.
Je dis que quant simple plaie vient ou chief, et li os n’est brisiez, si pren garde se c’est de gitement de piere ou de semblans choses, et li cuir est toutevoie rompus et est li plaie grans, et tu doutes levement d’aposteme chaut:	 If a simple wound occurs on the head and the bone is not broken but it has been caused by an arrow or similar things, and the skin is completely torn and the wound is large, you doubt the formation of an abscess; warmly incise it:
si le fai tantost sainier de la cephalique meismement s’il vient poc de sanc de la plaie, et soit li sainie au contraire de la partie navree;	 immediately make it drain from the head itself if blood comes a little bit from the wound, and let it drain in the opposite direction of the damaged part:
et eschuisse li malaides repletion de vin et de viandes grosses.	 remove the patient's bloating caused by wine and heavy food.
Et s’il ne vuet sainier, si soit amenuisie sa viande, et ne boive point de vin, ne ne menjuce point de char;	 If it does not want to drain, let the patient's meat be reduced, and let him not drink wine, nor eat meat.
et met sor la plaie, se apostemes chaus i vient, coton moilliet en oile roset soulement, ou en vin stiptice;	 And place it on the wound if an abscess comes up there, cotton wool soaked in rose oil only, or in stiptic wine.
et s’il n’i a aposteme chaut, si met sus la plaie, s’elle est fresche a tout son sanc, et elle n’est muee par l’air, poudre, que je dirai un poc ci aprés;	 If there is no abscess, place it on the wound if it is fresh with all its blood and not moving due to air or wind, I will tell you what kind of powder a little later.
et se li ars l’ait muee, si met sus aucuns oignemens, tant qu’il soit sanez.	 And if the wound has moved due to fire, place some healing herbs on it until it heals.
Et se li plaie est grans si com de tailleure d’espee et de semblans, et les levres ne se pueent assembler par tentes, si les assemble par cousture, si com je dirai as plaies dou ventre, de la costure.	And if the wound is large like the size of a sword and cannot be closed with stitches, join them by sewing, as I will explain for abdominal wounds.
Se li plaie est descoverte de l’os, et pent, et ne tient mais que a un poc, si le cope;	 If the wound is opened to the bone, fleshy and does not hold together, bind it up.
puis cure la plaie de medicine, et restoure char dure en leu de cuir, et comande au malaide a mengier grosses viandes, si com testes et froment cuit, ausi com poulz, et semblans choses.	 Then treat the wound with medicine, replace tough flesh where there is skin, and instruct the patient to eat thick foods such as cooked tests (beans) and wheat, also cabbages and similar things.
Et se tu trueves ou cuir porriture, et il n’aert a l’os, si cope lou porrit tot, et giete fuer, puis le cure;	 And if you find or cut through corruption that is not bone, strike it all with the knife and throw away the rotten part, then heal it.
et se il ait artere en la plaie ou voine, dont sans cort, et il ne puet estainchier par medicines, si quier l’artere, et se tu la trueves desloie, si la lie d’un fil;	 If there is an artery in the wound or vein that cannot be stopped with medicine, then tie it and if you find it dislocated, tie it with a thread.
et se ceu ne profite mie, si la cauterize.	 And if that does not help, cauterize it.
Et se ces plaies sont petites et simples, si est li cure legiere:	 If these wounds are small and simple, the healing is easy.
et est que tu mettes ens ceste poudre qui soude ainsois que li ars l’ait muee.	 And you put this powder that causes the flesh to heal as soon as the worm has moved it.
Et li maniere de la poudre si est:	 The method of making the powder is:
pren encens une partie;	 Take incense one part;
sanc de dragon II parties;	 dragon's blood two parts;
chalz vive III parties, et le poudre subtilment, et emple la plaie, et l’estraint forment, tant qu’elle s’aerse bien et se joigne a tout son sanc;	 Live flesh in three parts and apply the fine powder on the wound, and hold it open shaped, until it dries well and joins all its blood.
et puis la lie bien, et la laisse sens desliier, s’elle n’enfle;	 And then tie it up well, and let it heal by itself if it does not swell.
car on n’oste la madicine tant qu’ele soit sanee.	 because the medicine is not to be stopped until it heals.
Et aucune fois fait on ceu de chalz soulement, quant on n’ait l’encens ne lou sanc de dragon, mais que li ars n’ait muee la plaie.	And sometimes they do this with just boiling water, when there is no incense or dragon's blood, but the wound has not yet opened.
Et se li ars ait mueit la plaie, meismement en esteit, si n’i met om mie ceste poudre;	 And if the wound has moved [healed], in that case do not put this powder on it;
mais met sus aucuns oignemens digestis, ou poulz de farine d’orge faites d’aigue et de miel, tant qu’ele giete bowe;	 but place some digestive herbs or barley flour made with water and honey on it until it is healed.
puis le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	 Then heal it with other treatments until it is healed.
Et se li brisure d’os vient avec la plaie, et elle est petite, si l’estrai as pinceures subtilz;	 If a bone break comes with the wound and it is small, remove it with fine tweezers;
et je vos dirai ci aprés les brisures dou chief.	 And I shall tell you after the fractures of the head.
de la plaie dou col	Of the collar wound
Se plaie vient ou col et elle est simple, si n’a point de difference entre li et celi dou chief, mais se li ners dou col ou li artere est copee.	If the wound comes from the neck and it is simple, without a difference between it and the one on the head, but if the nerve of the neck or the artery is cut.
Se c’est li ners, si n’i a autre engien que laissier la cure, et n’i mettre nulle chose restraignant, car il nuit as ners et les fait retraire;	 If it is the nose, there is no other remedy but to let it heal naturally and not put anything binding, because it harms the nose and makes it retreat.
et ne mettre sus la plaie rien froit, car li substance des ners est froide, et li continuation d’aus si est avec le cerveil, qui est li plus haus membres;	 And do not put anything cold on the wound, because the substance of the nose is cold and its continuation with the brain which is the highest member.
mais soit li medicine souez, si com chalz lavee en aigue douce, et mellee avec oile roset, et cucie lavee ausi en aigue douce, et autres pieres de mine selonc ceste maniere, et oignemens moistes.	 But the medicine should be soft like boiled chalk washed in sweet water and mixed with rose oil, and also boiled and washed again in sweet water, and other similar stones moistened in this manner.
Et se li plaie est grans, si la cout et lie de bendes, puis la cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if the wound is large, tie it up with strips, then treat it until it heals.
Et se les plaies sont parfondes et ele est chevee et pleinne de bowe, si la perce ou plus bas leu;	 And if the wounds are deep and swollen and full of pus, pierce or cut it lower.
et se li artere est copee, et decorremens de sanc en vient, si la desoivre, et la loie, et la cauterize se mestier est;	 And if the arteries are cut, bleeding occurs, then tie it off, and cauterize if necessary.
et se li espinee de la gorge est copee, ou li keurs, et li conduiz est gardez, par coi la viande va, si cout le keur sus la cainne de la gorge, et ne touchier la gorge mais la remet selonc sa figure naturel;	 And if the spine of the throat is cut or glands, and the conduit is kept, so that the meat goes, then keep the gland above the throat's cartilage, but do not touch the throat, instead return it to its natural shape.
et puis l’estraint avenanment, et le laisse aucuns jors, puis le cure d’oignemens desechans tant qu’il soit sanez;	 Then apply traction gradually and leave it for some days, then heal with hot poultices until it is healed.
et se li plaie a fait empression en l’os, si la quier;	 And if the wound presses into the bone, open it.
et s’il i a pieces d’os, si les trai fuers toz se tu pues, et ces que tu ne pues avoir, si laisse tant que li plaie porrisse, et soit desevree et aligie li issue;	 And if there are bone fragments, pull them out entirely if possible, and those you cannot remove, leave until the wound is healed and the opening is even.
et se li plaie est fresche, si poudre sus la poudre que j’ai dit.	 And if the wound is fresh, sprinkle the powder I have mentioned on it.
Et s’il a en la plaie os et il i a fistule, si la cure ensi com j’ai dit en son chapistre.	And if there is bone in the wound and it has a fistula, treat it as I said in its chapter.
de la plaie de lance ou de coutel	Of a wound from a lance or knife   (This line suggests that the text is discussing treatments for wounds inflicted by weapons.)
Se c’est cop de lance ou de coutel, et li plaie est parfonde, si regarde se de la plaie saut ventositez cant li malaides alainne:	 If it is a spear or sword wound and the wound is deep, check if gas escapes from the wound when the patient breathes in:
saiches adonques que li plaie est mortelz;	 Therefore, know that the wound is lethal;
et s’elle n’est parfonde, et elle est fresche a tout son sanc, si n’i mettre mie a la premiere houre la poudre, ne ne la liier mie por le sanc que ne demorse em parfont, et reviegne au cuer, et ocie lou malaide;	 And if it is not penetrated through and the wound is fresh with all its blood, do not put any powder on it immediately or bind it because the blood will dissolve it and return to the heart, killing the patient.
mais i met oignement atractif, et le lie II fois le jor;	 but apply an attracting ointment, and reapply it twice daily;
et se tu n’as oignement, si met en la plaie viel coton por succier fuers la moistor, et fai dormir le malaide sus la plaie III jors, ou IIII, ou plusors;	 and if you don't have an ointment, place a piece of old cotton on the wound to draw out moisture, and make the patient sleep on the wound for three or four days, or more;
si n’i venra mie spasme, ne tremor male de cuer n’estraingnemens d’alainne;	 if no spasm or severe tremors of the heart or any kind of coldness comes on.
et quant tu vois les bones dispositions, si saiches que li plaie est sauve.	 And when you see good positions, know that the wound is healed.
Cure la donques de tentes et d’autres cures, tant qu’il soit sanez;	 Then release it from bandages and other treatments until it becomes healthy;
et s’elle ne puet saner, et oevre, adés saiches que il i a fistule;	 If it cannot heal, then open it, from now on know that there is a fistula.
si la cure si com on doit.	 Treat the wound as it should be treated.
Et se li plaie est d’incision d’espee ou de coutel, et elle est simple, ou pis ou au dos, si la cure de ceu qui est devant;	 If the wound is from a sword cut or knife, and it is simple, or worse, on the front or the back, treat the one in front.
s’elle est grans, de cousture;	 If it is large, stitch it up.
et s’elle est petite, de poudre, et s’elle est empressee en l’os, et en a copeit pieces, si quier la plaie, et les trai fuers s’il sont desevrez;	 If it is small, powder it and if it has penetrated the bone and broken into pieces, remove the wound and pull out the parts if they are separated.
et s’il ne sont desevrez, si laisse porrir la plaie, si aligera li estractions;	 If they are not discharged, let the wound fester, align the extractions.
et des autres plaies as autres membres est li jugemens si com nos avons dit.	 And for other wounds on various limbs, the judgement is as we have said.
dou derrompement dou ventre	The rupture of the abdomen
Li derompemens dou ventre est grans et moiens et petis;	 The abdominal ruptures are great and medium-sized and small;
de la grant plaie saut aucune fois li intestine, ou li ners des intestines, par coi li intromission d’aus;	 From the large wound the intestines can once jump out or the intestinal nerves, which causes the internal inflammation;
et li costure est plus malaisie, et aucune fois vaut pis li petite plaie que li grans, por ceu c’on remet plus a poinnes les intestines en, s’on ne les i remet de chaut en chaut;	 And the stitching is more difficult, and sometimes a small wound is worse than a large one, because it is harder to put the intestines back in if not done carefully from the start.
por ce que li intestine enflent tantost qu’il sentent le froit, si rentrent plus a poinnes, et por ceu vaut mues li moieinne plaie, por ceu c’on ramoine mues l’intestine a son leu que as autres II.	 Because the intestines swell quickly when they feel the cold, they return more easily if stitched in carefully, and because of this, a medium-sized wound is better, since the intestines are stitched back to their place more easily than with other wounds.
Et saiches que li routure dou ventre est selonc IIII manieres:	 And know that the hernia of the belly is according to four ways:
les II costures communes avienent en la costure dou ventre, et li costure des autres plaies dou cors et II autres costures propres sont communes as autres plaies;	 The two common hernias occur in the abdominal hernia, and the hernias of other body parts and the other specific hernias are common to other injuries.
et toutevoie elles sont plus propres avec la costure dou ventre, et je dirai une chescune et declairerai.	 And yet they are more specific with the abdominal hernia, and I will say one of them and explain it.
Je di que quant li plaie est petite, et aucune chose de l’intestine ist fuer, et griés chose est dou remettre, ceu est par l’une des II manieres:	 I say that when the wound is small and nothing of the intestine protrudes, and it is easy to put back, this is one of the four ways:
ou por la petitece de la plaie, si com nos avons dit, ou por ce que li intestine est enflez por le froit.	 or because of the smallness of the wound, as we have said, or because the intestine is swollen due to cold.
Et quant il est frois, eschaufez lou en teil maniere:	 And when it is cold, heat it up in some way:
moillie une esponge ou I mol drapeil en aigue tede soulement, ou tu cuis en aigue squinant et cipre et spique, et arose l’intestine tant que li enfleure soit ostee;	 Soak a sponge or a linen cloth only in hot water, or cook in boiling water and cypress and thistle, and warm the intestine until it is removed.
et aucune fois fait ce vins restraingnans, et est muedre que awe soule por desenfler.	 And sometimes do this with restraining wine, and boil it to make it stronger to reduce swelling.
Et quant tu vois l’enfleure departir, si amoiste l’intestine d’aigue ou altee et malves soient cuites, car par ceu est aligie li entree a poc de chose;	 And when you see the swelling diminish, moisten the intestine with either hot or cold water and vegetables that are cooked, as it quickly closes off the opening.
et s’il n’i puet entrer, si fent un poc la plaie a l’estrument de coi on cope les emorroydes;	 If it cannot enter, then make a small incision in the wound with the instrument used for hemorrhoids.
et li premiere cure est muedre que li taille, que nus n’i doit taillier sens grant necessiteit n’i ait;	 And the first treatment is to moisten it, as we should not cut too much unless absolutely necessary.
et c’est li estrumens por le fendre:	 And this is the instrument to break (or split):
si trenche dedens en la corbeure et defuer non, et vez ci la forme:	 It should cut within the hollow part and not bend, and look at its shape:
Et quant li plaie est enlargie, et li intestine saut fuer, si le remet arer selonc la forme naturel en son leu propre, se tu en as pooir, car ce vaut mues.	 And when the wound is enlarged, and the intestines leap out, put them back in place according to their natural shape in their proper place, if you have the power to do so, for it is necessary.
Quant li plaie est large, et elle est en la partie desoz lou ventre, si covient que tu faices gesir lou malaide sus son dos, et met ses jambes plus haut que son chief;	 When the wound is wide and it is in the part below the belly, you must make the patient lie down on his back, and put his legs higher than his head:
et s’elle est en la partie desoz le ventre, si met le chief et le pis plus haut que les parties desoz, et ausi se li routure dou ventre est en l’une des II parties si met t’entente en ceu que li partie navree soit plus haute que li autre;	 If it is in the part below the belly, put the head and feet higher than the parts below, and so if the wound of the belly is in one of the two parts, be mindful that the affected part should be raised higher than the other:
et ensi covient amenistrer ceu que je dis en plaies grans et moienes.	 And thus you must treat as I have said for large and small wounds.
Es plaies petites met ceu que t’est apparilliet, puis aies entre tes mains I ministre pitous ki teigne toute la routure a sa main, et assemble les levres;	 For small wounds, take what is appropriate and gently administer the treatment with your hand, touching all the wound with your fingers and pressing the lips (or edges) together:
et c’est la maniere commune de costures, et est que tu preignes une aguille ou plusors, selonc la quantiteit de la largesce de la plaie, puis laisse des le chief de la plaie I doi d’espaice, et i fiche une aguille ou il ait I boin fil fort;	 And this is the common way of stitching, and you should take a needle or more, according to the width of the wound, then leave from the edge of the wound a distance, and sew with a needle where the good thread is strong.
et perce les II chiés dou cuir avec les II chiés dou siphac, qui est desoz le cuir dedens, tant que tu la faices percier de celle partie, et assemble les II chief dou siphac les IIII ensamble;	 Pierce the two shoulders of skin with two awls, which is underneath the skin, from that part, until you have pierced it, and join the two heads of the awl together in four.
puis l’estrain d’un fil double entor l’aguille de II pars, puis assemble les II chiés de la plaie avenanment, et puis laisse I doi d’espaice, et i fiche une autre aguille;	 then draw a double thread around the needle from both sides, then join the two edges of the wound together, and leave a space, and sew another stitch.
puis la lie dou fil si com tu as fait la premiere aguille, et ne cesser de ceu faire selonc ceu que tu as mestier des aguilles, tant que toute li plaie soit restrainte;	 then tie the thread as you did with the first stitch, and do not stop doing this according to the number of stitches needed, until the entire wound is tightened.
et soient les aguilles moienes, entre subtilz et grosses, car les aguilles subtilz copent toute la char, et les trop grosses si ne pueent mie bien entrer:	 And the needles should be of medium thickness, neither too fine nor too coarse; for fine needles pierce through the whole flesh, and excessively thick ones cannot enter well.
por ceu covient qu’elles soient moienes;	 because they should be of medium thickness.
et ne covient mie bouter les aguilles trop au defuer de la char et dou cuir, k’elles ne copent et oevrent la plaie devant la soudure;	 and it is not good to push the needles too far through the flesh and skin, lest they pierce and open the wound before the suture.
et puis cope les chiés des aguilles, qu’elles ne blecent lou malaide au dormir, et i met tentes ou drapelz au chiés des aguilles por mues tenir, et les laisse tant que li plaie soit soudee;	 then bind the heads of the needles to prevent them from pricking the patient while sleeping, and place tents or cloths over the heads of the needles to hold them in place until the wound is healed.
et ceste maniere de costure as aguilles est plus covenauble en petites plaies, car il i soffist une aguille ou II.	 and this way of suturing with needles is more suitable for small wounds, for in large ones, two needles should be used.
Li seconde costure si est commune, et est que tu assemble les II chiés dou cuir et les II chiés dou syfac ensamble a une aguille ou il ait I fort fil moien;	 The second stitch is common, and it is that you assemble the two bones of the skin and the two bones of the thigh together with a needle that has a strong medium-thick thread.
et quant tu avras perciez ces chiez toz IIII ensamble, si ramoinne l’aguille a la partie ou tu as encomenciet, en la maniere c’on cout les dras;	 and when you have pierced all four bones together, you withdraw the needle from the part where you began, in the manner one sews garments.
et met d’espaice entre chescune costure la grossece d’un menor doi;	 and place a distance between each stitch the thickness of a finger.
ceste costure sevent li home, et je cousi une plaie c’uns hons avoit ou ventre, qui estoit navrez d’un coutel, et estoit li plaie plus d’une palme de grant, et issoit des intestines bien II palmes de grant, et estoit li plaie enmi le ventre.	 This stitch is for men, and I sew a wound that a man had in his belly, which was cut by a knife, and the wound was more than one palm wide, and inside were intestines that were two palms wide, and the wound was within the belly.
Je li ramenai l’intestine puis k’il ot esteit XXIIII houres fuer, et fut li plaie soudee jusc’a XV jors, et le curai, et fut sanez.	 I brought back the intestine when it had been twenty-four hours away, and the wound healed up to fifteen days, and it was cured, and became healthy.
Et li mire l’avoient jugiet qu’il morroit, et ce fut miracle;	 And they had judged him to be dying, but it was a miracle.
et ne le curai mie d’oignement, car je estoie en I leu ou on n’en trovoit point, ne nule medicines;	 and did not treat him with ointment, for I was in a place where no such thing was found nor any medicine.
et metoie sens plus sus la plaie coton viel II fois le jor, et le lavoie d’aigue de miel tant qu’il fut sanez.	 and placed cotton old twice a day on the wound, and washed it with water of honey until it was healed.
Or vos dirai les II propres manieres de cousture:	 Now I will tell you the two proper ways of sewing:
pren l’aguille, et la boute des la partie defuers jusc’a celi dedens;	 take the needle and thread it from the outside part to the inside.
quant elle a perciet le keur de droit en droit, si lai le chief dou siphac ou cousteit ou tu as bouteit l’aguille, et la fai percier d’autre part des la partie dedens jusc’a celi defuer;	 when it has pierced the skin straight through, then put the end of the thread or sew where you have stuck the needle, and pierce it from the inside to the outside.
et li entendemens de ceste costure si est que tu cous ausi com li peletier font les pelz, et que tu laisses une fois le syfac d’une part, et le reprent d’autre, tant que li costure soit toute acomplie.	 And the understanding of this stitching is that you sew it like a tailor sews fur, and that you leave one opening at a time, and then close it from the other side, until the stitching is completely finished.
