And the break occurs in a similar way as it happens in the arm, and for this reason, the restoration is the same as that of the arm, and the work is all the same. And if the two bones are broken together, then the leg turns in every direction.
Et se li os subtilz est brisiez, si torne devant.	If the thin bones are broken, they turn forward.
Et se li gros os est brisiez, si sent on grant dolor, et le voit on bien;	 And if the large bone is broken, one feels great pain, and it can be seen.
et torne desoz.	 and turns under.
Adonques amenistre extension, et le met igal, et lie les esteles igalement;	 Then apply extension, make it even, and bind the limbs equally;
mais toutevoie, il covient se li brisure est laide, et il i a plusors pieces, que li extension soit menor et plus legiere;	 However, if the fracture is deformed and there are several parts, the extension should be less and lighter;
et l’alige selonc ta vertu.	 align it according to your skill.
Et quant tu as tout acomplit ton ovraige, si pren II faixes de fust chevees que porpreignent la jambe d’une part et d’autre, et soient dou lonc de la jambe des le genoil jusque desoz;	 And when you have completed your work, take two rods with crossbars that support the leg from one side and the other, and be of the length of the leg from the knee to beneath.
puis envoloupe en II leus I bendeil desus et desoz, et le lie em mileu ausi, et a ceste lieure ne pora li jambe decliner a destre ne a senestre, et ensi est bien;	 then wrap it in two layers of bandages above and below, and bind it in the middle so that the leg will not decline to the right or left, and thus it is good.
et aucun i aministrent I bers dou lonc de la jambe, et s’est de fust, et i met on la jambe por warder de movement, et proprement fait on ceu en la brisure ou il a plaie;	 And no one administers the iron rod of the leg length, and it is bound, and the leg is held still, and properly done in the break where there is pain.
et remue chescun jor la jambe, por veoir s’il i a aposteme chaut n’autre accident;	 And move the leg every day to see if there is an abscess or other incident.
si le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	 Treat it until it heals.
de la brisure des os dou piet	of the fracture of the bones from the foot
A la cheville ne vient point de brisure, mais as os dou piet vient aucune fois brisure et as dois poc, et n’i avient fuer que quassure em plusor dispositions.	At the ankle, there is no fracture, but the bones of the foot sometimes have a fracture and the toes also, and there is no cure except with many positions.
Et s’il avient as os dou piet brisure, et tu vois ces os sormonter l’un l’autre, si mette si malaides som piet sus la terre, ausi com s’il voloit aler, et puis met maintenant ton piet sus lou sien, lai ou li os sont levez, puis le presse tant k’il reveignent en lor leus;	 If there is a fracture of the foot bone and you see the bones pressing against each other, then put the patient's foot on the ground as if he wants to walk, then put your foot on his foot where the bones are raised, then press it until they return to their place.
puis met l’emplaustre et estoupes sus, et met desoz lou ventre dou piet une petite tauble a II chiés plains, puis l’estraint au piet avenanment, puis que tu as envoloupez drapelz entor, et autres choses dont tu as mestier.	 Then put the splint and padding on it, and under the foot of the patient place a small flat table with two even feet, then hold the foot forward, then, after you have wrapped cloths around it, and other things you need.
Et quant .iij. jors ou .iiij. seront passez, si deslie lou liien, car tu troveras les os igalz, soient brisiez, soient desaluez.	And when three or four days have passed, loosen the linen, for you will find the bones even, whether they are broken or dislocated.
Et s’il i a aucuns des dois brisiez, si les restoure, si com nos avons dit as dois de la main;	 And if any of the two bones are broken, restore them as we have said for the hand's bones.
puis met au doi brisiet une estele selonc la longesce dou doi, et soit un poc plus large, puis met desoz le piet celle tauble que j’ai dit, et l’estrain avenanment;	 Then insert a splint along the length of the broken bone and make it slightly wider, then put the foot under a table as I said before, and bind it tightly.
et s’il en i a II ou III, ou plus, brisiez, si met sus chescun doi une estele selonc sa quantiteit, envoloupee en I drapeil de lin, et estraint la tauble desoz lou piet;	 and if there are two or three, or more broken bones, put a splint over each bone according to its quantity, wrapped in one linen cloth, and bind the table under the foot.
et soit estans sus lou chief de la tauble defuer lou ventre dou piet, si qu’il le teigne bien.	 and let it stand above the table's head away from the belly of the foot, so that it covers it well.
Et covient que tu n’oblier mie les autres choses que j’ai dit as autres briseures, des que nos avons dit;	 And you must not forget the other things I said about broken bones, from what we have said before.
et secor chescun accident si com il covient.	 And attend to each accident as needed.
de la brisure de l’os dou poignil	of the wrist bone fracture
Quant li os de la nature la femme est brisiez, si la fai seoir enlargie, puis l’encline a la partie dou dos, et soit tenue par derrier;	 When the bone of nature (hip) breaks the woman, make her sit upright, then lean her towards the lower back and hold from behind.
puis emplisse li baile la nature de la malaide de couton, et en i mette ausi gros com I sto;	 Then fill the hollow of nature (pelvis) of the patient with cotton and put in as much as will fit.
puis deboute la femme, et lieve lou dos poc et poc, et adonques saut li coton, tant qu’il vient a l’entree de la nature, et revient li os avec lou sto;	 Then turn the woman, lift her lower back little by little, and then pull the cotton out until it comes to the entrance of the pelvis, and the bone returns with the head.
et quant elle vuet pissier, si oste lou coton, et quant elle a pissiet, se li remette, et ensi faice VII jors ou entor:	 And when she wishes to urinate, remove the cotton, and when she has urinated, reset it, and do this for seven days or more.
si sera restoree li brisure, et se tu vues, pren une vessie de berbis, et lie au pertus une cainne, et boute toute la vessie en la nature;	 The break will be restored, and if you see, take a bladder of goat's skin, and attach a tube to the end, and blow all the air out of the bladder into the pelvis.
puis soffle en la cainne forment, tant que li vessie soit enflee dedens:	 Blow air into the hollow of the thigh, until the bladder is inflated within.
la nature si revenra li brisure;	 The nature will heal the break.
puis soit emplie de coton, et le laisse ensi aucuns jors, tant qu’il soit sanez.	 Then fill it with cotton and leave it thus for some days until it is healed.
Et quant li os dou poignil de l’ome est brisiez, ou de la femme, si le restoure ensi com nos avons dit en l’os de la hainche;	 And when the shaft of the arm bone is broken, whether for a man or a woman, restore it as we have said in the thigh bone.
et ne sont mie occultees ces briseures prochienes a celui qui i met son estude et son us, et entent mon livre.	 These breaks shall not be concealed from one who applies his study and experience to them; read my book.
Car li brisure li signifie em plusors dispositions la droite voie de la restauration:	 For the break indicates in many positions the right way of restoration.
enten le donques.	 And so on.
En la verge, quant elle est brisie, pren une gorge d’oie et i boute la verge;	 In a spear when it is broken, take an owl's gourd and insert the spear into it.
puis envoloupe drapelz entor, et le laisse III jors ou enqui entor, et il sera sanez hastanment.	 Then wrap cloths around [it], and leave it for three days or more; and it will heal quickly.
de brisure avec plaie	Of breakage with wound
Il covient a celui qui a brisure avec plaie, meismement s’elle est grans, si com li os de la cuixe ou de l’ajutoire ou semblant, qu’il soit sainiez maintenant, si que les sainies que nos avons dit le tesmoignent.	It is necessary for one who has a breakage with wound, especially if it is large such as the bones of the leg or shoulder, that it be healed now, so that the wounds that we have mentioned bear witness to it.
Et se li plaie saine, si la restainche de vitriole, se tu n’as autre chose, puis rencomence a restorer la briseure en cele meisme houre, ou celui jor, se apostemes chaus n’i vient.	And if the wound heals, anoint it with vitriol (if you have no other), then immediately begin to heal the breakage in that same hour or day, unless abscesses appear.
Et se apostemes chaus i vient, si laisse la restauration jusc’a nuevime jor, tant que li apostemes soit apaisiez, et n’i touchier ne au tier jor ne au quart, car tu i feroies venir malvais accident.	If abscesses appear, wait until the ninth day for healing to begin, allowing the abscesses to subside; do not touch it on the third or fourth day as it may cause harm.
Et se li os brisiez est aparans sus lou keur descovert, si covient que tu lou mettes a point legierement a tes mains, a extension petite.	And if the bone breaks out near the opening, it should be gently set back into place with slight extension.
Et se li extensions ne t’est apareillie por mettre igal a tes mains, si le ramoine a cest estrument qui est de fer, qui a VII dois ou VIII de lonc, et li largesce est selonc la quantiteit de la plaie;	 If the extension is not equipped for you to equalize with your hands, then straighten it with this instrument made of iron, which is 7 or 8 inches long, and the width according to the size of the wound.
et por ceu est mestier au mire qu’il empreigne III ou IIII, selonc ceu qu’il en ait mestier en chescune cure de briseure;	 and therefore it is necessary for the surgeon to take 3 or 4, according to what is needed in each cure of breaking.
et soit rons et un poc gros, k’il ne ploie mie a la compression sus lou membre a ton ovraige, et soit agus devant, et gros des le mileu en avant, ensi:	 and be round and slightly large, so that it does not bend during the compression on the member at your work, and sharp in front, and thick from the middle to the tip, like this:
Et est apelez «palainche», por coi il covient que li chiés corbes soit mis sus lou chief de l’os apparent;	 And it is called "palainche," because the crooked neck should be placed on top of the prominent bone (i.e., the cheekbone).
et le boute a une fois, tant k’il reviegne, et soit igalz l’un encontre l’autre.	 and push it once, until it goes back to its original position, and make sure it is even on both sides.
Et se li brisure est subtilz, et li estrumens ne puet bien prendre l’os, si covient que tu copes lou chief de l’os, tant que li estrumens en ait possance.	 And if the break is subtle and the tool cannot grasp the bone well, you must cut the head of the bone, so that the tool has power over it.
Et se tu ne pues ramener l’os, si com nos avons dit, si lou cope d’un estrument covenable a ceu, ou incisoire ou soieure, a ton pooir;	 And if you cannot reset the bone as we have said, then strike it with an appropriate instrument, either a chisel or a hammer, within your power.
puis reis ceu qui est demorez en l’os d’aspreteit et de menues escorces.	 Then carve off the protruding part in the bone with sharpness and small chips.
Et quant li os est ramenez, et li malaides sent grant dolor aprés, saiches qu’il n’est mie en son leu natureil.	 And when the bone is reset, and the patient feels great pain afterward, know that it is not in its natural place.
Si fai tant qu’il soit en son leu, puis moille I drapeil en vin stiptique noir, et proprement se c’est en esteit;	 Continue until it is in its place, then wet the cloth with black sticky wine, and clean it thoroughly if it is heated.
et ne mettre mie sus la plaie cerote ne autre chose ou il ait oile, qu’il n’i faice venir porriture et corruption;	 and do not put any oil or other substance on the wound that could cause pus and corruption to form.
puis aministre esteles quant tu as restoreit l’os, et laisse la plaie descoverte, et cope la coverture tout entor, selonc la quantiteit de la plaie, et te done bien en garde que li plaie ne soit estrainte avec la brisure;	 Then administer ointment when you have reset the bone, and leave the wound open, and cover it all around, according to the size of the wound, and be careful that the wound is not constricted with a fracture.
et maintes fois ont ce fait li fol mire, et ont fait venir sus le malaide ou mort ou corrodent aucune fois;	 And many times this has been done by foolish people, and they have caused the patient to become sick or die, or corrode at some point.
et soit li estrignemens plus molz et plus souef des autres brisures.	 And the bindings should be softer and more flexible than other fractures.
Et se li plaie est male ou grans, et tu doutes que mavais accidens n’i veigne, si com nos avons dit, et tu trueves dolor au leu, si n’i covient mie mettre sus esteles;	 And if the wound is bad or large and you doubt that a bad accident may come to it, as we have said, and you feel pain at the place, do not put ointment on it.
mais envoloupe entor, en leu d’esteles, drapelz durs, et les lie.	 But wrap around it instead of ointment, with hard cloths, and tie them up.
Et quant tu vois aprés I jor ou II enjanrer bowe a la plaie, si oste ceu que tu as mis sus a tout vin, et i met oignement sanant plaies, si com oignement tetrafarmaçon et semblans.	 And after a day or two, when the wound has begun to swell, take away what you have put on it and apply healing ointment for wounds, such as healing ointment made from four substances and similar ones.
Et covient que tu deslies lou membre .ij. fois le jor, lou matin et au vespre, tant qu’il soit soudez et sanez.	And you should loosen the limb two times a day, in the morning and at evening, as long as it is healed and sound.
Et covient que li membres soit aparilliez en teil maniere que li bowe corre aval legierement.	And the limbs should be aligned in such a way that the bone moves downward gently.
Et se maint jor trespassent, et il ne puet souder mais rent adés bowe, saiches k’il i a petites pieces d’os, por coi il covient que tu quieres la plaie avec tente, et oste toutes ces pieces desevrees que font venir celle dolor.	And if it passes for many days and cannot heal but again bows, you know that there are small bone fragments; therefore, you must press the wound with force, and remove all the dislocated bone fragments that cause the pain.
Et se fistule vient au leu, ou autre maniere de corruption, si covient que tu le cures, selonc ceu qu’il dist en son chapistre ci devant.	 And if a fistula or other form of corruption comes to the place, you must treat it, according to what is written in the chapter above.
Et quant li os est brisiez, et apert sus lou membre, si com li os de la cuixe ou de l’ajutoire, et autres semblans des grans membres, si ne le traire mie, car maintes fois en vient li mors, mais le laisse tant qu’il porrisse;	 And when the bone is broken and exposed through a limb, such as the bone of the thigh or shoulder, or similar large members, do not draw it out, for many times death occurs. But let it be until it can be drawn.
par aventure cherra par lui aprés XX jors ou XXX, puis cure la plaie, se tu pues;	 perhaps after twenty days or thirty, then treat the wound if possible.
et se tu ne pues, si la laisse.	 and if you cannot, then leave it.
des brus qui vienent sor la sodure	The burning cautery commands the sick to let their hairs grow long and even; if they prick at their base, hold the eyes steady so they do not move until they grow.
Nous vienent maintes fois aprés la santeit de la briseure, meismement quant c’est pres de la jointure, et laide chose est a veoir li figure dou membre;	 Often after the healing of the fracture, especially when it is near the joint, a terrible sight is to be seen on the appearance of the limb.
et par aventure ne puet faire li membres ses ovraiges naturelz.	 And perhaps the limbs cannot perform their natural functions.
Pren warde donques se li nous est fres:	 Therefore, take care for ourselves.
si li aministre medicines stiptiques, si com aloes, encens, et mirre, et sarcocolle, acaice, et semblans autres, ensi que tu preignes aucune de ces choses, ou toutes ensamble, et les confit avec vin stiptique ou avec abun d’uef ou avec aisil;	 If you administer medicines such as aloes, incense, myrrh, sarcocola, acacia and similar things, take one of these things or all together, crush them with a sharp stone or grind them with pestle and mortar, and then mix them with vinegar, egg white, or honey.
et les met sus le nout en estoupes, et l’estraint bien, et ne la desliier en mains jors;	 And he places it on a bed of ashes, and holds it tight, and does not loosen it for many days.
et puis la desloie, et rencomence une autre, tant que li nodations soit ostee;	 Then he dislocates (it) again and begins another, until the swelling is gone;
ou tu estrain sus une piece de plonc bien faite;	 or you hold it on a well-made plank.
car li proprietez dou plonc si est qu’il oste toutes les enfleures desus les membres;	 for the properties of the plank are such that they remove all the swelling from the limbs;
et se li nodation est ja convertie en durteit ausi com piere, et il est besoing de l’oster, si la cope desus, et fent la superfluiteit apparent;	 and if the swelling has turned into hardness like stone, it must be removed by striking the top of it and making the excess visible.
ou tu la reis a aucun raseur, tant qu’ele soit ostee, et la cure tant qu’ele soit sanee.	 or you grate (it) with any scraper until it is removed, and treat it until it heals.
dou membre qui est foibles aprés la garison	The limb which is weak after being treated
Quant li brisure de l’os est restoree, et demoure aprés li membres foibles et subtilz, si avient por mout de causes:	 When the bone fracture has been restored and stays after that, the limbs remain weak and delicate due to many causes.
de coi l’une est por ceu qu’il fut liiez trop estroit, et ne fut mie liiez si com il covenoit;	 Because one was tied too tightly and was not tied as it should have been.
ou por ceu qu’il i ot trop de liiens, et ne pooit venir li norrissemens au membre;	 because there were too many bindings, and the limbs could not receive the necessary nutrients.
ou por multitude d’arosement;	 due to excessive bleeding.
ou por trop grans movements, ne mie en son houre;	 due to excessively large movements, not at the right time.
ou por ceu qu’il a poc de sanc en son cors, si est foibles.	 because he has little blood in his body, so he is weak.
Et li cure si est que tu faices mengier le malaide, et faire le cors tendre, tant que li sans soit multipliiez en lui;	 And the cure is to make the patient eat, and make the body strong, until the blood is multiplied in him.
et li aministre bain, et li done joie et liesce;	 and administer baths, and give joy and pleasure.
puis met poix sus le membre, si que li poix atraie a li grant norrissement, et l’arose sovent d’aigue tede, tant que li norrissement corre au membre;	 then put wax on the member, so that the wax attracts great nourishment, and the wound often bleeds cold water, until the nourishment returns to the member.
et reviegne a sa figure natureil.	 And return to its natural shape.
dou membre tort aprés la santeit	twisted limb after health
Quant li membres est tors aprés la restauration, et li os brisiez apert, et li forme dou membre est laide, toutevoie ne pert mie son ovraige natureil:	 When the limb is twisted after restoration, and the bones are broken open, and the shape of the limb is ugly, nevertheless do not lose its natural function.
si ne croire mie les folz qui dient c’on doit brisier lou membre tout de noveil, et maint fol mire ont ce fait en nostre terre;	 do not believe the foolish ones who say one must break the limb entirely anew, and many have done so in our land.
et cist ovraiges est blamez, et en vient grans malz, et par aventure li mors;	 and this practice is condemned, and it brings great harm, and by chance death.
toutevoie, se li nodations et li torture sont fres, si covient k’il soient arosez d’aigue chaude, ou herbes mollifians soient cuites, si com foilles de vismalve, et racines, et mellilote, et semblans choses;	 Nevertheless, if the nodes and tortures are fresh, it is necessary that they be cauterized with hot water, or herbs softening should be cooked, such as mallow leaves, radishes, and medlot roots, and similar things.
et li fai I emplaustre mollificatif, si com dyaquilon bien fait, et tu pren le muscillaige de vismalve, et la confit avec graisse de geline ou oile de sisament, et fai emplaustre sus;	 And you make the plaster soothing, as one well knows how to do, and you take the musk of vismalve, and mix it with linseed oil or camomile oil, and apply the plaster on top.
ou tu pren figues graisses, et les broie avec fien de colon, et semblans medicines que amenuisent le soudement.	 And you take figs softened in oil, and grind them with the straw of wheat, and similar medicines that reduce inflammation.
Et aucune fois est ostee li nodacion por froter continuelment et longement a mains moistes.	 And sometimes, the dislocation is opened by rubbing continuously and for a long time with moist hands.
Et soit amenistrez movement au membre chescune houre.	 Movements should be brought to the limb every hour.
Et se li tortuositez est enveillie et endurcie, ausi com piere, et besoins est de l’oster au fer, si la covient coper jusc’a l’os, a l’incisoire subtil legierement;	 And if the twisting is swollen and hardened like stone, it requires to be cauterized, so it must be covered up to the bone, with a subtle incision made lightly.
et mettre cusenson et estude en la cure.	 And put poultice and linen in the treatment.
Ci encomence li livres des dislocations	Here begins the book of dislocations
Dislocations est issue d’aucune jointe de son leu, por coi il ne se puet muevre, et est li membres mal figurez, et sent li malaides grant dolor et grant lesion.	Dislocation occurs when a joint moves out of its place, which prevents it from moving, and the limb is misaligned, causing the patient great pain and injury.
Quant dislocation vient a aucun, si le covient maintenant ramener sens targier.	When dislocation occurs in any limb, it must now be reset carefully.
Car s’on tarde, si enfle li leus, et par aventure si le remet on a poines au leu;	 For if it is delayed, the wound swells, and perhaps it is reset to its place.
por ceu ne covient mie c’on le mueve a l’oure k’il est enflez:	 For this reason, one must not move it when swollen.
maintes fois fait venir spame et autres dolors;	 Often causes spasms and other pains.
toutevoie, quant ce avenra, si fai sainier lou malaide, puis le laisse, tant que li apostemes chas soit apaisiez;	 However, when this happens, if you can make the patient purge, let him rest until all abscesses are appeased.
puis arose le membre d’aigue chaude et d’oile, puis le ramoinne legierement, et cure chescun membre si com li cure venra en son leu.	 Then immerse the limb in hot water and oil, gently reset it, and treat each member according to its place.
Et j’ai ordenez les chapistres des dislocations des lou chief jusc’a piez.	And I have arranged the chapters on shoulder dislocations from head to foot.
des mandibules	of the lower jaws (jawbones)
Poc avient que les mandibules soient desaluees andous, et li dislocations d’ambedous est selonc II manieres:	 It rarely happens that the jaw is dislocated outwards, and dislocations of both occur in two ways:
ou elles sont un poc ostees de lor leus, et mollifies un poc;	 or they are slightly displaced from their places and softened a little.
ou elles sont desaluees entierement, et pendent vers lou pis, et cort li salive de la bouche qu’il ne la puet tenir, ne ne puet clore sa bouche, et envoloupe sa langue avec la parole.	 or they are completely dislocated and hang towards the bottom, with the saliva running from the mouth that he cannot hold, cannot close his mouth, and wraps his tongue around with speech.
Quant li dislocations est petite, si revient par li em plusors disposicions.	When a dislocation is small, it often returns with multiple displacements.
Et s’elle est entiere et acomplie, si covient que tu la ramoinne hastanment, et ne targier mie;	 And if it is whole and complete, you must reset it quickly, without delay.
et en tel maniere que li ministres teigne le chief dou malaide, et boute li mires som pochet de l’une de ses mains en la racine de la dislocation de la mandibule dedens la bouche, se li dislocations est de II pars;	 and in such a manner that the assistant holds the head of the patient, and pushes one of his fingers into the root of the dislocation of the jaw within the mouth, if the dislocation is in two parts.
et li autre doi des mains soient defuer, por mettre igal;	 and the other hand should be open, to hold evenly.
et comande au malaide qu’il les amollisse, ses mandibules, et les mueve de toutes pars.	 instruct the patient to soften, his jaws, and move them in all directions.
Et li mires la mete igal, tant qu’elle reveigne en son leu.	And the patient must keep the meat equal, until it returns to its place.
Et se li ramener est griés, meismement se ce sont les II mandibules ensamble, si les arose d’aigue chaude et d’oile, tant que les ramoinnes legierement;	 If the resetting is painful, especially if it is both jaws together, apply sharp hot water and oil, until they are reset easily.
ne ne targier mie dou ramener, si com nos avons dit.	 Do not delay in resetting, as we have said.
Et quant elles sont ramenees igalment, et li bouche dou malaide clot bien sens mollifiier, si met sus drapelz moilliez en cerote fait d’oile roset et de cire, puis le lie legierement de molz liiens;	 And when they (the dislocated limbs) are reset equally, the patient's mouth should close well and soften with a poultice made of rose oil and wax, then gently tie it with a few bandages.
et dorme li malaides sus son dos, et ses chiés soit estans entre II cussins, si qu’il ne lou mueve ne a destre ne a senestre, ne ne s’efforce mie de maixier, mais preigne legiere viande, tant que les dolors soient ostees, et soient noees les mandibules;	 The patient should sleep on his back, with his arms between two pillows, so that they do not move to the left or right, nor try to move at all, but take soft food until the pain is gone, and the jaws are sewn.
et puis menjuce ce qu’il vuet legierement, et ne se travaille mie d’ovrir la bouche au mengier et au boivre, tant que li mandibule soit bien noee et sanee.	 And then eat whatever he wants lightly, and do not make an effort to open the mouth to eat or drink, until the jaws are well sewn and healed.
Et se les .ij. mandibules ne pueent estre remises a point a une houre, et ne sont mie converties a lor leus, si en vient fievres et sode acostumees, et par aventure solution de ventre, et par aventure vomist cole pure.	And if the two jaws cannot be set right within an hour and are not restored to their place, fever and usual symptoms may occur, and possibly a stomach problem or vomiting of clear bile.
Et quant tu verras ceu, adonc saiches que c’est perdicions;	 And when you see this, then know that it is destruction.
et maintes fois muert cil cui il avient, en VIIII jors.	 and many who experience it die within eight days.
de la forcelle	of the noose
Li forcele ne puet desaluer dou costeit dedens la continuation de li et dou pis, et est desaluee aucune fois au defuer, et bien le sent on.	The noose cannot dislocate from the inside along its length and width, but it can be dislocated at times from the outside, and one feels it.
Et li restauration si est que li malaides gise sovin sor son dos, et estende ses bras;	 And the restoration is that the patient lies face down on his back, and extends his arms.
et puis presse le leu forment a ta palme, et elle revenra;	 then press the place firmly with your palm, and it will return.
puis met sus l’emplaustre et lou bendeil, et l’estraint;	 then put the splint and bandage on it, and hold it.
et li chiez qui est devers lou coute ne puet desaluer;	 and the head that is towards the side cannot dislocate.
se poc non, et se il desalue aucune fois, si le ramoinne a son leu, si com nos avons dit;	 if it should not do so, and if it does dislocate once, reset it to its place, as we have said;
puis met sus l’emplaustre et le bendeil, et l’estraint, et coumande au malaide qu’il se repose tant qu’il soit sanez;	 then put the splint and bandage on it, hold it, and instruct the patient to rest until he is well.
et ensi meisme est ramenez li chiés de l’espale, quant il est desevrez de son leu.	 And similarly, the head of the shoulder is repositioned when it is dislocated from its place.
de la dislocation de l’espaule	Of the dislocation of the shoulder
Saiches que li espaule n’est desaluee fuer que selonc III manieres:	 Know that the dislocation of the shoulder occurs in three ways:
de coi l’une est qu’ele desalue a la partie de l’assele au desoz;	 The first is when it dislocates at the part below the socket.
et li seconde est a la partie dou pis;	 And the second one is to the part of the thigh;
et par aventure desalue a la partie desus, et ceu avient poc;	 And by chance, it dislocates in the upper part, and this happens little.
et ne desalue mie derrier por l’espaule, et ne desalue mie dedens por les ners;	 and it does not dislocate behind because of the shoulder, and it does not dislocate inside due to the nerves.
et plusors fois desalue desoz vers l’assele, meismement a ces qui ont poc de char, car a ces saut ele fuer hastanment;	 And it often dislocates downwards towards the buttock, especially in those who have little flesh, for these leap out suddenly.
a ces qui ont assez char, saut ele a poines, et rentre a poines.	 In those with enough flesh, it leaps out very little and returns very little.
Et par aventure avient a aucuns homes percussion ou casseure, et enfle li espaule d’un aposteme chaut, et cuide qu’elle est desaluee par ceu.	And sometimes it happens to some men that they receive a blow or break and the shoulder swells with a hot abscess, and they think it is dislocated due to this.
Il covient donques que tu l’esprueves, tant que tu en soies certains;	 Therefore, you must examine it, as long as you are certain;
et adonques encomence la cure.	 And then begin the treatment.
Et est conue li dislocations quant il est aval vers l’assele, et met difference entre l’espaule malade et la saine, et tu troveras entre lor diversiteit manifeste;	 Dislocations are known when they move downwards towards the buttock, and you should distinguish between the sick shoulder and the healthy one, and you will find a clear difference between them.
et troveras au chief de l’espaule une fosse, et desoz l’assele au tochier le chief de l’espaule, ausi com se ce soit uns oes;	 You will find a hollow at the top of the shoulder, and press down on it with your thumb so that you can put the head of the shoulder back into place, just like setting a bone.
et ne puet li malaides ramener sa main a son neis, ne movoir de nulz movemens;	 The patient cannot return their hand to its original position or make any movement.
et ausi, s’elle est desaluee en haut, si n’est mie occultee, car tu le trueves manifestement au tochier;	 If it is dislocated upwards, do not hide it, for you can feel it clearly with your thumb.
et ceste maniere de dislocation n’est mie fors a ramener, quant elle est novele, ou se li enfes est malaides.	 This type of dislocation is not only able to be reset when it is new, but also if the infant is ill.
Et li maniere est que li ministres lieve la main dou malaide en haut, puis met tes peuchas desoz l’assele, et lieve la jointure a force en haut au leu;	 The manner is that the attendant lifts the hand of the patient up, then places their fists under it, and forces the joint upward to its place.
et li ministres lieve la main, et l’estende en haut, pues le mette desoz;	 And the ministers place the hand, stretch it upwards, then put it underneath;
si venra hastanment.	 It will come immediately.
Et s’elle ne vient si com nos avons dit em mains jors aprés, si covient ke li malaides soit baigniez en aigue chaude;	 And if it does not come as we have said in hands for several days, then the patient should be bathed in hot water.
et li amenistre arosement mollifiant et assouajant, si com decoction de altee et de fenugrec et de mellilote en aigue, et soit amenistree;	 and he is given a soothing and calming balm, such as the decoction of elder and fenugreek and melilot in hot water, and it should be administered.
puis soit sovinez li malaides sus son dos, et mette on desoz l’assele un sto de lainne igal, ne trop mol ne trop dur, puis mette li mires son talon sus le sto, et lieve le chief de l’espaule vertuousement, et traie la main dou malaide;	 Then the patient should be made to lie on his back, and a cloth of equal thickness, not too soft nor too hard, is placed under the affected area. Then the minister holds the heel of the patient while pulling the arm of the patient with care.
et uns autres ministres teigne lou chief dou malaide, si qu’il ne se mueve aval;	 And another assistant holds the head of the patient still, so it does not move downwards.
celle espaule revient tout maintenant, et se tu vues si le ramoinne selonc ceste maniere:	 This shoulder returns immediately, and if you see it dislocate again in this way:
et est que tu faices estre present I home qui soit plus grans que li malaides;	 and it is that you have someone who is larger than the patient present.
et soit drois devers lou costeit, et boute s’espaule desoz l’assele dou malaide, et lieve l’assele en haut, si que li malaides pende en l’ar;	 and stand opposite the patient's side, push his shoulder under the patient's armpit, lift the armpit upwards so that the patient hangs on the arm.
et uns autres ministres traie la main dou malaide aval devers lou ventre.	 and another assistant pulls the patient's hand down towards the belly.
Et se li malaides est trop legiers, si pent avec lui aucune chose pesant, et li dislocation revient maintenant.	 And if the patient is too weak, they cannot bear any heavy thing, and the dislocation returns immediately.
Et le ramoinne on ausi en autre maniere:	 It is also reset in another way:
et est c’on fiche I lonc tison en terre, dont li chiés soit ausi reons com I pistal, et ne soit ne trop gros ne trop graile;	 and it is that a long needle is stuck into the ground so that the head of the shoulder is as round as a pea, but not too thick or too thin.
puis soit mis desoz lou malaide, mais k’il ait drapelz souef sus, et li malaides soit estans dou lonc dou fust;	 Then lay the patient down, but with soft sheets under him, and the patient should be long on the bed.
puis soit estendue sa main aval d’autre part forment, et li jointure revenra en son leu hastanment;	 Extend the affected hand below towards the other side, and the joint will quickly return to its place.
et s’elle ne vuet revenir por toutes ces choses que nos avons dit, si fai ceste cure:	 And if it does not return by all these things we have said, perform this treatment:
pren I tison de II bras de grant et IIII dois de large, qui ait le chief reont por mues entrer em parfont desoz l’assele, selonc ceste forme:	 Take a stick of two hands' length (approximately 91 cm) and four fingers' width (about 20 cm), having the head rounded for easy insertion deep into the anus, in this shape:
puis lie sus le chief dou fust drapelz souez, que li fust ne blece lou malaide, puis le met desoz l’assele dou malaide;	 fold the top of the stick with cloth so it does not hurt the patient, then insert it into the anus of the patient.
et estende som bras sus le fust dou lonc, et lie l’ajutoire sus le fust, et lou bras au chief de la main, puis met le bras sus I eschillon d’une eschiele dou large, et soit estendue li mains aval, et soit laissiez li cors pendans d’autre part:	 extend one arm above the stick, place the patient's shoulder on the stick, place the hand at the top of the stick, then place the other arm above an elbow-sized support and extend both hands below, leaving the body hanging from another side.
li jointure reva ens maintenant.	 the joint is now revealed.
Et quant elle est ens, en quel maniere que ce soit, si covient que tu mettes desoz l’assele une spere de laine igal, puis met l’emplaustre aparilliet de poudre dou molin, avec encens et aubun d’uef, sus toute l’espaule et entor, puis l’estrain desoz l’assele avenanment, et torne le liien sus l’emplaustre, et embraice la main a son col, et soit li mains demorans ensi.	And when the joint is reset, whichever way it may be, you must place an equal piece of woolen cloth beneath the joint; then apply an ointment made with flour from the mill, along with incense and egg yolk over the entire shoulder and around it; then hold the limb below the joint, and twist the linen thread around the ointment, and embrace the hand at its neck, and keep the hands in place.
Et covient qu’il menjuce poc, tant que li membres soit confortez, car il sanera plus tost;	 It is necessary that he eats little food, until the limb is comfortable, because it will heal faster.
et puis menjuce plus aprés V jors ou VII, et le mueve;	 And then move it more after five or seven days, and let it move.
et s’il est fermeis et il n’est mollifiez, si est sanez.	 If it is hardened and not softened, it is healthy.
Et se li jointure est fuer de leu por moistor que i est venue, ou por autre cause, si covient que tu i aministres cauteres a III pertus, si com il est mis devant ou chapistre des cauteres.	 And if the joint is out of place due to moisture or for some other reason, then you must administer fire cauterization at three places as stated in the chapter on cauteries.
Et se tu fais tout ceu, et il deslie aprés VII jors, et li jointure ne se tient, et ne puet lever som bras amont, adonc saiches que li nerf au chief de l’espaule sont copeit ou estendut ou amollis;	 And if you do all this and it dislocates after seven days and the joint does not hold together and cannot lift its arm above, then know that the nerve at the head of the shoulder is crushed or stretched or softened.
et saiches que li jointure n’iert jamais fichie en son leu.	 And know that the joint will never be properly set in its place.
Li dislocation qui est devers lou pis, et les mameles, ou derrier, si est faite par impulsion, et estendement de mains, et i aministre on autre lieure;	 A dislocation that is towards the hip or the buttocks, or behind, is caused by violence and stretching of hands, and another treatment is administered.
et cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	 Treat it until it heals.
Et se aprés la sanation vient grietez au membre, et tardemens em movement, si use li malaides bain maintes fois, tant que celle grietez soit alegie, et reviegne a sa premiere nature.	And after the healing comes pain in the member, and slow movement, then the patient uses warm baths many times, until the pain subsides and returns to its original state.
de la dislocation dou coute	of the dislocation cost
Saiches que li jointure dou coute est desaluee a poinnes, et a poinnes revient;	 Know that the dislocation of the shoulder is dislocated at the point and returns at the point.
et s’est desaluee de toutes pars, et meismement devant et derrier, et li dislocations n’est mie reponue, car on la voit bien et sent bien;	 And it is dislocated from all parts, both front and back, and the dislocation is not repositioned, because it can be seen clearly and felt.
et desalue selonc chescune figure.	 And it dislocates according to each shape.
Et quant tu joins le coute malaide avec lou sain, si le pues veoir apertement.	 And when you join the bone of the patient with the healthy one, you should see it clearly.
Car li jointure est chevee, et ne puet ploier lou bras, ne touchier son espaule a tout.	 For the joint is thick, and cannot bend the arm nor reach the shoulder completely.
Et covient que tu le ramoinnes ainsois que apostemes chaus i viegne, car se apostemes chaus i venoit, si seroit grief li ramener;	 And you must reset it in the same way as an abscess comes to a head, because if an abscess comes to a head, it would be harmful to reset.
et par aventure ne puet estre ramenez dou tout en tout, meismement quant ele est au derrier;	 And perhaps it cannot be reset completely in every way, especially when it is at the back.
si vaut pis que les autres dislocations, et est de plus grant dolor, et par aventure i vient li mors.	 If so, it is worth more than other dislocations, and it is of greater pain, and perhaps death may come from it.
Et li restauration si est, quant elle est telz c’on la puet ramener, que tu li estendes sa main a tes II mains;	 And the restoration [of the shoulder] is such that you extend your hand to both hands.
et ses bras soit espandus, et les mains dou mire selonc le coute entor, desor et desoz, et boute la jointure a ses peuchas ensamble, ou a la racine de sa palme, tant qu’ele reviegne a son leu.	 And his arms should be spread out, and the hands to the mirror according to the cut around, outside and inside, and push the joint to its sockets together, or to the root of its palm, until it returns to its place.
Et se li dislocations est au devant, si revient quant il double sa main a sa main, et fier de la racine de la palme lou coute qui est desaluez.	And if the dislocation is at the front, it will return when you fold your hand to the other, and press from the root of the palm on the side that has been dislocated.
Et s’il ne vuet revenir au leu, si aministre fort extension;	 And if it does not want to return to its place, apply strong traction;
et est que dui ministre estendent le bras, et le teignent dui ministre, si qu’il ne se mueve a l’estension;	 and two men should stretch the arm, and one should pull it, so that it does not move during traction;
puis torne le bras de chescune part, puis que tu as envoloupeit un drapeil double lonc et large;	 Then turn the arm on each side, and when you have wrapped a double long and wide cloth around it;
et quant li mires a jointe la jointure a sa main, si l’oigne d’aucun oile por amolir la jointure, puis boute la jointure forment, tant qu’ele reviegne;	 And when the mirror has joined the joint to his hand, apply some oil to soften the joint, then push the joint together, until it returns.
et quant elle est au leu, si met sus emplaustre sec avec aubun d’uef, et l’estrain forment, et pent le bras au col dou malaide, et le laisse aucuns jors, puis le deslie.	 And when it is in place, put a dry plaster made with egg on it and hold it in position, and keep the arm around the patient's neck for some days, then release it.
Et se li jointure est ferme en son leu, si deslie lou liien, et le laisse;	 And if the joint is closed in its place, then leave it alone;
et se tu vois que li jointure n’estrigne bien, si rencomence l’emplaustre et lou lien, et le laisse ensi aucuns jors, tant qu’il soit fermement mis;	 and if you see that the joint does not hold together well, then repeat the plaster and bandage, and leave it like this for some days until it is firmly set.
puis le deslie.	 Then release it.
Et se il sent grieteit aprés le ramenement de la jointe, et elle se muet, si le baigne et frote bellement, et presse tant qu’il soit assouagiez;	 And if it hurts after the reposition of the joint and swells, then wash and rub well, and press until it is soothed.
ou tu met sus la jointure une naige de mouton grasse, puis la laisse I jor et une nuit, puis l’oste, et lou fai entrer ou bain;	 Or place a sheepskin pad over the joint, leave it for a day and a night, then remove it, and make it enter water.
et quant il sue, se li frote la jointure tempreement, puis remet la naige sus, et puis entre ou bain;	 And when it swells, gently rub the joint, then place the arm over it, and then immerse it in water.
et ensi fai II fois ou III, tant qu’il soit sanez;	 And do this two or three times until it is healed.
et se tu vues, si met sus fien de vaiche moiste chaufeit avec burre, et l’estrain sus;	 If you see it, place warm and moist sheep's wool on it and bind it up.
si revenra a sa disposition.	 It will return to its position.
li dislocation de la main	the dislocation of the hand
Li jointure de la main desalue, et li revenue est legiere, plus que les autres jointures.	 The joint of the hand becomes dislocated, but it returns to its place more easily than other joints.
Toutevoie, il la covient ramener au leu hastanment, en l’oure meisme qu’ele est desaluee, ainsois que li leus soit enflez, ou qu’il i viegne aposteme chaut.	 Immediately, you must put it back in its place as soon as it is dislocated, unless the joints are swollen or hot with abscesses.
Et li ramenemens si est que tu mettes la main malaide sus une tauble, et estende li ministres la main, et li mires la mette igal, ensi que il mette sa paume sus l’aparance de la jointure, et la boute tant qu’elle reviegne.	 And the repositioning is that you place the affected hand on a table, and extend the fingers of your assistants, and align the mirror to it so that the back of your hand rests on the appearance of the joint, and push until it returns.
Toutevoie, il covient que vos regardez s’il est bien a leu;	 Therefore, you must ensure it is properly set.
adonc mette li malaides lou dos de sa main sus une tauble a l’estension et au ramenement.	 Place the patient's hand on a table for extension and repositioning.
Et se li dislocations est au dos de la main, si mette li malaides son dos de sa main sus la tauble, et li mires mette sa main sus cele apparance de la jointure.	 And if the dislocation is at the back of the hand, place the patient's back of their hand on the table, and have them place their other hand on the appearance of the joint.
S’elle revient maintenant, c’est bien.	 If it returns to its place now, that is good.
Se ce non, si l’estrain d’emplaustres apaisans apostemes chaus, et lou laisse ensi sens rencomencier.	 If not, press the affected area with plasters, and let it rest to start healing.
Et s’il ne le puet soffrir, et tu ne la pues mettre au leu aprés aucuns jors, si demore li jointure torte;	 And if the patient cannot bear it, and you cannot set it in place after any days, then the dislocation remains twisted.
et ne nuist niant au malaide fuer que tant que li mains est amoillie, et ne puet estraindre aucune chose a tout:	 Furthermore, the patient should not be harmed excessively as long as his hand is injured and cannot exert any force.
adonc saiches que li nerf sont copez, ou li artere;	 Therefore, know that nerves or arteries have been cut.
si n’i a autre engien fuer que d’estraindre par cautere delez le cas, et par aventure n’i vaut autre chose.	 If there is no other tool available except to straighten it with a fire cautery, it does not have any other value.
Et quant li mains est au leu, si met sus l’emplaustre que nos avons dit, puis l’estrain et le laisse .v. jors, puis le deslie et laisse ensi.	And when the hand is injured, apply the plaster as we have said, then strap and leave for five days, then unbind and let be.
Et s’il ne la puet bien movoir, et il i a aucune grieteit, si la moille d’aigue chaude, et le frote tant qu’il soit sanez.	If it cannot move well and there is no swelling, moisten with warm water and rub until it is healed.
de la dislocation des dois de la main	of the dislocation of the fingers of the hand
Aucune fois sont desaluez li doi de la main a chescune part, aucune fois au dos de la palme ou au ventre;	 The fingers of the hand are occasionally dislocated on both sides, occasionally at the back of the palm or the belly.
adonques estent le doi, et boute la dislocation a tes pouchés tant qu’il reviegne, puis sostien lou chief dou doi, et le pent vers la partie ou il est desjoins;	 Then push the dislocated finger back into place as it returns, then hold the finger's head and bend it towards the side where it is disjointed.
et le laisse II jors, et puis le met igal celui jor;	 And let it rest for two days, then equalize it on that day.
et de nut le lie, si com nos avons dit, et lou deslie de jor, et lou fai movoir, et le relie la nut;	 Then bind it, as we have said, and dislocate it for a day, and make it move, then tie it back in place.
et fai ce sovent, tant qu’il soit estroit, et tout ausi fai, se il est desaluez au ventre de la main, et fai si com tu as fait ci devant, tant qu’il soit sanez;	 And do this often until it is narrow, and do the same thing if it is dislocated at the stomach of the hand, and do what you have done before, until it heals.
et tout ausi fai, quant il est desaluez d’autre part.	 And do the same thing when it is dislocated from another side.
dou desaluement de l’eschinee dou dos	When the vertebrae of the back are dislocated.
Quant l’eschinee dou dos ou dou col est desaluee, ou il en i a plusors desaluees, si n’i a point de cure, car li mors haste le malaide.	When the vertebrae of the back or neck are dislocated, or there are multiple dislocations, there is no cure, for death soon follows the patient.
Et li signes si est que li egestions saut fuer sens volunteit, ne ne la puet tenir, et maintes fois sont mollifiez aucun membre, ou les II cuixes ou li dui bras ou I.	 And the signs are that the emissions leap without will, and it cannot be held; and many times, some limb is softened, either both knees or the two arms or one.
Et maintes fois se muet li eschinee a IIII pars;	 And many times, the spine becomes mute at four parts;
celle qui se muet au derrier si est apelee «gilbositez»:	 The dislocation that occurs at the back is called "gilbositez":
li cure si est que tu rewarde se li gilbositez est venue d’enfance:	 The treatment is to check if the gilbositez has occurred from birth:
si n’i ait point de cure ne de sanation dou tot.	 if it has no cure or healing from the very beginning.
Et celle que vient de cheoir ou de percussions ou de semblans choses, dirent li ancien manieres de cures par grans paroles, ou il n’a mie en toutes grant profit;	 And those that come from falling or beatings or similar things, the old ways of cure used to be described with great words, but there is no real benefit in all cases.
mais je l’ai abregiet selonc mon entention, et ai formez estrumens en diverses manieres.	 However, I have shortened it according to my intention, and made instruments in various ways.
Je dis que en la gilbositeit que vient au pis devant, nen a engien ne santeit;	 I say that in the gilbositez coming at the worst place, there is no remedy or health.
et ausi cele que vient droitement en II costez, et ne puet on curer fuers que celi proprement qui vient au dos, si com je dis;	 And similarly the one that comes directly between two sides, and cannot be cured except by the one that comes at the back as I said.
et est que li malaides soit estendus sus sa faice en I leu igal, et ait de l’estrain desoz lui, qu’il ne se blece;	 And it is that the patient should be extended on his face in the same place, and have support beneath him so he does not bruise.
puis fiche I tison au chief en terre forment, et I autre as piez, et lie un liien pardesoz les asseles dou malaide, et I autre as hainches, et as genous, et as chevilles;	 Then insert the iron point into the base of the head and the other at the feet, and tie a rope over the soles of the patient, and another around the ankles, and the knees, and the shins.
et dui ministre saichent les liiens, li uns au chief et li autres as piez, parmi les II tisons;	 and two assistants hold the ropes, one at the head and the other at the feet, around the two iron points.
et soient bien fermez, li tison si com nos avons dit, et li mires mette ses paumes sus l’espinee forment, tant qu’ele reviegne.	 and they should be tightly closed, the iron points as we have said, and the mirror places his hands on the spine until it returns.
Et s’elle ne revient par ceste cure, si pren une tauble de III bras de lonc, et chevé desoz la paroit, et li malaides soit en costé, et boute le chief de la tauble desoz la paroit, puis met le mileu de la tauble sus l’espinee;	 And if it does not return with this treatment, take a board three feet long and sharpened at one end, place the patient on his side, push the chief of the board under the back, then place the middle of the board on the spine.
et mette li mires ses piez sus l’autre chief de la tauble, et presse bien, tant qu’il reviegne au leu;	 And place the mirrors on the opposite head of the table, and press firmly, until it returns to its place.
et se tu vues, si le fai au tornet qui torne a la main.	 If you see it, do so using the lathe that turns with your hand.
Et est que tu fiches II tisons au chief dou malaide d’un bras de grant, et devers les piez II autres, et ait entre chescun tison, desoure et desoz, une paume d’espaice de lonc;	 And you insert two pins into the head of the patient's large arm, and between each pin, have about a span of space on either side.
et ait en chescun tison I pertus, ou li tornet corre, et soient li tison fermement en terre, si qu’il ne se muevent;	 And let there be in each pin the lathe turner, and the pins must be firmly set in the ground, so that they do not move.
et entre chescuns II tisons ait I tison tornant, sor coi li liien tornent, et ait en II tornans II petis tisons d’une paume de lonc, por torner le tornet;	 And between each pin, place the turning pin as in the loom, and have two small pins of a span length to turn the lathe.
et puis lie lou lien qui est parmi les asseles au tornet devers le chief, et l’autre liien devers les piez a l’autre tornet, et chescuns des ministres torne son tornet a tout le liien, et li maistres mette l’espinee igal si com nos avons dit.	 And then tighten the ligament that is between the shoulder blades towards the head, and the other ligament towards the feet at the opposite shoulder blade; each of the ministers turns his shoulder blade to the entire ligament, and the masters align the spine equally as we have said.
Et quant elle est igalz, si met sus emplaustre desiccatif avec abun d’uef, et puis les estoupes, et puis l’estele d’une tablete de III dois de lonc, que porpreigne lou leu de la gilbositeit et la partie de l’espondile sainne, puis le lie d’un liien, si com nos avons dit, et use li malaides de norrissement subtil, tant qu’il soit sanez;	 And when it is aligned, place a desiccating plaster with egg white on top, then bandage (it), and then bind with a stick of wood three feet long that reaches the swelling and the healthy part of the spine, then tie with a ligament as we have said, and use warm and subtle poultices until it is healed.
et s’aucune chose vient en la fin de la santez, si covient aministrer medicines amollissans et asouajans, avec l’estele que nos avons dit ci devant;	 And if anything comes at the end of healing, it is necessary to administer softening and calming medicines, along with the stick that we have said before.
et aucune fois i aministre on une piece de plonc, et aucune fois vient li apparance en la derriere spondile dou dos, et cuide on que ce soit dislocations;	 And sometimes a piece of wood is administered, and sometimes the appearance appears at the rear spondyle of the back, and it is thought to be dislocation.
et c’est li os qui apert, por coi on n’i doit mie avoir presumption:	 This is the bone that opens, which is why one should not have any presumption about it:
par aventure feroit venir la mort.	 By chance may come death.
des dislocations de la hainche	Of the dislocations of the shoulder
Saiches que as jointures de la hainche et as jointures de l’espaule ne vient fuers que dislocacions soulement, ne n’i vient mie si com as autres jointures;	 Know that the joints of the neck and the shoulder come out only due to dislocation, they do not come loose like other joints.
et li jointure de la hainche est desaluee selonc IIII parties:	 The joint of the neck is dislocated according to four parts:
dedens et defuer ,et devant et derrier;	 inside and outside, front and back.
et plus dedens c’aillors, et poc desalue devant et derrier.	 More towards the inside, but less dislocated in front and back.
Et li conoissance de sa dislocations dedens si est que quant on joint la jambe malaide avec la sainne, si est plus longe, et apert plus li malaides genous que li sains, et ne puet li malaides doubler son genoil au feu;	 And the knowledge of its dislocation within is that when the sick leg is joined with the healthy one, it is longer and the sick person's knee opens wider than the healthy one, and the sick person cannot bend their knee in fire.
et est li leus qui est delez enflez d’aposteme chaut, por ceu que li chiés de la cuixe vient lai.	 And it is the joint that is dislocated swollen with abscess heat, because the hipbone comes there.
Et li signe de celui cui il vient au defuer, si est que cist accident sont contraire a ces devant.	And the sign of the one who experiences this happening, is that this event is contrary to those beforehand.
Et li signes de celui cui avient au devant, si est qu’il estent bien sa jambe selonc l’acomplissement;	 And the signs of the one who has it in front, they should be well aligned according to completion.
toutevoie, ne double mie le genoil sens dolor, et s’on le vuet faire aler, si ne puet avant, et retient son urine, et enfle li angre, et quant il vait, si passe sus le talon.	 However, the knee does not bend in pain, and if you want to make it walk, it cannot move forward, and it retains its urine, and when it walks, it passes over the heel.
Et li signes de celui cui il avient derrier, si est qu’il ne puet espandre son genoil, ne doubler, et est celle jambe plus torte de l’autre, et li angre est mollifié, et est li chiés de la cuixe au leu desoz les costes.	And the signs of the one whose leg is twisted behind, is that he cannot extend his knee nor bend it, and this leg is more twisted than the other, and the ankle is softened, and the head of the calf is below the ribs.
Li ramenemens de ceste semblance de dislocation si est que tu rewarde se li dislocations est anciainne, et elle demore selonc sa disposition, si n’i a nule cure;	 The remedies for this kind of dislocation are that you look if the dislocation is old and stays according to its position, without any treatment.
et n’i covient mie qu’il ait presumption.	 And it should not be assumed that there will be recovery in such cases.
Et en celi dont li dislocation est fresche, et c’est des IIII manieres de dislocation, si te haste que tu tornes la jointe, et l’esten dedens et defuer, et la muef a destre et senestre;	 And in the one whose dislocation is fresh, and it is of the four types of dislocations, hasten that you turn the joint, and push it inwards and outwards, and move it to the right and left;
par aventure si revenra, et n’a mestier d’autre cure.	 In case it returns, it does not need any further treatment.
Et s’il ne revient en ceste maniere, si covient que tu apareilles I ministre fort, et esten la jambe fort a II mains, ou a I liien que soit liiez sus lou genoil;	 And if it does not return in this manner, then you must apply strong pressure to the limb with both hands, or tie it with a rope above the knee.
et uns autres ministres estende sa main desus en teil maniere qu’il boute ses mains desoz ses asseles, puis l’estrigne d’un souef liien sus la cuixe;	 and another assistant stretches his hand over it in such a manner that he pushes his hands underneath the buttocks, then tightens a strong rope above the calf.
et uns autres tigne lou chief dou liien;	 and others hold the head with the rope.
et estendent amont et aval tuit a une fois, tant que li malaide soit levez de terre a une fois, et demoure pendans.	 They extend upwards and downwards all at once, until the patient is raised off the ground all at once, and remains suspended.
Ceste maniere d’estension si est commune as .iiij. semblances, et se li dislocation est revenue, si com nos avons dit, c’est bien.	This method of extension is common to the four similar cases, and if the dislocation returns, as we have said, it is good.
Se ceu non, si covient mettre cure a sa semblance.	 If that does not work, it is necessary to treat its appearance.
Quant li dislocations est au pardedens, si covient que tu sovines le malaide sus son costeit sain, puis met le liien sus la racine de la cuixe, et le leu qui est desoz l’angre, puis estent le liien en haut devers l’angre, et devers la forcele;	 When the dislocation is at the front, it is necessary that you make the patient lie on his healthy side, then tie a rope around the root of the thigh, and the limb which is below the joint, then pull the rope up towards the joint, and towards the shoulder.
puis preigne uns autres ministres ses bras, et embraice le gros leu de la cuixe malaide, et l’estende au defuer forment:	 Then take another attendant to hold its arms, and embrace the sick limb's thigh with both hands, and extend it outwards as far as possible.
si revenra a son leu maintenant;	 It will return to its place now.
et ceste maniere de dislocation est plus legiere des autres.	 And this method of dislocation is easier than the others.
Et se tu ne la pues serrer en ceste maniere que nos avons dit, si covient que tu lies les II piés dou malaide ensamble d’un fort liien souef sus les II talons, et sus les II genous, et soit li jambe malaide estendue II dois plus que li autres;	 And if you cannot hold it in this manner as we have said, then you must bind the two feet of the patient together tightly with a strong rope above the heels and knees, and the affected leg should be extended two folds more than the others.
puis soit pendus sus le chief d’un fust, et soit en sus de terre II bras de lonc;	 then hang it from a pole by the head, and suspend it two arms length above the ground.
puis comande a I ministre qu’il embraice le chief de la cuixe, et soit uns autres ministres pendans avec le malaide, qui embraice forment la cuixe, car li jointure revient maintenant hastanment.	 then instruct the minister to grasp the thigh, and let another minister be hanging with the patient, who will hold the thigh firmly, as the joint is returning now quickly.
Et quant li dislocations est au defuer, si gise li malaides, si com nos avons dit en celui qui a gilbositeit, et estraigne I liien sus la jambe malaide proprement, et sus le peis ausi;	 And when the dislocation is at an angle, let the patient lie down as we have said in the one with displacement, and tighten the rope around the affected leg properly, and around the body also.
puis met II tisons, I au chief et I autre as piez, puis fiche I tison entre les cuixes au malaide emmi la forme;	 Then insert the hot irons, one at the head and another at other places, then push the iron between the thighs towards the patient.
et ait plantei de drapelz moistes entor, qu’il ne blece lou malaide, puis estende chescuns ministre devers lui, et li mires mette igal a sa main la dislocation.	 And place damp cloths around it to prevent burning the patient, then extend each assistant away from him, and equalize his hand with the dislocation.
S’elle revient, c’est boin.	 If it returns (to its place), that is good.
Se ce non, met sus .ie. table, et le presse ensi com nos avons dit en la gilbositeit, et gise li malaides sus le sain costeit.	 If not, put it on a table and press it as we have said in the gilbositeit, and let the patient lie down on the healthy side.
Et quant li dislocations est devant, si covient estendre la jambe malaide hastanment, et selonc ce que j’ai dit;	 And when the dislocation is present, you must extend the patient's leg immediately, and as I have said.
et mette li mires sa paine d’estre sus l’angre malaide, puis presse a l’autre main, et l’estent aval devers lou genoil.	 And place the hand of the assistant on the upper part of the dislocation, then press with the other hand and push down towards the knee.
Et se li dislocations est au defuer, si ne covient pas estendre le malaide aval, ne lever sus la terre, ains covient qu’il soit ausi com se li hainche estoit desaluee au defuer, si com nos avons dit dou couchement sus les II hainches;	 And if the dislocation is at the back, you should not extend the patient downwards or lift him up, but rather it should be as when a bed is dislocated at the back, as we have said in the laying on two beds.
et soit sus sa faice, et li lien estendut si com nos avons dit ci devant, et doit om presser sus la jointure a la table;	 And place it [the affected limb] on a flat surface, and extend the ligament as we have said before, and press firmly on the joint with the table.
et sera a point quant li malaides estendra ses jambes, et elles seront igalz;	 And when the patient extends their legs, they will be even and equal.
adonques ajoste les cuixes, et met l’emplaustre, et l’estrain d’un bendeil, si que li hainche ne se mueve;	 Then adjust the thighs, put the splint on, and tie a bandage so that the limb does not move.
et se repose III jors ou IIII, puis le deslie, et met l’emplaustre sus;	 And rest for three or four days, then untie it [the bandage], and put the splint on again.
et se tu vois qu’elles soient igalz, si l’estrain, si com devant, et le laisse III jors;	 If you see that they [legs] are even, tie it [the bandage], as before, and leave it for three days.
puis le deslie, et lou fai aler belement, tant que li membres soit confortez.	 Then untie it [the bandage], and make him walk well, until the limb is comfortable.
de la dislocation dou genoil	The dislocation of the knee
Li genous est desaluez selonc III manieres:	 The thighbone (femur) is dislocated in three ways:
c’est a savoir, dedens et defuer, et derrier;	 That is to say, from within and outward, and backward.
et ne desalue point devant.	 And does not dislocate forward.
Et li signes si est que tu comande au malaide qu’il plie sa jambe a sa cuixe, et s’ele ne s’aert a sa cuixe, saiches qu’il est desaluez;	 And the signs are that you instruct the patient to bend his leg at the knee, and if it does not bend at the knee, then he is dislocated.
et li restauration de toutes si est que tu faices seoir le malaide droit, et estende sa jambe s’il puet, et li met ton dos sus sa faice, et met son piet sus tes piez;	 and the restoration of all is that you make the patient sit straight, extend his leg if he can, and place your back on his face, and place his foot on your feet.
puis pren son genoil a tes paumes, et retrai entre tes dois, puis plie les II costez dou genoil forment;	 Then take the thigh with both hands, pull it towards you between your arms, and bend the two sides of the thigh.
et uns autres ministres estende son piet, tant que li genous reviegne a son leu, et li signes est qu’il aert bien sa jambe a sa cuixe legierement;	 And another assistant extends his foot until the thighbone returns to its place, and the signs are that he slightly bends his leg at the knee.
et met l’emplastre sus, et fai aerdre la jambe a la cuixe, et les loie ensamble fort III jors ou IIII, puis le deslie;	 And apply the plaster on it, and immobilize the leg at the knee for three or four days, then release it.
et ne se travaille mie li malaides d’aler, tant que li membres soit confortez.	 And do not make the patient walk at all, until the limb is comfortable.
Et se li membres n’est a point, si aministre estendement fort, si com nos avons dit en la cure de la hainche, tant qu’il soit sanez	 And if the limb is not broken, administer strong stretching, as we have said in the treatment of dislocation, until it is healed.
de la dislocation dou talon	of the ankle dislocation
Li talons est aucune fois esmeus, et aucune fois desaluez plenement, et dedens et defuer.	The heels are sometimes bruised, and sometimes completely dislocated, both inside and out.
Et li signes si est que li cheville est enflee, et tent avant a la partie ou elle est desaluee:	 The signs are that the ankle is swollen, and it bends towards the part where it is dislocated:
li ramenemens si est legier, et le doit on estendre legierement a ses mains quant il est esmeus soulement.	 The reductions (dislocation corrections) are easy, and they should be extended lightly to the hands only when relaxed.
Et quant il est desaluez dou tot, si covient que tu faices seoir le malaide droit, et le tigne I ministres fors par la jambe, desus la cheville;	 And when it is dislocated completely, you must make the patient sit upright, and hold the limb (the affected arm) by the ankle above the ankle.
puis trai le piet a toi a ta main destre, et puis a la senestre II fois, puis l’estent en haut, et boute bellement lou piet en haut;	 Then pull the foot towards you with your right hand, then to the left hand twice, then lift it up and push the foot up forcefully.
et fai ce II fois, si com nos avons dit, em boutant et en traiant lou piet;	 And do it as we have said, by pushing and pulling on the limb;
s’elle revient, c’est bien;	 if it goes back into place, that's good;
se ce non, si rencomence l’ovraige, car il revient;	 but if not, repeat the procedure as it will return;
et s’il ne puet revenir ensi, si fai gesir lou malaide sor son dos sus terre, et fiche I passeil fermement en terre entre ses cuixes, et lie drapelz entor, qu’il ne blece lou malaide;	 and if it cannot return in this way, place the patient on his back on the ground, drive the spit firmly into the ground between his knees, and tie cloths around so as not to prick the patient.
puis teigne li ministres la cuixe, et uns autres ministres estende lou piet a ses mains ou a I liien, k’il lie sus le col dou piet;	 then mark the minister the thigh, and another minister extends the limb to his hands or elbow, so that he holds it up at the neck of the limb.
puis estende chescuns ministres igalment, et li passelz soit adés entre les cuixes dou malaide por retenir le malaide quant on l’estent;	 then each minister extends himself evenly, and the passerby remains close between the thighs of the patient to hold him down when stretching.
puis mette li mires igal la dislocation a ses mains, et uns autres ministres teigne la jambe sainne au desoz, et li dislocation revenra hastanment.	 Then place the patient's hand with the dislocation equal to yours, and another servant hold the healthy leg below it, and the dislocation will quickly return.
Et quant elle iert a point, si met l’emplastre et estoupes sus, et l’estrain forment, et lie lou piet a la jambe, et warde les ners qui sont sus la cheville derrier, que li liiens ne soit trop estrois;	 And when it is positioned, apply the plaster and the cloth, mold it firmly, tie it to the leg, and guard the nerves which are behind the ankle, so that the bindings are not too tight.
puis le laisse II jors ou III, et se li liiens amolist, si l’estrain;	 Then leave it for two or three days, and if the bindings loosen, tighten them again.
puis le deslie au tier jor ou au quart, et deffent a aler lou malaide par IIII jors;	 Then untie it on the third day or the fourth, and let the patient walk for four days.
et s’il va devant cel termine, ce n’est mie seurtez qu’il ne desalue encor.	 And if he goes before that time, it is not certain that it will not dislocate again.
Et se apostemes chaus i vient, si covient que tu l’apaises, si com nos avons dit autre part, tant qu’il soit sanez.	If an abscess opens, you must calm it, as we have said elsewhere, until it heals.
des dois	of the two
Quant li doi sont desaluez, si les covient bellement estendre sens travail, et c’est legiere chose.	When the arms are dislocated, they must be stretched out gently without effort, and it is an easy thing to do.
Et se li dislocations est en aucun nout dou dos dou piet, si covient que tu faices seoir le malaide sus I leu plain ou sus .ie. table tot droit, et met ton piet sus ce qui apert de ces jointures, puis presse a ton piet forment, tant qu’il reviegne;	 And if the dislocation is in any notch of the back or neck, you must make the patient sit on a flat surface or table straight, and put your foot on what opens the joints, then press firmly on your foot until it returns.
et quant il est igalz, et il n’i apert nient, si met desoz la plante dou piet une table a II chiés, puis l’estrain forment, et le laisse III jors, puis le deslie;	 And when it is even and there is no opening, place a table under the foot of the shoulder, then hold firmly and leave it for three days, then release.
et le fai reposer, tant qu’il soit sanez.	 let it rest until it heals.
de plaie et de dislocation ensamble	of wound and dislocation together
Quant plaie vient avec la dislocation, et on la vuet restorer, maintes fois avient que li malaides muert:	 When a wound comes with dislocation and it is to be restored, many times the patient dies.
si ne soies mie presumptuous en la cure, se tu n’es saiges en l’art et tu ne l’as useit longement, et se tu n’es pitous et misericors et tardis, ne mie hardis;	 Do not be hasty in the cure, if you are not wise in the art and have not practiced it for a long time, and if you are not compassionate and merciful, do not be bold.
et use au comencement de choses apaisans aposteme chaut, et laisse le malaide en la main Deu, se tu n’i vois esperance de santeit;	 And at the beginning, apply soothing ointment on the abscess and leave the patient in God's hands, if you see no hope of healing.
et quant tu i vois esperance, si ramoinne maintenant le membre au leu, ainsois que li apostemes chaus i viegne;	 And when there is hope, reset the limb to its place, so that the abscess heals.
et quant li membres est a leu, si aministre choses apaisans aposteme chaut, et cure la plaie, si com il covient, d’oignemens desiccatis;	 And when the limb is in place, apply soothing ointment on the abscess and treat the wound as required, using dry cauterizing ointments.
et se avec la dislocation a brisure, et os menus desevrez, si les oste, et fai ce que nos avons dit en maladies simples;	 And if there is a dislocation with fracture and broken bones, set them and do as we have said in simple illnesses.
et te garde d’entrer en voie de paour, selonc ce que j’ai dit, car ce te vaut mues selonc ton Creator, et por la saveteit de t’arme et de ton cors.	 And beware of entering into fear, as I have said, for it will harm you according to your Creator, and by the wisdom of your weapon and body.
